<s> Ever your affectionate </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] SHREWSBURY, _Thursday, Aug </s>
<s> 12th, 1858._ A wonderful audience last night at Wolverhampton </s>
<s> If such a thing can be, they were even quicker and more intelligent than the audience I had in Edinburgh </s>
<s> They were so wonderfully good and were so much on the alert this morning by nine o'clock for another reading, that we are going back there at about our Bradford time </s>
<s> I never saw such people </s>
<s> And the local agent would take no money, and charge no expenses of his own </s>
<s> This place looks what Plorn would call "ortily" dull </s>
<s> Local agent predicts, however, "great satisfaction to Mr Dickens, and excellent attendance" </s>
<s> I have just been to look at the hall, where everything was wrong, and where I have left Arthur making a platform for me out of dining-tables </s>
<s> If he comes back in time, I am not quite sure but that he is himself going to write to Gad's Hill </s>
<s> We talk of coming up from Chester _in the night to-morrow, after the reading_; and of showing our precious selves at an apparently impossibly early hour in the Gad's Hill breakfast-room on Saturday morning </s>
<s> I have not felt the fatigue to any extent worth mentioning; though I get, every night, into the most violent heats </s>
<s> We are going to dine at three o'clock (it wants a quarter now) and have not been here two hours, so I have seen nothing of Clement </s>
<s> Tell Georgy with my love, that I read in the same room in which we acted, but at the end opposite to that where our stage was </s>
<s> We are not at the inn where the amateur company put up, but at The Lion, where the fair Miss Mitchell was lodged alone </s>
<s> We have the strangest little rooms (sitting-room and two bed-rooms all together), the ceilings of which I can touch with my hand </s>
<s> The windows bulge out over the street, as if they were little stern-windows in a ship </s>
<s> And a door opens out of the sitting-room on to a little open gallery with plants in it, where one leans over a queer old rail, and looks all downhill and slant-wise at the crookedest black and yellow old houses, all manner of shapes except straight shapes </s>
<s> To get into this room we come through a china closet; and the man in laying the cloth has actually knocked down, in that repository, two geraniums and Napoleon Bonaparte </s>
<s> I think that's all I have to say, except that at the Wolverhampton theatre they played "Oliver Twist" last night (Mr Toole the Artful Dodger), "in consequence of the illustrious author honouring the town with his presence" </s>
<s> We heard that the device succeeded very well, and that they got a good many people </s>
<s> John's spirits have been equable and good since we rejoined him </s>
<s> Berry has always got something the matter with his digestion--seems to me the male gender of Maria Jolly, and ought to take nothing but Revalenta Arabica </s>
<s> Bottled ale is not to be got in these parts, and Arthur is thrown upon draught </s>
<s> My dearest love to Georgy and to Katey, also to Marguerite </s>
<s> Also to all the boys and the noble Plorn </s>
<s> Ever your affectionate Father </s>

<s> [Sidenote: The same.] ADELPHI HOTEL, LIVERPOOL, _Friday Night, Aug </s>
<s> 20th, 1858._ I received your welcome and interesting letter to-day, and I write you a very hurried and bad reply; but it is _after the reading_, and you will take the will for the deed under these trying circumstances, I know </s>
<s> We have had a tremendous night; the largest house I have ever had since I first began--two thousand three hundred people </s>
<s> To-morrow afternoon, at three, I read again </s>
<s> My cold has been oppressive, and is not yet gone </s>
<s> I have been very hard to sleep too, and last night I was all but sleepless </s>
<s> This morning I was very dull and seedy; but I got a good walk, and picked up again </s>
<s> It has been blowing all day, and I fear we shall have a sick passage over to Dublin to-morrow night </s>
<s> Tell Mamie (with my dear love to her and Katie) that I will write to her from Dublin--probably on Sunday </s>
<s> Tell her too that the stories she told me in her letter were not only capital stories in themselves, but _excellently told_ too </s>
<s> What Arthur's state has been to-night--he, John, Berry, and Boylett, all taking money and going mad together--you _cannot_ imagine </s>
<s> They turned away hundreds, sold all the books, rolled on the ground of my room knee-deep in checks, and made a perfect pantomime of the whole thing </s>
<s> He has kept quite well, I am happy to say, and sends a hundred loves </s>
<s> In great haste and fatigue </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] MORRISON'S HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Monday, Aug </s>
<s> 23rd, 1858._ We had a nasty crossing here </s>
<s> We left Holyhead at one in the morning, and got here at six </s>
<s> Arthur was incessantly sick the whole way </s>
<s> I was not sick at all, but was in as healthy a condition otherwise as humanity need be </s>
<s> We are in a beautiful hotel </s>
<s> Our sitting-room is exactly like the drawing-room at the Peschiere in all its dimensions </s>
<s> I never saw two rooms so exactly resembling one another in their proportions </s>
<s> Our bedrooms too are excellent, and there are baths and all sorts of comforts </s>
<s> The Lord Lieutenant is away, and the place looks to me as if its professional life were away too </s>
<s> Nevertheless, there are numbers of people in the streets </s>
<s> Somehow, I hardly seem to think we are going to do enormously here; but I have scarcely any reason for supposing so (except that a good many houses are shut up); and I _know_ nothing about it, for Arthur is now gone to the agent and to the room </s>
<s> The men came by boat direct from Liverpool </s>
<s> They had a rough passage, were all ill, and did not get here till noon yesterday </s>
<s> Donnybrook Fair, or what remains of it, is going on, within two or three miles of Dublin </s>
<s> They went out there yesterday in a jaunting-car, and John described it to us at dinner-time (with his eyebrows lifted up, and his legs well asunder), as "Johnny Brooks's Fair;" at which Arthur, who was drinking bitter ale, nearly laughed himself to death </s>
<s> Berry is always unfortunate, and when I asked what had happened to Berry on board the steamboat, it appeared that "an Irish gentleman which was drunk, and fancied himself the captain, wanted to knock Berry down" </s>
<s> I am surprised by finding this place very much larger than I had supposed it to be </s>
<s> Its bye-parts are bad enough, but cleaner, too, than I had supposed them to be, and certainly very much cleaner than the old town of Edinburgh </s>
<s> The man who drove our jaunting-car yesterday hadn't a piece in his coat as big as a penny roll, and had had his hat on (apparently without brushing it) ever since he was grown up </s>
<s> But he was remarkably intelligent and agreeable, with something to say about everything </s>
<s> For instance, when I asked him what a certain building was, he didn't say "courts of law" and nothing else, but: "Av you plase, sir, it's the foor coorts o' looyers, where Misther O'Connell stood his trial wunst, ye'll remimber, sir, afore I tell ye of it" </s>
<s> When we got into the Phoenix Park, he looked round him as if it were his own, and said: "THAT'S a park, sir, av yer plase" </s>
<s> I complimented it, and he said: "Gintlemen tills me as they'r bin, sir, over Europe, and never see a park aqualling ov it </s>
<s> 'Tis eight mile roond, sir, ten mile and a half long, and in the month of May the hawthorn trees are as beautiful as brides with their white jewels on </s>
<s> Yonder's the vice-regal lodge, sir; in them two corners lives the two sicretirries, wishing I was them, sir </s>
<s> There's air here, sir, av yer plase </s>
<s> There's scenery here, sir </s>
<s> There's mountains--thim, sir </s>
<s> Yer coonsider it a park, sir </s>
<s> It is that, sir" </s>
<s> You should have heard John in my bedroom this morning endeavouring to imitate a bath-man, who had resented his interference, and had said as to the shower-bath: "Yer'll not be touching _that_, young man </s>
<s> Divil a touch yer'll touch o' that insthrument, young man" </s>
<s> It was more ridiculously unlike the reality than I can express to you, yet he was so delighted with his powers that he went off in the absurdest little gingerbeery giggle, backing into my portmanteau all the time </s>
<s> My dear love to Katie and to Georgy, also to the noble Plorn and all the boys </s>
<s> I shall write to Katie next, and then to Aunty </s>
<s> My cold, I am happy to report, is very much better </s>
<s> I lay in the wet all night on deck, on board the boat, but am not as yet any the worse for it </s>

<s> I will keep the envelope open until he comes in </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] MORRISON'S HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Wednesday, Aug </s>
<s> 25th, 1858._ I begin my letter to you to-day, though I don't know when I may send it off </s>
<s> We had a very good house last night, after all, that is to say, a great rush of shillings and good half-crowns, though the stalls were comparatively few </s>
<s> For "Little Dombey," this morning, we have an immense stall let--already more than two hundred--and people are now fighting in the agent's shop to take more </s>
<s> Through some mistake of our printer's, the evening reading for this present Wednesday was dropped, in a great part of the announcements, and the agent opened no plan for it </s>
<s> I have therefore resolved not to have it at all </s>
<s> Arthur Smith has waylaid me in all manner of ways, but I remain obdurate </s>
<s> I am frightfully tired, and really relieved by the prospect of an evening--overjoyed </s>
<s> They were a highly excitable audience last night, but they certainly did not comprehend--internally and intellectually comprehend--"The Chimes" as a London audience do </s>
<s> I am quite sure of it </s>
<s> I very much doubt the Irish capacity of receiving the pathetic; but of their quickness as to the humorous there can be no doubt </s>
<s> I shall see how they go along with Little Paul, in his death, presently </s>
<s> While I was at breakfast this morning, a general officer was announced with great state--having a staff at the door--and came in, booted and plumed, and covered with Crimean decorations </s>
<s> It was Cunninghame, whom we knew in Genoa--then a captain </s>
<s> He was very hearty indeed, and came to ask me to dinner </s>
<s> Of course I couldn't go </s>
<s> Olliffe has a brother at Cork, who has just now (noon) written to me, proposing dinners and excursions in that neighbourhood which would fill about a week; I being there a day and a half, and reading three times </s>
<s> The work will be very severe here, and I begin to feel depressed by it </s>
<s> (By "here," I mean Ireland generally, please to observe.) We meant, as I said in a letter to Katie, to go to Queenstown yesterday and bask on the seashore </s>
<s> But there is always so much to do that we couldn't manage it after all </s>
<s> We expect a tremendous house to-morrow night as well as to-day; and Arthur is at the present instant up to his eyes in business (and seats), and, between his regret at losing to-night, and his desire to make the room hold twice as many as it _will_ hold, is half distracted </s>
<s> I have become a wonderful Irishman--must play an Irish part some day--and his only relaxation is when I enact "John and the Boots," which I consequently do enact all day long </s>
<s> The papers are full of remarks upon my white tie, and describe it as being of enormous size, which is a wonderful delusion, because, as you very well know, it is a small tie </s>
<s> Generally, I am happy to report, the Emerald press is in favour of my appearance, and likes my eyes </s>
<s> But one gentleman comes out with a letter at Cork, wherein he says that although only forty-six I look like an old man </s>
<s> _He_ is a rum customer, I think </s>
<s> The Rutherfords are living here, and wanted me to dine with them, which, I needn't say, could not be done; all manner of people have called, but I have seen only two </s>
<s> John has given it up altogether as to rivalry with the Boots, and did not come into my room this morning at all </s>
<s> Boots appeared triumphant and alone </s>
<s> He was waiting for me at the hotel-door last night </s>
<s> "Whaa't sart of a hoose, sur" </s>
<s> he asked me </s>
<s> "Capital" </s>
<s> "The Lard be praised fur the 'onor o' Dooblin" </s>
<s> Arthur buys bad apples in the streets and brings them home and doesn't eat them, and then I am obliged to put them in the balcony because they make the room smell faint </s>
<s> Also he meets countrymen with honeycomb on their heads, and leads them (by the buttonhole when they have one) to this gorgeous establishment and requests the bar to buy honeycomb for his breakfast; then it stands upon the sideboard uncovered and the flies fall into it </s>
<s> He buys owls, too, and castles, and other horrible objects, made in bog-oak (that material which is not appreciated at Gad's Hill); and he is perpetually snipping pieces out of newspapers and sending them all over the world </s>
<s> While I am reading he conducts the correspondence, and his great delight is to show me seventeen or eighteen letters when I come, exhausted, into the retiring-place </s>
<s> Berry has not got into any particular trouble for forty-eight hours, except that he is all over boils </s>
<s> I have prescribed the yeast, but ineffectually </s>
<s> It is indeed a sight to see him and John sitting in pay-boxes, and surveying Ireland out of pigeon-holes </s>
<s> _Same Evening before Bed-time._ Everybody was at "Little Dombey" to-day, and although I had some little difficulty to work them up in consequence of the excessive crowding of the place, and the difficulty of shaking the people into their seats, the effect was unmistakable and profound </s>
<s> The crying was universal, and they were extraordinarily affected </s>
<s> There is no doubt we could stay here a week with that one reading, and fill the place every night </s>
<s> Hundreds of people have been there to-night, under the impression that it would come off again </s>
<s> It was a most decided and complete success </s>
<s> Arthur has been imploring me to stop here on the Friday after Limerick, and read "Little Dombey" again </s>
<s> But I have positively said "No" </s>
<s> The work is too hard </s>
<s> It is not like doing it in one easy room, and always the same room </s>
<s> With a different place every night, and a different audience with its own peculiarity every night, it is a tremendous strain </s>
<s> I was sick of it to-day before I began, then got myself into wonderful train </s>
<s> Here follows a dialogue (but it requires imitation), which I had yesterday morning with a little boy of the house--landlord's son, I suppose--about Plorn's age </s>
<s> I am sitting on the sofa writing, and find him sitting beside me </s>

<s> Ye'r right </s>

<s> There are two stupid old louts at the room, to show people into their places, whom John calls "them two old Paddies," and of whom he says, that he "never see nothing like them (snigger) hold idiots" (snigger) </s>

<s> But when we shall have turned this week, once knocked off Belfast, I shall see land, and shall (like poor Timber in the days of old) "keep up a good heart" </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BELFAST, _Saturday, Aug </s>
<s> 28th, 1858._ When I went down to the Rotunda at Dublin on Thursday night, I said to Arthur, who came rushing at me: "You needn't tell me </s>
<s> I know all about it" </s>
<s> The moment I had come out of the door of the hotel (a mile off), I had come against the stream of people turned away </s>
<s> I had struggled against it to the room </s>
<s> There, the crowd in all the lobbies and passages was so great, that I had a difficulty in getting in </s>
<s> They had broken all the glass in the pay-boxes </s>
<s> They had offered frantic prices for stalls </s>
<s> Eleven bank-notes were thrust into that pay-box (Arthur saw them) at one time, for eleven stalls </s>
<s> Our men were flattened against walls, and squeezed against beams </s>
<s> Ladies stood all night with their chins against my platform </s>
<s> Other ladies sat all night upon my steps </s>
<s> You never saw such a sight </s>
<s> And the reading went tremendously </s>
<s> It is much to be regretted that we troubled ourselves to go anywhere else in Ireland </s>
<s> We turned away people enough to make immense houses for a week </s>
<s> We arrived here yesterday at two </s>
<s> The room will not hold more than from eighty to ninety pounds </s>
<s> The same scene was repeated with the additional feature, that the people are much rougher here than in Dublin, and that there was a very great uproar at the opening of the doors, which, the police in attendance being quite inefficient and only looking on, it was impossible to check </s>
<s> Arthur was in the deepest misery because shillings got into stalls, and half-crowns got into shillings, and stalls got nowhere, and there was immense confusion </s>
<s> It ceased, however, the moment I showed myself; and all went most brilliantly, in spite of a great piece of the cornice of the ceiling falling with a great crash within four or five inches of the head of a young lady on my platform (I was obliged to have people there), and in spite of my gas suddenly going out at the time of the game of forfeits at Scrooge's nephew's, through some Belfastian gentleman accidentally treading on the flexible pipe, and needing to be relighted </s>
<s> We shall not get to Cork before mid-day on Monday; it being difficult to get from here on a Sunday </s>
<s> We hope to be able to start away to-morrow morning to see the Giant's Causeway (some sixteen miles off), and in that case we shall sleep at Dublin to-morrow night, leaving here by the train at half-past three in the afternoon </s>
<s> Dublin, you must understand, is on the way to Cork </s>
<s> This is a fine place, surrounded by lofty hills </s>
<s> The streets are very wide, and the place is very prosperous </s>
<s> The whole ride from Dublin here is through a very picturesque and various country; and the amazing thing is, that it is all particularly neat and orderly, and that the houses (outside at all events) are all brightly whitewashed and remarkably clean </s>
<s> I want to climb one of the neighbouring hills before this morning's "Dombey" </s>
<s> I am now waiting for Arthur, who has gone to the bank to remit his last accumulation of treasure to London </s>
<s> Our men are rather indignant with the Irish crowds, because in the struggle they don't sell books, and because, in the pressure, they can't force a way into the room afterwards to sell them </s>
<s> They are deeply interested in the success, however, and are as zealous and ardent as possible </s>

<s> Ever, my dearest Mamie, Your most affectionate Father </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] MORRISON'S HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Sunday Night, Aug </s>
<s> 29th, 1858._ I am so delighted to find your letter here to-night (eleven o'clock), and so afraid that, in the wear and tear of this strange life, I have written to Gad's Hill in the wrong order, and have not written to you, as I should, that I resolve to write this before going to bed </s>
<s> You will find it a wretchedly stupid letter; but you may imagine, my dearest girl, that I am tired </s>

<s> Enormous </s>
<s> We turned away half the town </s>

<s> Every night, by-the-bye, since I have been in Ireland, the ladies have beguiled John out of the bouquet from my coat </s>
<s> And yesterday morning, as I had showered the leaves from my geranium in reading "Little Dombey," they mounted the platform, after I was gone, and picked them all up as keepsakes </s>
<s> I have never seen _men_ go in to cry so undisguisedly as they did at that reading yesterday afternoon </s>
<s> They made no attempt whatever to hide it, and certainly cried more than the women </s>
<s> As to the "Boots" at night, and "Mrs Gamp" too, it was just one roar with me and them; for they made me laugh so that sometimes I _could not_ compose my face to go on </s>
<s> You must not let the new idea of poor dear Landor efface the former image of the fine old man </s>

<s> It is the oddest carriage in the world, and you are always falling off </s>
<s> But it is gay and bright in the highest degree </s>

<s> What with a sixteen mile ride before we left Belfast, and a sea-beach walk, and a two o'clock dinner, and a seven hours' railway ride since, I am--as we say here--"a thrifle weary" </s>
<s> But I really am in wonderful force, considering the work </s>
<s> For which I am, as I ought to be, very thankful </s>
<s> Arthur was exceedingly unwell last night--could not cheer up at all </s>
<s> He was so very unwell that he left the hall(!) and became invisible after my five minutes' rest </s>

<s> The local agent was with me, and proposed that he (the wretched Arthur) should go to his office and balance the accounts then and there </s>
<s> He went, in the jacket and slippers, and came back in twenty minutes, _perfectly well_, in consequence of the admirable balance </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> Wilkie Collins.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, Sept </s>
<s> 6th, 1858._ MY DEAR WILKIE, First, let me report myself here for something less than eight-and-forty hours </s>
<s> I come last (and direct--a pretty hard journey) from Limerick </s>
<s> The success in Ireland has been immense </s>
<s> The work is very hard, sometimes overpowering; but I am none the worse for it, and arrived here quite fresh </s>
<s> Secondly, will you let me recommend the enclosed letter from Wigan, as the groundwork of a capital article, in your way, for H </s>
<s> W. </s>
<s> There is not the least objection to a plain reference to him, or to Phelps, to whom the same thing happened a year or two ago, near Islington, in the case of a clever and capital little daughter of his </s>
<s> I think it a capital opportunity for a discourse on gentility, with a glance at those other schools which advertise that the "sons of gentlemen only" are admitted, and a just recognition of the greater liberality of our public schools </s>
<s> There are tradesmen's sons at Eton, and Charles Kean was at Eton, and Macready (also an actor's son) was at Rugby </s>
<s> Some such title as "Scholastic Flunkeydom," or anything infinitely contemptuous, would help out the meaning </s>
<s> Surely such a schoolmaster must swallow all the silver forks that the pupils are expected to take when they come, and are not expected to take away with them when they go </s>
<s> And of course he could not exist, unless he had flunkey customers by the dozen </s>
<s> Secondly--no, this is thirdly now--about the Christmas number </s>
<s> I have arranged so to stop my readings, as to be available for it on _the 15th of November_, which will leave me time to write a good article, if I clear my way to one </s>
<s> Do you see your way to our making a Christmas number of this idea that I am going very briefly to hint </s>
<s> Some disappointed person, man or woman, prematurely disgusted with the world, for some reason or no reason (the person should be young, I think) retires to an old lonely house, or an old lonely mill, or anything you like, with one attendant, resolved to shut out the world, and hold no communion with it </s>
<s> The one attendant sees the absurdity of the idea, pretends to humour it, but really thus to slaughter it </s>
<s> Everything that happens, everybody that comes near, every breath of human interest that floats into the old place from the village, or the heath, or the four cross-roads near which it stands, and from which belated travellers stray into it, shows beyond mistake that you can't shut out the world; that you are in it, to be of it; that you get into a false position the moment you try to sever yourself from it; and that you must mingle with it, and make the best of it, and make the best of yourself into the bargain </s>
<s> If we could plot out a way of doing this together, I would not be afraid to take my part </s>
<s> If we could not, could we plot out a way of doing it, and taking in stories by other hands </s>
<s> If we could not do either (but I think we could), shall we fall back upon a round of stories again </s>
<s> That I would rather not do, if possible </s>
<s> Will you think about it </s>
<s> And can you come and dine at Tavistock House _on Monday, the 20th September, at half-past five_ </s>
<s> I purpose being at home there with the girls that day </s>
<s> Answer this, according to my printed list for the week </s>
<s> I am off to Huddersfield on Wednesday morning </s>
<s> I think I will now leave off; merely adding that I have got a splendid brogue (it really is exactly like the people), and that I think of coming out as the only legitimate successor of poor Power </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Wilkie, affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Mary Boyle.] STATION HOTEL, YORK, _Friday, Sept </s>
<s> 10th, 1858._ DEAREST MEERY, First let me tell you that all the magicians and spirits in your employ have fulfilled the instructions of their wondrous mistress to admiration </s>
<s> Flowers have fallen in my path wherever I have trod; and when they rained upon me at Cork I was more amazed than you ever saw me </s>
<s> Secondly, receive my hearty and loving thanks for that same </s>
<s> (Excuse a little Irish in the turn of that sentence, but I can't help it) </s>
<s> Thirdly, I have written direct to Mr Boddington, explaining that I am bound to be in Edinburgh on the day when he courteously proposes to do me honour </s>
<s> I really cannot tell you how truly and tenderly I feel your letter, and how gratified I am by its contents </s>
<s> Your truth and attachment are always so precious to me that I can_not_ get my heart out on my sleeve to show it you </s>
<s> It is like a child, and, at the sound of some familiar voices, "goes and hides" </s>
<s> You know what an affection I have for Mrs Watson, and how happy it made me to see her again--younger, much, than when I first knew her in Switzerland </s>
<s> God bless you always </s>
<s> Ever affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] ROYAL HOTEL, SCARBOROUGH, _Sunday, Sept </s>
<s> 11th, 1858._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, We had a very fine house indeed at York </s>
<s> All kinds of applications have been made for another reading there, and no doubt it would be exceedingly productive; but it cannot be done </s>
<s> At Harrogate yesterday; the queerest place, with the strangest people in it, leading the oddest lives of dancing, newspaper reading, and tables d'hôte </s>
<s> The piety of York obliging us to leave that place for this at six this morning, and there being no night train from Harrogate, we had to engage a special engine </s>
<s> We got to bed at one, and were up again before five; which, after yesterday's fatigues, leaves me a little worn out at this present </s>
<s> I have no accounts of this place as yet, nor have I received any letter here </s>
<s> But the post of this morning is not yet delivered, I believe </s>
<s> We have a charming room, overlooking the sea </s>
<s> Leech is here (living within a few doors), with the partner of his bosom, and his young family </s>
<s> I write at ten in the morning, having been here two hours; and you will readily suppose that I have not seen him </s>
<s> Of news, I have not the faintest breath </s>
<s> I seem to have been doing nothing all my life but riding in railway-carriages and reading </s>
<s> The railway of the morning brought us through Castle Howard, and under the woods of Easthorpe, and then just below Malton Abbey, where I went to poor Smithson's funeral </s>
<s> It was a most lovely morning, and, tired as I was, I couldn't sleep for looking out of window </s>
<s> Yesterday, at Harrogate, two circumstances occurred which gave Arthur great delight </s>
<s> Firstly, he chafed his legs sore with his black bag of silver </s>
<s> Secondly, the landlord asked him as a favour, "If he could oblige him with a little silver" </s>
<s> He obliged him directly with some forty pounds' worth; and I suspect the landlord to have repented of having approached the subject </s>
<s> After the reading last night we walked over the moor to the railway, three miles, leaving our men to follow with the luggage in a light cart </s>
<s> They passed us just short of the railway, and John was making the night hideous and terrifying the sleeping country, by _playing the horn_ in prodigiously horrible and unmusical blasts </s>
<s> My dearest love, of course, to the dear girls, and to the noble Plorn </s>
<s> Apropos of children, there was one gentleman at the "Little Dombey" yesterday morning, who exhibited, or rather concealed, the profoundest grief </s>
<s> After crying a good deal without hiding it, he covered his face with both his hands, and laid it down on the back of the seat before him, and really shook with emotion </s>
<s> He was not in mourning, but I supposed him to have lost some child in old time </s>
<s> There was a remarkably good fellow of thirty or so, too, who found something so very ludicrous in "Toots," that he _could not_ compose himself at all, but laughed until he sat wiping his eyes with his handkerchief </s>
<s> And whenever he felt "Toots" coming again he began to laugh and wipe his eyes afresh, and when he came he gave a kind of cry, as if it were too much for him </s>
<s> It was uncommonly droll, and made me laugh heartily </s>
<s> Ever, dear Georgy, your most affectionate </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] SCARBOROUGH ARMS, LEEDS, _Wednesday, Sept </s>
<s> 15th, 1858._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, I have added a pound to the cheque </s>
<s> I would recommend your seeing the poor railway man again and giving him ten shillings, and telling him to let you see him again in about a week </s>
<s> If he be then still unable to lift weights and handle heavy things, I would then give him another ten shillings, and so on </s>
<s> Since I wrote to Georgy from Scarborough, we have had, thank God, nothing but success </s>
<s> The Hull people (not generally considered excitable, even on their own showing) were so enthusiastic, that we were obliged to promise to go back there for two readings </s>
<s> I have positively resolved not to lengthen out the time of my tour, so we are now arranging to drop some small places, and substitute Hull again and York again </s>
<s> But you will perhaps have heard this in the main from Arthur </s>
<s> I know he wrote to you after the reading last night </s>
<s> This place I have always doubted, knowing that we should come here when it was recovering from the double excitement of the festival and the Queen </s>
<s> But there is a very large hall let indeed, and the prospect of to-night consequently looks bright </s>
<s> Arthur told you, I suppose, that he had his shirt-front and waistcoat torn off last night </s>
<s> He was perfectly enraptured in consequence </s>
<s> Our men got so knocked about that he gave them five shillings apiece on the spot </s>
<s> John passed several minutes upside down against a wall, with his head amongst the people's boots </s>
<s> He came out of the difficulty in an exceedingly touzled condition, and with his face much flushed </s>
<s> For all this, and their being packed as you may conceive they would be packed, they settled down the instant I went in, and never wavered in the closest attention for an instant </s>
<s> It was a very high room, and required a great effort </s>
<s> Oddly enough, I slept in this house three days last year with Wilkie </s>
<s> Arthur has the bedroom I occupied then, and I have one two doors from it, and Gordon has the one between </s>
<s> Not only is he still with us, but he _has_ talked of going on to Manchester, going on to London, and coming back with us to Darlington next Tuesday!! </s>
<s> These streets look like a great circus with the season just finished </s>
<s> All sorts of garish triumphal arches were put up for the Queen, and they have got smoky, and have been looked out of countenance by the sun, and are blistered and patchy, and half up and half down, and are hideous to behold </s>
<s> Spiritless men (evidently drunk for some time in the royal honour) are slowly removing them, and on the whole it is more like the clearing away of "The Frozen Deep" at Tavistock House than anything within your knowledge--with the exception that we are not in the least sorry, as we were then </s>
<s> Vague ideas are in Arthur's head that when we come back to Hull, we are to come here, and are to have the Town Hall (a beautiful building), and read to the million </s>
<s> I can't say yet </s>
<s> That depends </s>
<s> I remember that when I was here before (I came from Rockingham to make a speech), I thought them a dull and slow audience </s>
<s> I hope I may have been mistaken </s>
<s> I never saw better audiences than the Yorkshire audiences generally </s>
<s> I am so perpetually at work or asleep, that I have not a scrap of news </s>
<s> I saw the Leech family at Scarboro', both in my own house (that is to say, hotel) and in theirs </s>
<s> They were not at either reading </s>
<s> Scarboro' is gay and pretty, and I think Gordon had an idea that we were always at some such place </s>
<s> Kiss the darling Plorn for me, and give him my love; dear Katie too, giving her the same </s>
<s> I feel sorry that I cannot get down to Gad's Hill this next time, but I shall look forward to our being there with Georgy, after Scotland </s>
<s> Tell the servants that I remember them, and hope they will live with us many years </s>
<s> Ever, my dearest Mamie, Your most affectionate Father </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] KING'S HEAD, SHEFFIELD, _Friday, Sept </s>
<s> 17th, 1858._ I write you a few lines to Tavistock House, thinking you may not be sorry to find a note from me there on your arrival from Gad's Hill </s>
<s> Halifax was too small for us </s>
<s> I never saw such an audience though </s>
<s> They were really worth reading to for nothing, though I didn't do exactly that </s>
<s> It is as horrible a place as I ever saw, I think </s>

<s> It will be by no means easy to get into the place the numbers who have already paid </s>

<s> We must come back here towards the end of October, and are again altering the list and striking out small places </s>
<s> The trains are so strange and unintelligible in this part of the country that we were obliged to leave Halifax at eight this morning, and breakfast on the road--at Huddersfield again, where we had an hour's wait </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] STATION HOTEL, NEWCASTLE-ON-TYNE, _Sunday, Sept </s>
<s> 26th, 1858._ EXTRACT </s>
<s> The girls (as I have no doubt they have already told you for themselves) arrived here in good time yesterday, and in very fresh condition </s>
<s> They persisted in going to the room last night, though I had arranged for their remaining quiet </s>
<s> We have done a vast deal here </s>
<s> I suppose you know that we are going to Berwick, and that we mean to sleep there and go on to Edinburgh on Monday morning, arriving there before noon </s>
<s> If it be as fine to-morrow as it is to-day, the girls will see the coast piece of railway between Berwick and Edinburgh to great advantage </s>
<s> I was anxious that they should, because that kind of pleasure is really almost the only one they are likely to have in their present trip </s>
<s> Stanfield and Roberts are in Edinburgh, and the Scottish Royal Academy gave them a dinner on Wednesday, to which I was very pressingly invited </s>
<s> But, of course, my going was impossible </s>
<s> I read twice that day </s>
<s> Remembering what you do of Sunderland, you will be surprised that our profit there was very considerable </s>
<s> I read in a beautiful new theatre, and (I thought to myself) quite wonderfully </s>
<s> Such an audience I never beheld for rapidity and enthusiasm </s>
<s> The room in which we acted (converted into a theatre afterwards) was burnt to the ground a year or two ago </s>
<s> We found the hotel, so bad in our time, really good </s>
<s> I walked from Durham to Sunderland, and from Sunderland to Newcastle </s>
<s> Don't you think, as we shall be at home at eleven in the forenoon this day fortnight, that it will be best for you and Plornish to come to Tavistock House for that Sunday, and for us all to go down to Gad's Hill next day </s>
<s> My best love to the noble Plornish </s>
<s> If he is quite reconciled to the postponement of his trousers, I should like to behold his first appearance in them </s>
<s> But, if not, as he is such a good fellow, I think it would be a pity to disappoint and try him </s>
<s> And now, my dearest Georgy, I think I have said all I have to say before I go out for a little air </s>
<s> I had a very hard day yesterday, and am tired </s>
<s> Ever your most affectionate </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr John Forster.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, _Sunday, Oct </s>
<s> 10th, 1858._ MY DEAR FORSTER, As to the truth of the readings, I cannot tell you what the demonstrations of personal regard and respect are </s>
<s> How the densest and most uncomfortably-packed crowd will be hushed in an instant when I show my face </s>
<s> How the youth of colleges, and the old men of business in the town, seem equally unable to get near enough to me when they cheer me away at night </s>
<s> How common people and gentlefolks will stop me in the streets and say: "Mr Dickens, will you let me touch the hand that has filled my home with so many friends" </s>
<s> And if you saw the mothers, and fathers, and sisters, and brothers in mourning, who invariably come to "Little Dombey," and if you studied the wonderful expression of comfort and reliance with which they hang about me, as if I had been with them, all kindness and delicacy, at their own little death-bed, you would think it one of the strangest things in the world </s>
<s> As to the mere effect, of course I don't go on doing the thing so often without carefully observing myself and the people too in every little thing, and without (in consequence) greatly improving in it </s>
<s> At Aberdeen, we were crammed to the street twice in one day </s>
<s> At Perth (where I thought when I arrived there literally could be nobody to come), the nobility came posting in from thirty miles round, and the whole town came and filled an immense hall </s>
<s> As to the effect, if you had seen them after Lilian died, in "The Chimes," or when Scrooge woke and talked to the boy outside the window, I doubt if you would ever have forgotten it </s>
<s> And at the end of "Dombey" yesterday afternoon, in the cold light of day, they all got up, after a short pause, gentle and simple, and thundered and waved their hats with that astonishing heartiness and fondness for me, that for the first time in all my public career they took me completely off my legs, and I saw the whole eighteen hundred of them reel on one side as if a shock from without had shaken the hall </s>
<s> The dear girls have enjoyed themselves immensely, and their trip has been a great success </s>
<s> I hope I told you (but I forget whether I did or no) how splendidly Newcastle[4] came out </s>
<s> I am reminded of Newcastle at the moment because they joined me there </s>
<s> I am anxious to get to the end of my readings, and to be at home again, and able to sit down and think in my own study </s>
<s> But the fatigue, though sometimes very great indeed, hardly tells upon me at all </s>
<s> And although all our people, from Smith downwards, have given in, more or less, at times, I have never been in the least unequal to the work, though sometimes sufficiently disinclined for it </s>
<s> My kindest and best love to Mrs Forster </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] ROYAL HOTEL, DERBY, _Friday, Oct </s>
<s> 22nd, 1858._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, I am writing in a very poor condition; I have a bad cold all over me, pains in my back and limbs, and a very sensitive and uncomfortable throat </s>
<s> There was a great draught up some stone steps near me last night, and I daresay that caused it </s>
<s> The weather on my first two nights at Birmingham was so intolerably bad--it blew hard, and never left off raining for one single moment--that the houses were not what they otherwise would have been </s>
<s> On the last night the weather cleared, and we had a grand house </s>
<s> Last night at Nottingham was almost, if not quite, the most amazing we have had </s>
<s> It is not a very large place, and the room is by no means a very large one, but three hundred and twenty stalls were let, and all the other tickets were sold </s>
<s> Here we have two hundred and twenty stalls let for to-night, and the other tickets are gone in proportion </s>
<s> It is a pretty room, but not large </s>
<s> I have just been saying to Arthur that if there is not a large let for York, I would rather give it up, and get Monday at Gad's Hill </s>
<s> We have telegraphed to know </s>
<s> If the answer comes (as I suppose it will) before post time, I will tell you in a postscript what we decide to do </s>
<s> Coming to London in the night of to-morrow (Saturday), and having to see Mr Ouvry on Sunday, and having to start for York early on Monday, I fear I should not be able to get to Gad's Hill at all </s>
<s> You won't expect me till you see me </s>
<s> Arthur and I have considered Plornish's joke in all the immense number of aspects in which it presents itself to reflective minds </s>
<s> We have come to the conclusion that it is the best joke ever made </s>
<s> Give the dear boy my love, and the same to Georgy, and the same to Katey, and take the same yourself </s>
<s> Arthur (excessively low and inarticulate) mutters that he "unites" </s>
<s> [We knocked up Boylett, Berry, and John so frightfully yesterday, by tearing the room to pieces and altogether reversing it, as late as four o'clock, that we gave them a supper last night </s>
<s> They shine all over to-day, as if it had been entirely composed of grease.] Ever, my dearest Mamie, Your most affectionate Father </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WOLVERHAMPTON, _Wednesday, Nov </s>
<s> 3rd, 1858._ Little Leamington came out in the most amazing manner yesterday--turned away hundreds upon hundreds of people </s>
<s> They are represented as the dullest and worst of audiences </s>
<s> I found them very good indeed, even in the morning </s>
<s> There awaited me at the hotel, a letter from the Rev </s>
<s> Mr Young, Wentworth Watson's tutor, saying that Mrs Watson wished her boy to shake hands with me, and that he would bring him in the evening </s>
<s> I expected him at the hotel before the readings </s>
<s> But he did not come </s>
<s> He spoke to John about it in the room at night </s>
<s> The crowd and confusion, however, were very great, and I saw nothing of him </s>
<s> In his letter he said that Mrs Watson was at Paris on her way home, and would be at Brighton at the end of this week </s>
<s> I suppose I shall see her there at the end of next week </s>
<s> We find a let of two hundred stalls here, which is very large for this place </s>
<s> The evening being fine too, and blue being to be seen in the sky beyond the smoke, we expect to have a very full hall </s>
<s> Tell Mamey and Katey that if they had been with us on the railway to-day between Leamington and this place, they would have seen (though it is only an hour and ten minutes by the express) fires and smoke indeed </s>
<s> We came through a part of the Black Country that you know, and it looked at its blackest </s>
<s> All the furnaces seemed in full blast, and all the coal-pits to be working </s>
<s> It is market-day here, and the ironmasters are standing out in the street (where they always hold high change), making such an iron hum and buzz, that they confuse me horribly </s>
<s> In addition, there is a bellman announcing something--not the readings, I beg to say--and there is an excavation being made in the centre of the open place, for a statue, or a pump, or a lamp-post, or something or other, round which all the Wolverhampton boys are yelling and struggling </s>
<s> And here is Arthur, begging to have dinner at half-past three instead of four, because he foresees "a wiry evening" in store for him </s>
<s> Under which complication of distractions, to which a waitress with a tray at this moment adds herself, I sink, and leave off </s>
<s> My best love to the dear girls, and to the noble Plorn, and to you </s>
<s> Marguerite and Ellen Stone not forgotten </s>
<s> All yesterday and to-day I have been doing everything to the tune of: And the day is dark and dreary </s>
<s> Ever, dearest Georgy, Your most affectionate and faithful </s>
<s> P.S.--I hope the brazier is intolerably hot, and half stifles all the family </s>
<s> Then, and not otherwise, I shall think it in satisfactory work </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Rev </s>
<s> James White.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, W </s>
<s> C., _Friday, Nov </s>
<s> 5th, 1858._ MY DEAR WHITE, May I entreat you to thank Mr Carter very earnestly and kindly in my name, for his proffered hospitality; and, further, to explain to him that since my readings began, I have known them to be incompatible with all social enjoyments, and have neither set foot in a friend's house nor sat down to a friend's table in any one of all the many places I have been to, but have rigidly kept myself to my hotels </s>
<s> To this resolution I must hold until the last </s>
<s> There is not the least virtue in it </s>
<s> It is a matter of stern necessity, and I submit with the worst grace possible </s>
<s> Will you let me know, either at Southampton or Portsmouth, whether any of you, and how many of you, if any, are coming over, so that Arthur Smith may reserve good seats </s>
<s> Tell Lotty I hope she does not contemplate coming to the morning reading; I always hate it so myself </s>
<s> Mary and Katey are down at Gad's Hill with Georgy and Plornish, and they have Marguerite Power and Ellen Stone staying there </s>
<s> I am sorry to say that even my benevolence descries no prospect of their being able to come to my native place </s>
<s> On Saturday week, the 13th, my tour, please God, ends </s>
<s> My best love to Mrs White, and to Lotty, and to Clara </s>
<s> Ever, my dear White, affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Frank Stone, A.R.A.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, W.C., _Monday, Dec </s>
<s> 13th, 1858._ MY DEAR STONE, Many thanks for these discourses </s>
<s> They are very good, I think, as expressing what many men have felt and thought; otherwise not specially remarkable </s>
<s> They have one fatal mistake, which is a canker at the foot of their ever being widely useful </s>
<s> Half the misery and hypocrisy of the Christian world arises (as I take it) from a stubborn determination to refuse the New Testament as a sufficient guide in itself, and to force the Old Testament into alliance with it--whereof comes all manner of camel-swallowing and of gnat-straining </s>
<s> But so to resent this miserable error, or to (by any implication) depreciate the divine goodness and beauty of the New Testament, is to commit even a worse error </s>
<s> And to class Jesus Christ with Mahomet is simply audacity and folly </s>
<s> I might as well hoist myself on to a high platform, to inform my disciples that the lives of King George the Fourth and of King Alfred the Great belonged to one and the same category </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr B </s>
<s> W </s>
<s> Procter.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Sunday, Dec </s>
<s> 18th, 1858._ MY DEAR PROCTER, A thousand thanks for the little song </s>
<s> I am charmed with it, and shall be delighted to brighten "Household Words" with such a wise and genial light </s>
<s> I no more believe that your poetical faculty has gone by, than I believe that you have yourself passed to the better land </s>
<s> You and it will travel thither in company, rely upon it </s>
<s> So I still hope to hear more of the trade-songs, and to learn that the blacksmith has hammered out no end of iron into good fashion of verse, like a cunning workman, as I know him of old to be </s>
<s> Very faithfully yours, my dear Procter </s>

<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> During the winter, Charles Dickens was living at Tavistock House, removing to Gad's Hill for the summer early in June, and returning to London in November </s>
<s> At this time a change was made in his weekly journal </s>
<s> "Household Words" became absolutely his own--Mr Wills being his partner and editor, as before--and was "incorporated with 'All the Year Round,'" under which title it was known thenceforth </s>
<s> The office was still in Wellington Street, but in a different house </s>
<s> The first number with the new name appeared on the 30th April, and it contained the opening of "A Tale of Two Cities" </s>
<s> The first letter which follows shows that a proposal for a series of readings in America had already been made to him </s>
<s> It was carefully considered and abandoned for the time </s>
<s> But the proposal was constantly renewed, and the idea never wholly relinquished for many years before he actually decided on making so distant a "reading tour" </s>
<s> Mr Procter contributed to the early numbers of "All the Year Round" some very spirited "Songs of the Trades" </s>
<s> We give notes from Charles Dickens to the veteran poet, both in the last year, and in this year, expressing his strong approval of them </s>
<s> The letter and two notes to Mr (afterwards Sir Antonio) Panizzi, for which we are indebted to Mr Louis Fagan, one of Sir A </s>
<s> Panizzi's executors, show the warm sympathy and interest which he always felt for the cause of Italian liberty, and for the sufferings of the State prisoners who at this time took refuge in England </s>
<s> We give a little note to the dear friend and companion of Charles Dickens's daughters, "Lotty" White, because it is a pretty specimen of his writing, and because the young girl, who is playfully "commanded" to get well and strong, died early in July of this year </s>
<s> She was, at the time this note was written, first attacked with the illness which was fatal to all her sisters </s>
<s> Mamie and Kate Dickens went from Gad's Hill to Bonchurch to pay a last visit to their friend, and he writes to his eldest daughter there </s>
<s> Also we give notes of loving sympathy and condolence to the bereaved father and mother </s>
<s> In the course of this summer Charles Dickens was not well, and went for a week to his old favourite, Broadstairs--where Mr Wilkie Collins and his brother, Mr Charles Allston Collins, were staying--for sea-air and change, preparatory to another reading tour, in England only </s>
<s> His letter from Peterborough to Mr Frank Stone, giving him an account of a reading at Manchester (Mr Stone's native town), was one of the last ever addressed to that affectionate friend, who died very suddenly, to the great grief of Charles Dickens, in November </s>
<s> The letter to Mr Thomas Longman, which closes this year, was one of introduction to that gentleman of young Marcus Stone, then just beginning his career as an artist, and to whom the premature death of his father made it doubly desirable that he should have powerful helping hands </s>
<s> Charles Dickens refers, in a letter to Mrs Watson, to his portrait by Mr Frith, which was finished at the end of 1858 </s>
<s> It was painted for Mr Forster, and is now in the "Forster Collection" at South Kensington Museum </s>
<s> The Christmas number of this year, again written by several hands as well as his own, was "The Haunted House" </s>
<s> In November, his story of "A Tale of Two Cities" was finished in "All the Year Round," and in December was published, complete, with dedication to Lord John Russell </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Arthur Smith.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, W.C., _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 26th, 1859._ MY DEAR ARTHUR, Will you first read the enclosed letters, having previously welcomed, with all possible cordiality, the bearer, Mr Thomas C </s>
<s> Evans, from New York </s>
<s> You having read them, let me explain that Mr Fields is a highly respectable and influential man, one of the heads of the most classical and most respected publishing house in America; that Mr Richard Grant White is a man of high reputation; and that Felton is the Greek Professor in their Cambridge University, perhaps the most distinguished scholar in the States </s>
<s> The address to myself, referred to in one of the letters, being on its way, it is quite clear that I must give some decided and definite answer to the American proposal </s>
<s> Now, will you carefully discuss it with Mr Evans before I enter on it at all </s>
<s> Then, will you dine here with him on Sunday--which I will propose to him--and arrange to meet at half-past four for an hour's discussion </s>
<s> The points are these: First </s>
<s> I have a very grave question within myself whether I could go to America at all </s>
<s> Secondly </s>
<s> If I did go, I could not possibly go before the autumn </s>
<s> Thirdly </s>
<s> If I did go, how long must I stay </s>
<s> Fourthly </s>
<s> If the stay were a short one, could _you_ go </s>
<s> Fifthly </s>
<s> What is his project </s>
<s> What could I make </s>
<s> What occurs to you upon his proposal </s>
<s> I have told him that the business arrangements of the readings have been from the first so entirely in your hands, that I enter upon nothing connected with them without previous reference to you </s>
<s> Ever faithfully </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 1st, 1859._ MY DEAR CERJAT, I received your always welcome annual with even more interest than usual this year, being (in common with my two girls and their aunt) much excited and pleased by your account of your daughter's engagement </s>
<s> Apart from the high sense I have of the affectionate confidence with which you tell me what lies so tenderly on your own heart, I have followed the little history with a lively sympathy and regard for her </s>
<s> I hope, with you, that it is full of promise, and that you will all be happy in it </s>
<s> The separation, even in the present condition of travel (and no man can say how much the discovery of a day may advance it), is nothing </s>
<s> And so God bless her and all of you, and may the rosy summer bring her all the fulness of joy that we all wish her </s>
<s> To pass from the altar to Townshend (which is a long way), let me report him severely treated by Bully, who rules him with a paw of iron; and complaining, moreover, of indigestion </s>
<s> He drives here every Sunday, but at all other times is mostly shut up in his beautiful house, where I occasionally go and dine with him _tête- -tête_, and where we always talk of you and drink to you </s>
<s> That is a rule with us from which we never depart </s>
<s> He is "seeing a volume of poems through the press;" rather an expensive amusement </s>
<s> He has not been out at night (except to this house) save last Friday, when he went to hear me read "The Poor Traveller," "Mrs Gamp," and "The Trial" from "Pickwick" </s>
<s> He came into my room at St </s>
<s> Martin's Hall, and I fortified him with weak brandy-and-water </s>
<s> You will be glad to hear that the said readings are a greater _furore_ than they ever have been, and that every night on which they now take place--once a week--hundreds go away, unable to get in, though the hall holds thirteen hundred people </s>
<s> I dine with ---- to-day, by-the-bye, along with his agent; concerning whom I observe him to be always divided between an unbounded confidence and a little latent suspicion </s>
<s> He always tells me that he is a gem of the first water; oh yes, the best of business men </s>
<s> and then says that he did not quite like his conduct respecting that farm-tenant and those hay-ricks </s>
<s> There is a general impression here, among the best-informed, that war in Italy, to begin with, is inevitable, and will break out before April </s>
<s> I know a gentleman at Genoa (Swiss by birth), deeply in with the authorities at Turin, who is already sending children home </s>
<s> In England we are quiet enough </s>
<s> There is a world of talk, as you know, about Reform bills; but I don't believe there is any general strong feeling on the subject </s>
<s> According to my perceptions, it is undeniable that the public has fallen into a state of indifference about public affairs, mainly referable, as I think, to the people who administer them--and there I mean the people of all parties--which is a very bad sign of the times </s>
<s> The general mind seems weary of debates and honourable members, and to have taken _laissez-aller_ for its motto </s>
<s> My affairs domestic (which I know are not without their interest for you) flow peacefully </s>
<s> My eldest daughter is a capital housekeeper, heads the table gracefully, delegates certain appropriate duties to her sister and her aunt, and they are all three devotedly attached </s>
<s> Charley, my eldest boy, remains in Barings' house </s>
<s> Your present correspondent is more popular than he ever has been </s>
<s> I rather think that the readings in the country have opened up a new public who were outside before; but however that may be, his books have a wider range than they ever had, and his public welcomes are prodigious </s>
<s> Said correspondent is at present overwhelmed with proposals to go and read in America </s>
<s> Will never go, unless a small fortune be first paid down in money on this side of the Atlantic </s>
<s> Stated the figure of such payment, between ourselves, only yesterday </s>
<s> Expects to hear no more of it, and assuredly will never go for less </s>
<s> You don't say, my dear Cerjat, when you are coming to England </s>
<s> Somehow I feel that this marriage ought to bring you over, though I don't know why </s>
<s> You shall have a bed here and a bed at Gad's Hill, and we will go and see strange sights together </s>
<s> When I was in Ireland, I ordered the brightest jaunting-car that ever was seen </s>
<s> It has just this minute arrived per steamer from Belfast </s>
<s> Say you are coming, and you shall be the first man turned over by it; somebody must be (for my daughter Mary drives anything that can be harnessed, and I know of no English horse that would understand a jaunting-car coming down a Kentish hill), and you shall be that somebody if you will </s>
<s> They turned the basket-phaeton over, last summer, in a bye-road--Mary and the other two--and had to get it up again; which they did, and came home as if nothing had happened </s>
<s> They send their loves to Mrs Cerjat, and to you, and to all, and particularly to the dear _fiancée_ </s>
<s> So do I, with all my heart, and am ever your attached and affectionate friend </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Antonio Panizzi.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, _Monday Night, March 14th, 1859._ MY DEAR PANIZZI, If you should feel no delicacy in mentioning, or should see no objection to mentioning, to Signor Poerio, or any of the wronged Neapolitan gentlemen to whom it is your happiness and honour to be a friend on their arrival in this country, an idea that has occurred to me, I should regard it as a great kindness in you if you would be my exponent </s>
<s> I think you will have no difficulty in believing that I would not, on any consideration, obtrude my name or projects upon any one of those noble souls, if there were any reason of the slightest kind against it </s>
<s> And if you see any such reason, I pray you instantly to banish my letter from your thoughts </s>
<s> It seems to me probable that some narrative of their ten years' suffering will, somehow or other, sooner or later, be by some of them laid before the English people </s>
<s> The just interest and indignation alive here, will (I suppose) elicit it </s>
<s> False narratives and garbled stories will, in any case, of a certainty get about </s>
<s> If the true history of the matter is to be told, I have that sympathy with them and respect for them which would, all other considerations apart, render it unspeakably gratifying to me to be the means of its diffusion </s>
<s> What I desire to lay before them is simply this </s>
<s> If for my new successor to "Household Words" a narrative of their ten years' trial could be written, I would take any conceivable pains to have it rendered into English, and presented in the sincerest and best way to a very large and comprehensive audience </s>
<s> It should be published exactly as you might think best for them, and remunerated in any way that you might think generous and right </s>
<s> They want no mouthpiece and no introducer, but perhaps they might have no objection to be associated with an English writer, who is possibly not unknown to them by some general reputation, and who certainly would be animated by a strong public and private respect for their honour, spirit, and unmerited misfortunes </s>
<s> This is the whole matter; assuming that such a thing is to be done, I long for the privilege of helping to do it </s>
<s> These gentlemen might consider it an independent means of making money, and I should be delighted to pay the money </s>
<s> In my absence from town, my friend and sub-editor, Mr Wills (to whom I had expressed my feeling on the subject), has seen, I think, three of the gentlemen together </s>
<s> But as I hear, returning home to-night, that they are in your good hands, and as nobody can be a better judge than you of anything that concerns them, I at once decide to write to you and to take no other step whatever </s>
<s> Forgive me for the trouble I have occasioned you in the reading of this letter, and never think of it again if you think that by pursuing it you would cause them an instant's uneasiness </s>
<s> Believe me, very faithfully yours </s>

<s> In this wonderful epistle he says: "Dear papa, I write to tell you that I have given up all thoughts of being a doctor </s>

<s> Considering the consequences of executing the little commission by the next steamer, I perceived that the first consequence of the fifteen pounds would be that he would be robbed of it--of the horse, that it would throw him--and of the rifle, that it would blow his head off; which probabilities I took the liberty of mentioning, as being against the scheme </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] GAD'S HILL, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, June 11th, 1859._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, On Saturday night I found, very much to my surprise and pleasure, the photograph on my table at Tavistock House </s>

<s> One of the balustrades of the destroyed old Rochester bridge has been (very nicely) presented to me by the contractor for the works, and has been duly stonemasoned and set up on the lawn behind the house </s>
<s> I have ordered a sun-dial for the top of it, and it will be a very good object indeed </s>
<s> The Plorn is highly excited to-day by reason of an institution which he tells me (after questioning George) is called the "Cobb, or Bodderin," holding a festival at The Falstaff </s>
<s> He is possessed of some vague information that they go to Higham Church, in pursuance of some old usage, and attend service there, and afterwards march round the village </s>
<s> It so far looks probable that they certainly started off at eleven very spare in numbers, and came back considerably recruited, which looks to me like the difference between going to church and coming to dinner </s>
<s> They bore no end of bright banners and broad sashes, and had a band with a terrific drum, and are now (at half-past two) dining at The Falstaff, partly in the side room on the ground-floor, and partly in a tent improvised this morning </s>

<s> I have presented the band with five shillings, which munificence has been highly appreciated </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr John Forster.] GAD'S HILL, _Thursday Night, Aug </s>
<s> 25th, 1859._ MY DEAR FORSTER, Heartily glad to get your letter this morning </s>
<s> I cannot easily tell you how much interested I am by what you tell me of our brave and excellent friend the Chief Baron, in connection with that ruffian </s>
<s> I followed the case with so much interest, and have followed the miserable knaves and asses who have perverted it since, with so much indignation, that I have often had more than half a mind to write and thank the upright judge who tried him </s>
<s> I declare to God that I believe such a service one of the greatest that a man of intellect and courage can render to society </s>
<s> Of course I saw the beast of a prisoner (with my mind's eye) delivering his cut-and-dried speech, and read in every word of it that no one but the murderer could have delivered or conceived it </s>
<s> Of course I have been driving the girls out of their wits here, by incessantly proclaiming that there needed no medical evidence either way, and that the case was plain without it </s>
<s> Lastly, of course (though a merciful man--because a merciful man I mean), I would hang any Home Secretary (Whig, Tory, Radical, or otherwise) who should step in between that black scoundrel and the gallows </s>
<s> I can_not_ believe--and my belief in all wrong as to public matters is enormous--that such a thing will be done </s>
<s> I am reminded of Tennyson, by thinking that King Arthur would have made short work of the amiable ----, whom the newspapers strangely delight to make a sort of gentleman of </s>
<s> How fine the "Idylls" are </s>
<s> Lord </s>
<s> what a blessed thing it is to read a man who can write </s>
<s> I thought nothing could be grander than the first poem till I came to the third; but when I had read the last, it seemed to be absolutely unapproached and unapproachable </s>
<s> To come to myself </s>
<s> I have written and begged the "All the Year Round" publisher to send you directly four weeks' proofs beyond the current number, that are in type </s>
<s> I hope you will like them </s>
<s> Nothing but the interest of the subject, and the pleasure of striving with the difficulty of the forms of treatment, nothing in the mere way of money, I mean, could also repay the time and trouble of the incessant condensation </s>
<s> But I set myself the little task of making a _picturesque_ story, rising in every chapter with characters true to nature, but whom the story itself should express, more than they should express themselves, by dialogue </s>
<s> I mean, in other words, that I fancied a story of incident might be written, in place of the bestiality that _is_ written under that pretence, pounding the characters out in its own mortar, and beating their own interests out of them </s>
<s> If you could have read the story all at once, I hope you wouldn't have stopped halfway </s>
<s> As to coming to your retreat, my dear Forster, think how helpless I am </s>
<s> I am not well yet </s>
<s> I have an instinctive feeling that nothing but the sea will restore me, and I am planning to go and work at Ballard's, at Broadstairs, from next Wednesday to Monday </s>
<s> I generally go to town on Monday afternoon </s>
<s> All Tuesday I am at the office, on Wednesday I come back here, and go to work again </s>
<s> I don't leave off till Monday comes round once more </s>
<s> I am fighting to get my story done by the first week in October </s>
<s> On the 10th of October I am going away to read for a fortnight at Ipswich, Norwich, Oxford, Cambridge, and a few other places </s>
<s> Judge what my spare time is just now </s>
<s> I am very much surprised and very sorry to find from the enclosed that Elliotson has been ill </s>
<s> I never heard a word of it </s>
<s> Georgy sends best love to you and to Mrs Forster, so do I, so does Plorn, so does Frank </s>
<s> The girls are, for five days, with the Whites at Ramsgate </s>
<s> It is raining, intensely hot, and stormy </s>
<s> Eighteen creatures, like little tortoises, have dashed in at the window and fallen on the paper since I began this paragraph [Illustration: ink-blot] (that was one!) </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr Frank Stone, A.R.A.] PETERBOROUGH, _Wednesday Evening, Oct </s>
<s> 19th, 1859._ MY DEAR STONE, We had a splendid rush last night--exactly as we supposed, with the pressure on the two shillings, of whom we turned a crowd away </s>
<s> They were a far finer audience than on the previous night; I think the finest I have ever read to </s>
<s> They took every word of the "Dombey" in quite an amazing manner, and after the child's death, paused a little, and then set up a shout that it did one good to hear </s>
<s> Mrs Gamp then set in with a roar, which lasted until I had done </s>
<s> I think everybody for the time forgot everything but the matter in hand </s>
<s> It was as fine an instance of thorough absorption in a fiction as any of us are likely to see ever again </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Monsieur Regnier.] TAVISTOCK HOUSE, TAVISTOCK SQUARE, LONDON, W.C., _Wednesday, Nov </s>
<s> 16th, 1859._ MY DEAR REGNIER, I send you ten thousand thanks for your kind and explicit letter </s>
<s> What I particularly wished to ascertain from you was, whether it is likely the Censor would allow such a piece to be played in Paris </s>
<s> In the case of its being likely, then I wished to have the piece as well done as possible, and would even have proposed to come to Paris to see it rehearsed </s>
<s> But I very much doubted whether the general subject would not be objectionable to the Government, and what you write with so much sagacity and with such care convinces me at once that its representation would be prohibited </s>
<s> Therefore I altogether abandon and relinquish the idea </s>
<s> But I am just as heartily and cordially obliged to you for your interest and friendship, as if the book had been turned into a play five hundred times </s>
<s> I again thank you ten thousand times, and am quite sure that you are right </s>
<s> I only hope you will forgive my causing you so much trouble, after your hard work </s>
<s> My girls and Georgina send their kindest regards to Madame Regnier and to you </s>
<s> My Gad's Hill house (I think I omitted to tell you, in reply to your enquiry) is on the very scene of Falstaff's robbery </s>
<s> There is a little _cabaret_ at the roadside, still called The Sir John Falstaff </s>
<s> And the country, in all its general features, is, at this time, what it was in Shakespeare's </s>
<s> I hope you will see the house before long </s>
<s> It is really a pretty place, and a good residence for an English writer, is it not </s>
<s> Macready, we are all happy to hear from himself, is going to leave the dreary tomb in which he lives, at Sherborne, and to remove to Cheltenham, a large and handsome place, about four or five hours' railway journey from London, where his poor girls will at least see and hear some life </s>
<s> Madame Céleste was with me yesterday, wishing to dramatise "A Tale of Two Cities" for the Lyceum, after bringing out the Christmas pantomime </s>
<s> I gave her my permission and the book; but I fear that her company (troupe) is a very poor one </s>
<s> This is all the news I have, except (which is no news at all) that I feel as if I had not seen you for fifty years, and that I am ever your attached and faithful Friend </s>
