<s> _Wednesday, July 27th, 1864._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> FITZGERALD, First, let me assure you that it gave us all real pleasure to see your sister and you at Gad's Hill, and that we all hope you will both come and stay a day or two with us when you are next in England </s>
<s> Next, let me convey to you the intelligence that I resolve to launch "Miss Manuel," fully confiding in your conviction of the power of the story </s>
<s> On all business points, Wills will communicate with you </s>
<s> I purpose beginning its publication in our first September number, therefore there is no time to be lost </s>
<s> The only suggestion I have to make as to the MS </s>
<s> in hand and type is, that Captain Fermor wants relief </s>
<s> It is a disagreeable character, as you mean it to be, and I should be afraid to do so much with him, if the case were mine, without taking the taste of him, here and there, out of the reader's mouth </s>
<s> It is remarkable that if you do not administer a disagreeable character carefully, the public have a decided tendency to think that the _story_ is disagreeable, and not merely the fictitious person </s>
<s> What do you think of the title, NEVER FORGOTTEN </s>
<s> It is a good one in itself, would express the eldest sister's pursuit, and glanced at now and then in the text, would hold the reader in suspense </s>
<s> I would propose to add the line, BY THE AUTHOR OF BELLA DONNA </s>
<s> Let me know your opinion as to the title </s>
<s> I need not assure you that the greatest care will be taken of you here, and that we shall make you as thoroughly well and widely known as we possibly can </s>
<s> Very faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Sir James Emerson Tennent.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Friday, Aug </s>
<s> 26th, 1864._ MY DEAR TENNENT, Believe me, I fully intended to come to you--did not doubt that I should come--and have greatly disappointed Mary and her aunt, as well as myself, by not coming </s>
<s> But I do not feel safe in going out for a visit </s>
<s> The mere knowledge that I had such a thing before me would put me out </s>
<s> It is not the length of time consumed, or the distance traversed, but it is the departure from a settled habit and a continuous sacrifice of pleasures that comes in question </s>
<s> This is an old story with me </s>
<s> I have never divided a book of my writing with anything else, but have always wrought at it to the exclusion of everything else; and it is now too late to change </s>
<s> After receiving your kind note I resolved to make another trial </s>
<s> But the hot weather and a few other drawbacks did not mend the matter, for I have dropped astern this month instead of going ahead </s>
<s> So I have seen Forster, and shown him my chains, and am reduced to taking exercise in them, like Baron Trenck </s>
<s> I am heartily pleased that you set so much store by the dedication </s>
<s> You may be sure that it does not make me the less anxious to take pains, and to work out well what I have in my mind </s>
<s> Mary and Georgina unite with me in kindest regards to Lady Tennent and Miss Tennent, and wish me to report that while they are seriously disappointed, they still feel there is no help for it </s>
<s> I can testify that they had great pleasure in the anticipation of the visit, and that their faces were very long and blank indeed when I began to hint my doubts </s>
<s> They fought against them valiantly as long as there was a chance, but they see my difficulty as well as anyone not myself can </s>
<s> Believe me, my dear Tennent, ever faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Clarkson Stanfield, R.A.] THE ATHENÆUM, _Wednesday, Sept </s>
<s> 21st, 1864._ MY DEAR STANNY, I met George in the street a few days ago, and he gave me a wonderful account of the effect of your natural element upon you at Ramsgate </s>
<s> I expect you to come back looking about twenty-nine, and feeling about nineteen </s>
<s> This morning I have looked in here to put down Fechter as a candidate, on the chance of the committee's electing him some day or other </s>
<s> He is a most devoted worshipper of yours, and would take it as a great honour if you would second him </s>
<s> Supposing you to have not the least objection (of course, if you should have any, I can in a moment provide a substitute), will you write your name in the candidates' book as his seconder when you are next in town and passing this way </s>
<s> Lastly, if you should be in town on his opening night (a Saturday, and in all probability the 22nd of October), will you come and dine at the office and see his new piece </s>
<s> You have not yet "pronounced" in the matter of that new French stage of his, on which Calcott for the said new piece has built up all manner of villages, camps, Versailles gardens, etc etc etc etc, with no wings, no flies, no looking off in any direction </s>
<s> If you tell me that you are to be in town by that time, I will not fail to refresh your memory as to the precise day </s>

<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, _Tuesday, Oct </s>
<s> 25th, 1864._ MY DEAR CERJAT, Here is a limping brute of a reply to your always-welcome Christmas letter </s>
<s> But, as usual, when I have done my day's work, I jump up from my desk and rush into air and exercise, and find letter-writing the most difficult thing in my daily life </s>
<s> I hope that your asthmatic tendencies may not be strong just now; but Townshend's account of the premature winter at Lausanne is not encouraging, and with us here in England all such disorders have been aggravated this autumn </s>
<s> However, a man of your dignity _must_ have either asthma or gout, and I hope you have got the better of the two </s>
<s> In London there is, as you see by the papers, extraordinarily little news </s>
<s> At present the apprehension (rather less than it was thought) of a commercial crisis, and the trial of Müller next Thursday, are the two chief sensations </s>
<s> I hope that gentleman will be hanged, and have hardly a doubt of it, though croakers contrariwise are not wanting </s>
<s> It is difficult to conceive any other line of defence than that the circumstances proved, taken separately, are slight </s>
<s> But a sound judge will immediately charge the jury that the strength of the circumstances lies in their being put together, and will thread them together on a fatal rope </s>
<s> As to the Church, my friend, I am sick of it </s>
<s> The spectacle presented by the indecent squabbles of priests of most denominations, and the exemplary unfairness and rancour with which they conduct their differences, utterly repel me </s>
<s> And the idea of the Protestant establishment, in the face of its own history, seeking to trample out discussion and private judgment, is an enormity so cool, that I wonder the Right Reverends, Very Reverends, and all other Reverends, who commit it, can look in one another's faces without laughing, as the old soothsayers did </s>
<s> Perhaps they can't and don't </s>
<s> How our sublime and so-different Christian religion is to be administered in the future I cannot pretend to say, but that the Church's hand is at its own throat I am fully convinced </s>
<s> Here, more Popery, there, more Methodism--as many forms of consignment to eternal damnation as there are articles, and all in one forever quarrelling body--the Master of the New Testament put out of sight, and the rage and fury almost always turning on the letter of obscure parts of the Old Testament, which itself has been the subject of accommodation, adaptation, varying interpretation without end--these things cannot last </s>
<s> The Church that is to have its part in the coming time must be a more Christian one, with less arbitrary pretensions and a stronger hold upon the mantle of our Saviour, as He walked and talked upon this earth </s>
<s> Of family intelligence I have very little </s>
<s> Charles Collins continuing in a very poor way, and showing no signs of amendment </s>
<s> He and my daughter Katie went to Wiesbaden and thence to Nice, where they are now </s>
<s> I have strong apprehensions that he will never recover, and that she will be left a young widow </s>
<s> All the rest are as they were </s>
<s> Mary neither married nor going to be; Georgina holding them all together and perpetually corresponding with the distant ones; occasional rallyings coming off here, in which another generation begins to peep above the table </s>
<s> I once used to think what a horrible thing it was to be a grandfather </s>
<s> Finding that the calamity falls upon me without my perceiving any other change in myself, I bear it like a man </s>
<s> Mrs Watson has bought a house in town, to which she repairs in the season, for the bringing out of her daughter </s>
<s> She is now at Rockingham </s>
<s> Her eldest son is said to be as good an eldest son as ever was, and to make her position there a perfectly independent and happy one </s>
<s> I have not seen him for some years; her I often see; but he ought to be a good fellow, and is very popular in his neighbourhood </s>
<s> I have altered this place very much since you were here, and have made a pretty (I think an unusually pretty) drawing-room </s>
<s> I wish you would come back and see it </s>
<s> My being on the Dover line, and my being very fond of France, occasion me to cross the Channel perpetually </s>
<s> Whenever I feel that I have worked too much, or am on the eve of overdoing it, and want a change, away I go by the mail-train, and turn up in Paris or anywhere else that suits my humour, next morning </s>
<s> So I come back as fresh as a daisy, and preserve as ruddy a face as though I never leant over a sheet of paper </s>
<s> When I retire from a literary life I think of setting up as a Channel pilot </s>
<s> Pray give my love to Mrs Cerjat, and tell her that I should like to go up the Great St </s>
<s> Bernard again, and shall be glad to know if she is open to another ascent </s>
<s> Old days in Switzerland are ever fresh to me, and sometimes I walk with you again, after dark, outside the hotel at Martigny, while Lady Mary Taylour (wasn't it?) sang within very prettily </s>
<s> Lord, how the time goes </s>
<s> How many years ago </s>
<s> Affectionately yours </s>

<s> 1865 </s>
<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> For this spring a furnished house in Somer's Place, Hyde Park, had been taken, which Charles Dickens occupied, with his sister-in-law and daughter, from the beginning of March until June </s>
<s> During the year he paid two short visits to France </s>
<s> He was still at work upon "Our Mutual Friend," two numbers of which had been issued in January and February, when the first volume was published, with dedication to Sir James Emerson Tennent </s>
<s> The remaining numbers were issued between March and November, when the complete work was published in two volumes </s>
<s> The Christmas number, to which Charles Dickens contributed three stories, was called "Doctor Marigold's Prescriptions" </s>
<s> Being out of health, and much overworked, Charles Dickens, at the end of May, took his first short holiday trip into France </s>
<s> And on his way home, and on a day afterwards so fatal to him, the 9th of June, he was in that most terrible railway accident at Staplehurst </s>
<s> Many of our letters for this year have reference to this awful experience--an experience from the effects of which his nerves never wholly recovered </s>
<s> His letters to Mr Thomas Mitton and to Mrs Hulkes (an esteemed friend and neighbour) are graphic descriptions of this disaster </s>
<s> But they do NOT tell of the wonderful presence of mind and energy shown by Charles Dickens when most of the terrified passengers were incapable of thought or action, or of his gentleness and goodness to the dead and dying </s>
<s> The Mr Dickenson[14] mentioned in the letter to Mrs Hulkes soon recovered </s>
<s> He always considers that he owes his life to Charles Dickens, the latter having discovered and extricated him from beneath a carriage before it was too late </s>
<s> Our first letter to Mr Kent is one of congratulation upon his having become the proprietor of _The Sun_ newspaper </s>
<s> Professor Owen has been so kind as to give us some notes, which we publish for the sake of his great name </s>
<s> Charles Dickens had not much correspondence with Professor Owen, but there was a firm friendship and great mutual admiration between them </s>
<s> The letter to Mrs Procter is in answer to one from her, asking Charles Dickens to write a memoir of her daughter Adelaide, as a preface to a collected edition of her poems </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr William Charles Kent.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, Jan </s>
<s> 17th, 1865._ MY DEAR KENT, I meant to have written instantly on the appearance of your paper in its beautiful freshness, to congratulate you on its handsome appearance, and to send you my heartiest good wishes for its thriving and prosperous career </s>
<s> Through a mistake of the postman's, that remarkable letter has been tesselated into the Infernal Pavement instead of being delivered in the Strand </s>
<s> We have been looking and waiting for your being well enough to propose yourself for a mouthful of fresh air </s>
<s> Are you well enough to come on Sunday </s>
<s> We shall be coming down from Charing Cross on Sunday morning, and I shall be going up again at nine on Monday morning </s>
<s> It amuses me to find that you don't see your way with a certain "Mutual Friend" of ours </s>
<s> I have a horrible suspicion that you may begin to be fearfully knowing at somewhere about No </s>
<s> 12 or 13 </s>
<s> But you shan't if I can help it </s>
<s> Your note delighted me because it dwelt upon the places in the number that _I_ dwell on </s>
<s> Not that that is anything new in your case, but it is always new to me in the pleasure I derive from it, which is truly inexpressible </s>
<s> Ever cordially yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Procter.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Wednesday, Feb </s>

<s> PROCTER, Of course I will do it, and of course I will do it for the love of you and Procter </s>
<s> You can give me my brief, and we can speak about its details </s>
<s> Once again, of course I will do it, and with all my heart </s>
<s> I have registered a vow (in which there is not the least merit, for I couldn't help it) that when I am, as I am now, very hard at work upon a book, I never will dine out more than one day in a week </s>

<s> Macready.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Wednesday, March 1st, 1865._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, I have been laid up here with a frost-bitten foot (from hard walking in the snow), or you would have heard from me sooner </s>
<s> My reply to Professor Agassiz is short, but conclusive </s>
<s> Daily seeing improper uses made of confidential letters in the addressing of them to a public audience that have no business with them, I made not long ago a great fire in my field at Gad's Hill, and burnt every letter I possessed </s>
<s> And now I always destroy every letter I receive not on absolute business, and my mind is so far at ease </s>
<s> Poor dear Felton's letters went up into the air with the rest, or his highly distinguished representative should have had them most willingly </s>
<s> We never fail to drink old P'.s health on his birthday, or to make him the subject of a thousand loving remembrances </s>
<s> With best love to Mrs Macready and Katie, Ever, my dearest Macready, Your most affectionate Friend </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> C </s>
<s> Macready.] 16, SOMER'S PLACE, HYDE PARK, _Saturday Night, April 22nd, 1865._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, A thousand thanks for your kind letter, most heartily welcome </s>
<s> My frost-bitten foot, after causing me great inconvenience and much pain, has begun to conduct itself amiably </s>
<s> I can now again walk my ten miles in the morning without inconvenience, but am absurdly obliged to sit shoeless all the evening--a very slight penalty, as I detest going out to dinner (which killed the original old Parr by-the-bye) </s>
<s> I am working like a dragon at my book, and am a terror to the household, likewise to all the organs and brass bands in this quarter </s>
<s> Gad's Hill is being gorgeously painted, and we are here until the 1st of June </s>
<s> I wish I might hope you would be there any time this summer; I really _have_ made the place comfortable and pretty by this time </s>
<s> It is delightful to us to hear such good news of Butty </s>
<s> She made so deep an impression on Fechter that he always asks me what Ceylon has done for her, and always beams when I tell him how thoroughly well it has made her </s>
<s> As to _you_, you are the youngest man (worth mentioning as a thorough man) that I know </s>
<s> Oh, let me be as young when I am as----did you think I was going to write "old" </s>
<s> No, sir--withdrawn from the wear and tear of busy life is my expression </s>
<s> Poole still holds out at Kentish Town, and says he is dying of solitude </s>
<s> His memory is astoundingly good </s>
<s> I see him about once in two or three months, and in the meantime he makes notes of questions to ask me when I come </s>
<s> Having fallen in arrear of the time, these generally refer to unknown words he has encountered in the newspapers </s>
<s> His three last (he always reads them with tremendous difficulty through an enormous magnifying-glass) were as follows: 1 </s>
<s> What's croquet </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> What's an Albert chain </s>
<s> 3 </s>
<s> Let me know the state of mind of the Queen </s>
<s> When I had delivered a neat exposition on these heads, he turned back to his memoranda, and came to something that the utmost power of the enormous magnifying-glass couldn't render legible </s>
<s> After a quarter of an hour or so, he said: "O yes, I know" </s>
<s> And then rose and clasped his hands above his head, and said: "Thank God, I am not a dram-drinker" </s>
<s> Do think of coming to Gad's in the summer; and do give my love to Mrs Macready, and tell her I know she can make you come if she will </s>
<s> Mary and Georgy send best and dearest loves to her, to you, and to Katie, and to baby </s>
<s> Johnny we suppose to be climbing the tree of knowledge elsewhere </s>
<s> My dearest Macready, ever yours most affectionately </s>

<s> Macready.] GAD'S HILL, _Monday, June 12th, 1865._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, [_So far in his own writing._] Many thanks for your kind words of remembrance.[15] This is not all in my own hand, because I am too much shaken to write many notes </s>
<s> Not by the beating and dragging of the carriage in which I was--it did not go over, but was caught on the turn, among the ruins of the bridge--but by the work afterwards to get out the dying and dead, which was terrible </s>
<s> [_The rest in his own writing_.] Ever your affectionate Friend </s>
<s> P.S.--My love to Mrs Macready </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Thomas Mitton.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, June 13th, 1865._ MY DEAR MITTON, I should have written to you yesterday or the day before, if I had been quite up to writing </s>
<s> I was in the only carriage that did not go over into the stream </s>
<s> It was caught upon the turn by some of the ruin of the bridge, and hung suspended and balanced in an apparently impossible manner </s>
<s> Two ladies were my fellow-passengers, an old one and a young one </s>
<s> This is exactly what passed </s>
<s> You may judge from it the precise length of the suspense: Suddenly we were off the rail, and beating the ground as the car of a half-emptied balloon might </s>
<s> The old lady cried out, "My God" </s>
<s> and the young one screamed </s>
<s> I caught hold of them both (the old lady sat opposite and the young one on my left), and said: "We can't help ourselves, but we can be quiet and composed </s>
<s> Pray don't cry out" </s>
<s> The old lady immediately answered: "Thank you </s>
<s> Rely upon me </s>
<s> Upon my soul I will be quiet" </s>
<s> We were then all tilted down together in a corner of the carriage, and stopped </s>
<s> I said to them thereupon: "You may be sure nothing worse can happen </s>
<s> Our danger _must_ be over </s>
<s> Will you remain here without stirring, while I get out of the window" </s>
<s> They both answered quite collectedly, "Yes," and I got out without the least notion what had happened </s>
<s> Fortunately I got out with great caution and stood upon the step </s>
<s> Looking down I saw the bridge gone, and nothing below me but the line of rail </s>
<s> Some people in the two other compartments were madly trying to plunge out at window, and had no idea that there was an open swampy field fifteen feet down below them, and nothing else </s>
<s> The two guards (one with his face cut) were running up and down on the down side of the bridge (which was not torn up) quite wildly </s>
<s> I called out to them: "Look at me </s>
<s> Do stop an instant and look at me, and tell me whether you don't know me" </s>
<s> One of them answered: "We know you very well, Mr Dickens" </s>
<s> "Then," I said, "my good fellow, for God's sake give me your key, and send one of those labourers here, and I'll empty this carriage" </s>
<s> We did it quite safely, by means of a plank or two, and when it was done I saw all the rest of the train, except the two baggage vans, down in the stream </s>
<s> I got into the carriage again for my brandy flask, took off my travelling hat for a basin, climbed down the brickwork, and filled my hat with water </s>
<s> Suddenly I came upon a staggering man covered with blood (I think he must have been flung clean out of his carriage), with such a frightful cut across the skull that I couldn't bear to look at him </s>
<s> I poured some water over his face and gave him some to drink, then gave him some brandy, and laid him down on the grass, and he said, "I am gone," and died afterwards </s>
<s> Then I stumbled over a lady lying on her back against a little pollard-tree, with the blood streaming over her face (which was lead colour) in a number of distinct little streams from the head </s>
<s> I asked her if she could swallow a little brandy and she just nodded, and I gave her some and left her for somebody else </s>
<s> The next time I passed her she was dead </s>
<s> Then a man, examined at the inquest yesterday (who evidently had not the least remembrance of what really passed), came running up to me and implored me to help him find his wife, who was afterwards found dead </s>
<s> No imagination can conceive the ruin of the carriages, or the extraordinary weights under which the people were lying, or the complications into which they were twisted up among iron and wood, and mud and water </s>
<s> I don't want to be examined at the inquest, and I don't want to write about it </s>
<s> I could do no good either way, and I could only seem to speak about myself, which, of course, I would rather not do </s>
<s> I am keeping very quiet here </s>
<s> I have a--I don't know what to call it--constitutional (I suppose) presence of mind, and was not in the least fluttered at the time </s>
<s> I instantly remembered that I had the MS </s>
<s> of a number with me, and clambered back into the carriage for it </s>
<s> But in writing these scanty words of recollection I feel the shake and am obliged to stop </s>
<s> Ever faithfully </s>

<s> In the moment of going over the viaduct the whole of his pockets were shaken empty </s>

<s> He had been choking a quarter of an hour when I heard him groaning </s>

<s> As it was, I brought him up to London in the carriage with me, and couldn't make him believe he was hurt </s>
<s> He was the first person whom the brandy saved </s>
<s> As I ran back to the carriage for the whole full bottle, I saw the first two people I had helped lying dead </s>
<s> A bit of shade from the hot sun, into which we got the unhurt ladies, soon had as many dead in it as living </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>

<s> At the time in question I shall, please God, either have just finished, or be just finishing, my present book </s>
<s> Country rest and reflection will then be invaluable to me, before casting about for Christmas </s>
<s> I am a little shaken in my nervous system by the terrible and affecting incidents of the late railway accident, from which I bodily escaped </s>
<s> I am withdrawing myself from engagements of all kinds, in order that I may pursue my story with the comfortable sense of being perfectly free while it is a-doing, and when it is done </s>
<s> The consciousness of having made this engagement would, if I were to make it, render such sense incomplete, and so open the way to others </s>
<s> This is the real state of the case, and the whole reason for my declining </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>

<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _November 13th, 1865._ EXTRACT </s>
<s> MY DEAR CERJAT, Having achieved my book and my Christmas number, and having shaken myself after two years' work, I send you my annual greeting </s>
<s> How are you </s>
<s> Asthmatic, I know you will reply; but as my poor father (who was asthmatic, too, and the jolliest of men) used philosophically to say, "one must have something wrong, I suppose, and I like to know what it is" </s>
<s> In England we are groaning under the brigandage of the butcher, which is being carried to that height that I think I foresee resistance on the part of the middle-class, and some combination in perspective for abolishing the middleman, whensoever he turns up (which is everywhere) between producer and consumer </s>
<s> The cattle plague is the butcher's stalking-horse, and it is unquestionably worse than it was; but seeing that the great majority of creatures lost or destroyed have been cows, and likewise that the rise in butchers' meat bears no reasonable proportion to the market prices of the beasts, one comes to the conclusion that the public is done </s>
<s> The commission has ended very weakly and ineffectually, as such things in England rather frequently do; and everybody writes to _The Times_, and nobody does anything else </s>
<s> If the Americans don't embroil us in a war before long it will not be their fault </s>
<s> What with their swagger and bombast, what with their claims for indemnification, what with Ireland and Fenianism, and what with Canada, I have strong apprehensions </s>
<s> With a settled animosity towards the French usurper, I believe him to have always been sound in his desire to divide the States against themselves, and that we were unsound and wrong in "letting I dare not wait upon I would" </s>
<s> The Jamaica insurrection is another hopeful piece of business </s>
<s> That platform-sympathy with the black--or the native, or the devil--afar off, and that platform indifference to our own countrymen at enormous odds in the midst of bloodshed and savagery, makes me stark wild </s>
<s> Only the other day, here was a meeting of jawbones of asses at Manchester, to censure the Jamaica Governor for his manner of putting down the insurrection </s>
<s> So we are badgered about New Zealanders and Hottentots, as if they were identical with men in clean shirts at Camberwell, and were to be bound by pen and ink accordingly </s>
<s> So Exeter Hall holds us in mortal submission to missionaries, who (Livingstone always excepted) are perfect nuisances, and leave every place worse than they found it </s>
<s> Of all the many evidences that are visible of our being ill-governed, no one is so remarkable to me as our ignorance of what is going on under our Government </s>
<s> What will future generations think of that enormous Indian Mutiny being ripened without suspicion, until whole regiments arose and killed their officers </s>
<s> A week ago, red tape, half-bouncing and half pooh-poohing what it bounced at, would have scouted the idea of a Dublin jail not being able to hold a political prisoner </s>
<s> But for the blacks in Jamaica being over-impatient and before their time, the whites might have been exterminated, without a previous hint or suspicion that there was anything amiss </s>
<s> _Laissez aller_, and Britons never, never, never!---- Meantime, if your honour were in London, you would see a great embankment rising high and dry out of the Thames on the Middlesex shore, from Westminster Bridge to Blackfriars </s>
<s> A really fine work, and really getting on </s>
<s> Moreover, a great system of drainage </s>
<s> Another really fine work, and likewise really getting on </s>
<s> Lastly, a muddle of railways in all directions possible and impossible, with no general public scheme, no general public supervision, enormous waste of money, no fixable responsibility, no accountability but under Lord Campbell's Act </s>
<s> I think of that accident in which I was preserved </s>
<s> Before the most furious and notable train in the four-and-twenty hours, the head of a gang of workmen takes up the rails </s>
<s> That train changes its time every day as the tide changes, and that head workman is not provided by the railway company with any clock or watch </s>
<s> Lord Shaftesbury wrote to me to ask me what I thought of an obligation on railway companies to put strong walls to all bridges and viaducts </s>
<s> I told him, of course, that the force of such a shock would carry away anything that any company could set up, and I added: "Ask the minister what _he_ thinks about the votes of the railway interest in the House of Commons, and about his being afraid to lay a finger on it with an eye to his majority" </s>
<s> I seem to be grumbling, but I am in the best of humours </s>
<s> All goes well with me and mine, thank God </s>
<s> Last night my gardener came upon a man in the garden and fired </s>
<s> The man returned the compliment by kicking him in the groin and causing him great pain </s>
<s> I set off, with a great mastiff-bloodhound I have, in pursuit </s>
<s> Couldn't find the evil-doer, but had the greatest difficulty in preventing the dog from tearing two policemen down </s>
<s> They were coming towards us with professional mystery, and he was in the air on his way to the throat of an eminently respectable constable when I caught him </s>
<s> My daughter Mary and her aunt Georgina send kindest regard and remembrance </s>
<s> Katey and her husband are going to try London this winter, but I rather doubt (for they are both delicate) their being able to weather it out </s>
<s> It has been blowing here tremendously for a fortnight, but to-day is like a spring day, and plenty of roses are growing over the labourers' cottages </s>
<s> The _Great Eastern_ lies at her moorings beyond the window where I write these words; looks very dull and unpromising </s>
<s> A dark column of smoke from Chatham Dockyard, where the iron shipbuilding is in progress, has a greater significance in it, I fancy </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, Nov </s>
<s> 14th, 1865._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, As you want to know my views of the Sphinx, here they are </s>
<s> But I have only seen it once; and it is so extraordinarily well done, that it ought to be observed closely several times </s>
<s> Anyone who attentively notices the flower trick will see that the two little high tables hung with drapery cover each a trap </s>
<s> Each of those tables, during that trick, hides a confederate, who changes the paper cone twice </s>
<s> When the cone has been changed as often as is required, the trap is closed and the table can be moved </s>
<s> When the curtain is removed for the performance of the Sphinx trick, there is a covered, that is, draped table on the stage, which is never seen before or afterwards </s>
<s> In front of the middle of it, and between it and the audience, stands one of those little draped tables covering a trap; this is a third trap in the centre of the stage </s>
<s> The box for the head is then upon IT, and the conjuror takes it off and shows it </s>
<s> The man whose head is afterwards shown in that box is, I conceive, in the table; that is to say, is lying on his chest in the thickness of the table, in an extremely constrained attitude </s>
<s> To get him into the table, and to enable him to use the trap in the table through which his head comes into the box, the two hands of a confederate are necessary </s>
<s> That confederate comes up a trap, and stands in the space afforded by the interval below the stage and the height of the little draped table </s>
<s> his back is towards the audience </s>
<s> The moment he has assisted the hidden man sufficiently, he closes the trap, and the conjuror then immediately removes the little draped table, and also the drapery of the larger table; when he places the box on the last-named table _with the slide on_ for the head to come into it, he stands with his back to the audience and his face to the box, and masks the box considerably to facilitate the insertion of the head </s>
<s> As soon as he knows the head to be in its place, he undraws the slide </s>
<s> When the verses have been spoken and the trick is done, he loses no time in replacing the slide </s>
<s> The curtain is then immediately dropped, because the man cannot otherwise be got out of the table, and has no doubt had quite enough of it </s>
<s> With kindest regards to all at Penton, Ever your most affectionate </s>

<s> [15] This was a circular note which he sent in answer to innumerable letters of enquiry, after the accident </s>

<s> 1866 </s>
<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> The furnished house hired by Charles Dickens in the spring of this year was in Southwick Place, Hyde Park </s>
<s> Having entered into negotiations with the Messrs </s>
<s> Chappell for a series of readings to be given in London, in the English provinces, in Scotland and Ireland, Charles Dickens had no leisure for more than his usual editorial work for "All the Year Round" </s>
<s> He contributed four parts to the Christmas number, which was entitled, "Mugby Junction" </s>
<s> For the future all his English readings were given in connection with the Messrs </s>
<s> Chappell, and never in all his career had he more satisfactory or more pleasant business relations than those connected with these gentlemen </s>
<s> Moreover, out of this connection sprang a sincere friendship on both sides </s>
<s> Mr Dolby is so constantly mentioned in future letters, that they themselves will tell of the cordial companionship which existed between Charles Dickens and this able and most obliging "manager" </s>
<s> The letter to "Lily" was in answer to a child's letter from Miss Lily Benzon, inviting him to a birthday party </s>
<s> The play alluded to in the letter to M </s>
<s> Fechter was called "A Long Strike," and was performed at the Lyceum Theatre </s>
<s> The "Sultan" mentioned in the letter to Mr Fitzgerald was a noble Irish bloodhound, presented by this gentleman to Charles Dickens </s>
<s> The story of the dog's death is told in a letter to M </s>
<s> de Cerjat, which we give in the following year </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Mary Boyle.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Saturday, Jan </s>
<s> 6th, 1866._ MY DEAR MARY, Feeling pretty certain that I shall never answer your letter unless I answer it at once (I got it this morning), here goes </s>
<s> I did not dramatise "The Master of Ravenswood," though I did a good deal towards and about the piece, having an earnest desire to put Scott, for once, upon the stage in his own gallant manner </s>
<s> It is _an enormous success_, and increases in attraction nightly </s>
<s> I have never seen the people in all parts of the house so leaning forward, in lines sloping towards the stage, earnestly and intently attractive, as while the story gradually unfolds itself </s>
<s> But the astonishing circumstance of all is, that Miss Leclercq (never thought of for Lucy till all other Lucies had failed) is marvellously good, highly pathetic, and almost unrecognisable in person </s>
<s> What note it touches in her, always dumb until now, I do not pretend to say, but there is no one on the stage who could play the contract scene better, or more simply and naturally, and I find it impossible to see it without crying </s>
<s> Almost everyone plays well, the whole is exceedingly picturesque, and there is scarcely a movement throughout, or a look, that is not indicated by Scott </s>
<s> So you get a life romance with beautiful illustrations, and I do not expect ever again to see a book take up its bed and walk in like manner </s>
<s> I am charmed to learn that you have had a freeze out of my ghost story </s>
<s> It rather did give me a shiver up the back in the writing </s>
<s> "Dr </s>
<s> Marigold" has just now accomplished his two hundred thousand </s>
<s> My only other news about myself is that I am doubtful whether to read or not in London this season </s>
<s> If I decide to do it at all, I shall probably do it on a large scale </s>
<s> Many happy years to you, my dear Mary </s>
<s> So prays Your ever affectionate Jo </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr William Charles Kent.] GAD'S HILL, _Thursday, Jan </s>
<s> 18th, 1866._ MY DEAR KENT, I cannot tell you how grieved we all are here to know that you are suffering again </s>
<s> Your patient tone, however, and the hopefulness and forbearance of Ferguson's course, gives us some reassurance </s>
<s> Apropos of which latter reference I dined with Ferguson at the Lord Mayor's, last Tuesday, and had a grimly distracted impulse upon me to defy the toast-master and rush into a speech about him and his noble art, when I sat pining under the imbecility of constitutional and corporational idiots </s>
<s> I did seize him for a moment by the hair of his head (in proposing the Lady Mayoress), and derived some faint consolation from the company's response to the reference </s>
<s> O </s>
<s> no man will ever know under what provocation to contradiction and a savage yell of repudiation I suffered at the hands of ----, feebly complacent in the uniform of Madame Tussaud's own military waxers, and almost the worst speaker I ever heard in my life </s>
<s> Mary and Georgina, sitting on either side of me, urged me to "look pleasant" </s>
<s> I replied in expressions not to be repeated </s>
<s> Shea (the judge) was just as good and graceful, as he (the member) was bad and gawky </s>
<s> Bulwer's "Lost Tales of Miletus" is a most noble book </s>

<s> Try us, only try us, and we are content to stake the reputation of the establishment on the result </s>
<s> Ever affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Percy Fitzgerald.] GAD'S HILL, _Friday, Feb </s>
<s> 2nd, 1866._ MY DEAR FITZGERALD, I ought to have written to you days and days ago, to thank you for your charming book on Charles Lamb, to tell you with what interest and pleasure I read it as soon as it came here, and to add that I was honestly affected (far more so than your modesty will readily believe) by your intimate knowledge of those touches of mine concerning childhood </s>
<s> Let me tell you now that I have not in the least cooled, after all, either as to the graceful sympathetic book, or as to the part in it with which I am honoured </s>
<s> It has become a matter of real feeling with me, and I postponed its expression because I couldn't satisfactorily get it out of myself, and at last I came to the conclusion that it must be left in </s>
<s> My dear Fitzgerald, faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Friday, Feb </s>
<s> 9th, 1866._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, I found your letter here when I came back on Wednesday evening, and was extremely glad to get it </s>
<s> Frank Beard wrote me word that with such a pulse as I described, an examination of the heart was absolutely necessary, and that I had better make an appointment with him alone for the purpose </s>
<s> This I did </s>
<s> I was not at all disconcerted, for I knew well beforehand that the effect could not possibly be without that one cause at the bottom of it </s>
<s> There seems to be degeneration of some functions of the heart </s>
<s> It does not contract as it should </s>
<s> So I have got a prescription of iron, quinine, and digitalis, to set it a-going, and send the blood more quickly through the system </s>
<s> If it should not seem to succeed on a reasonable trial, I will then propose a consultation with someone else </s>
<s> Of course I am not so foolish as to suppose that all my work can have been achieved without _some_ penalty, and I have noticed for some time a decided change in my buoyancy and hopefulness--in other words, in my usual "tone" </s>
<s> I shall wait to see Beard again on Monday, and shall most probably come down that day </s>
<s> If I should not, I will telegraph after seeing him </s>
<s> Best love to Mamie </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Brookfield.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 20th, 1866._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> BROOKFIELD, Having gone through your MS </s>
<s> (which I should have done sooner, but that I have not been very well), I write these few following words about it </s>
<s> Firstly, with a limited reference to its unsuitability to these pages </s>
<s> Secondly, with a more enlarged reference to the merits of the story itself </s>
<s> If you will take any part of it and cut it up (in fancy) into the small portions into which it would have to be divided here for only a month's supply, you will (I think) at once discover the impossibility of publishing it in weekly parts </s>
<s> The scheme of the chapters, the manner of introducing the people, the progress of the interest, the places in which the principal places fall, are all hopelessly against it </s>
<s> It would seem as though the story were never coming, and hardly ever moving </s>
<s> There must be a special design to overcome that specially trying mode of publication, and I cannot better express the difficulty and labour of it than by asking you to turn over any two weekly numbers of "A Tale of Two Cities," or "Great Expectations," or Bulwer's story, or Wilkie Collins's, or Reade's, or "At the Bar," and notice how patiently and expressly the thing has to be planned for presentation in these fragments, and yet for afterwards fusing together as an uninterrupted whole </s>
<s> Of the story itself I honestly say that I think highly </s>
<s> The style is particularly easy and agreeable, infinitely above ordinary writing, and sometimes reminds me of Mrs Inchbald at her best </s>
<s> The characters are remarkably well observed, and with a rare mixture of delicacy and truthfulness </s>
<s> I observe this particularly in the brother and sister, and in Mrs Neville </s>
<s> But it strikes me that you constantly hurry your narrative (and yet without getting on) _by telling it, in a sort of impetuous breathless way, in your own person, when the people should tell it and act it for themselves_ </s>
<s> My notion always is, that when I have made the people to play out the play, it is, as it were, their business to do it, and not mine </s>
<s> Then, unless you really have led up to a great situation like Basil's death, you are bound in art to make more of it </s>
<s> Such a scene should form a chapter of itself </s>
<s> Impressed upon the reader's memory, it would go far to make the fortune of the book </s>
<s> Suppose yourself telling that affecting incident in a letter to a friend </s>
<s> Wouldn't you describe how you went through the life and stir of the streets and roads to the sick-room </s>
<s> Wouldn't you say what kind of room it was, what time of day it was, whether it was sunlight, starlight, or moonlight </s>
<s> Wouldn't you have a strong impression on your mind of how you were received, when you first met the look of the dying man, what strange contrasts were about you and struck you </s>
<s> I don't want you, in a novel, to present _yourself_ to tell such things, but I want the things to be there </s>
<s> You make no more of the situation than the index might, or a descriptive playbill might in giving a summary of the tragedy under representation </s>
<s> As a mere piece of mechanical workmanship, I think all your chapters should be shorter; that is to say, that they should be subdivided </s>
<s> Also, when you change from narrative to dialogue, or _vice versâ_, you should make the transition more carefully </s>
<s> Also, taking the pains to sit down and recall the principal landmarks in your story, you should then make them far more elaborate and conspicuous than the rest </s>
<s> Even with these changes I do not believe that the story would attract the attention due to it, if it were published even in such monthly portions as the space of "Fraser" would admit of </s>
<s> Even so brightened, it would not, to the best of my judgment, express itself piecemeal </s>
<s> It seems to me to be so constituted as to require to be read "off the reel" </s>
<s> As a book in two volumes I think it would have good claims to success, and good chances of obtaining success </s>
<s> But I suppose the polishing I have hinted at (not a meretricious adornment, but positively necessary to good work and good art) to have been first thoroughly administered </s>
<s> Now don't hate me if you can help it </s>
<s> I can afford to be hated by some people, but I am not rich enough to put you in possession of that luxury </s>
<s> Ever faithfully yours </s>
<s> P.S.--The MS </s>
<s> shall be delivered at your house to-morrow </s>
<s> And your petitioner again prays not to be, etc [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] ADELPHI, LIVERPOOL, _Friday, April 13th, 1866._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, The reception at Manchester last night was quite a magnificent sight; the whole of the immense audience standing up and cheering </s>

<s> He was put to bed in a public opposite, and was left there, poor man </s>

<s> I have taken advantage of it by crossing to Birkenhead and getting some air upon the water </s>
<s> It was fresh and beautiful </s>

<s> I am, of course, tired (the pull of "Marigold" upon one's energy, in the Free Trade Hall, was great); but I stick to my tonic, and feel, all things considered, in very good tone </s>
<s> The room here (I mean the hall) being my special favourite and extraordinarily easy, is _almost_ a rest </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] WATERLOO HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Wednesday, April 18th, 1866._ We had a tremendous house again last night at Glasgow; and turned away great numbers </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Lily Benzon.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, June 18th, 1866._ MY DEAR LILY, I am sorry that I cannot come to read to you "The Boots at the Holly Tree Inn," as you ask me to do; but the truth is, that I am tired of reading at this present time, and have come into the country to rest and hear the birds sing </s>
<s> There are a good many birds, I daresay, in Kensington Palace Gardens, and upon my word and honour they are much better worth listening to than I am </s>

<s> 13th, 1866._ MY DEAR PROCTER, I have read your biography of Charles Lamb with inexpressible pleasure and interest </s>
<s> I do not think it possible to tell a pathetic story with a more unaffected and manly tenderness </s>
<s> And as to the force and vigour of the style, if I did not know you I should have made sure that there was a printer's error in the opening of your introduction, and that the word "seventy" occupied the place of "forty" </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Sir James Emerson Tennent.] GAD'S HILL, _Monday, Aug </s>
<s> 20th, 1866._ MY DEAR TENNENT, I have been very much interested by your extract, and am strongly inclined to believe that the founder of the Refuge for Poor Travellers meant the kind of man to which it refers </s>
<s> Chaucer certainly meant the Pardonere to be a humbug, living on the credulity of the people </s>
<s> After describing the sham reliques he carried, he says: But with these relikes whawne that he found A poure personne dwelling up on lond Upon a day he gat him more monnie Than that the personne got in monthes time, And thus, with fained flattering and japes He made the personne, and the people, his apes </s>
<s> And the worthy Watts (founder of the charity) may have had these very lines in his mind when he excluded such a man </s>
<s> When I last heard from my boy he was coming to you, and was full of delight and dignity </s>
<s> My midshipman has just been appointed to the _Bristol_, on the West Coast of Africa, and is on his voyage out to join her </s>
<s> I wish it was another ship and another station </s>
<s> She has been unlucky in losing men </s>
<s> Kindest regard from all my house to yours </s>
<s> Faithfully yours ever </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> Charles Fechter.] GAD'S HILL, _Tuesday, Sept </s>
<s> 4th, 1866._ MY DEAR FECHTER, This morning I received the play to the end of the telegraph scene, and I have since read it twice </s>
<s> I clearly see the _ground_ of Mr Boucicault's two objections; but I do not see their _force_ </s>
<s> First, as to the writing </s>
<s> If the characters did not speak in a terse and homely way, their idea and language would be inconsistent with their dress and station, and they would lose, as characters, before the audience </s>
<s> The dialogue seems to be exactly what is wanted </s>
<s> Its simplicity (particularly in Mr Boucicault's part) is often very effective; and throughout there is an honest, straight-to-the-purpose ruggedness in it, like the real life and the real people </s>
<s> Secondly, as to the absence of the comic element </s>
<s> I really do not see how more of it could be got into the story, and I think Mr Boucicault underrates the pleasant effect of his own part </s>
<s> The very notion of a sailor, whose life is not among those little courts and streets, and whose business does not lie with the monotonous machinery, but with the four wild winds, is a relief to me in reading the play </s>
<s> I am quite confident of its being an immense relief to the audience when they see the sailor before them, with an entirely different bearing, action, dress, complexion even, from the rest of the men </s>
<s> I would make him the freshest and airiest sailor that ever was seen; and through him I can distinctly see my way out of "the Black Country" into clearer air </s>
<s> (I speak as one of the audience, mind.) I should like something of this contrast to be expressed in the dialogue between the sailor and Jew, in the second scene of the second act </s>
<s> Again, I feel Widdicomb's part (which is charming, and ought to make the whole house cry) most agreeable and welcome, much better than any amount in such a story, of mere comicality </s>
<s> It is unnecessary to say that the play is done with a master's hand </s>
<s> Its closeness and movement are quite surprising </s>
<s> Its construction is admirable </s>
<s> I have the strongest belief in its making a great success </s>
<s> But I must add this proviso: I never saw a play so dangerously depending in critical places on strict natural propriety in the manner and perfection in the shaping of the small parts </s>
<s> Those small parts cannot take the play up, but they can let it down </s>
<s> I would not leave a hair on the head of one of them to the chance of the first night, but I would see, to the minutest particular, the make-up of every one of them at a night rehearsal </s>
<s> Of course you are free to show this note to Mr Boucicault, and I suppose you will do so; let me throw out this suggestion to him and you </s>
<s> Might it not ease the way with the Lord Chamberlain's office, and still more with the audience, when there are Manchester champions in it, if instead of "Manchester" you used a fictitious name </s>
<s> When I did "Hard Times" I called the scene Coketown </s>
<s> Everybody knew what was meant, but every cotton-spinning town said it was the other cotton-spinning town </s>
<s> I shall be up on Saturday, and will come over about mid-day, unless you name any other time </s>
<s> Ever heartily </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Walter Thornbury] "ALL THE YEAR ROUND" OFFICE, _Saturday, Sept </s>
<s> 15th, 1866._ MY DEAR THORNBURY, Many thanks for your letter </s>
<s> In reference to your Shakespeare queries, I am not so much enamoured of the first and third subjects as I am of the Ariosto enquiry, which should be highly interesting </s>
<s> But if you have so got the matter in your mind, as that its execution would be incomplete and unsatisfactory to you unless you write all the three papers, then by all means write the three, and I will most gladly take them </s>
<s> For some years I have had so much pleasure in reading you, that I can honestly warrant myself as what actors call "a good audience" </s>
<s> The idea of old stories retold is decidedly a good one </s>
<s> I greatly like the notion of that series </s>
<s> Of course you know De Quincey's paper on the Ratcliffe Highway murderer </s>
<s> Do you know also the illustration (I have it at Gad's Hill), representing the horrible creature as his dead body lay on a cart, with a piece of wood for a pillow, and a stake lying by, ready to be driven through him </s>
<s> I don't _quite_ like the title, "The Social History of London" </s>
<s> I should better like some title to the effect, "The History of London's Social Changes in so many Years" </s>
<s> Such a title would promise more, and better express your intention </s>
<s> What do you think of taking for a first title, "London's Changes" </s>
<s> You could then add the second title, "Being a History," etc I don't at all desire to fix a limit to the series of old stories retold </s>
<s> I would state the general intention at the beginning of the first paper, and go on like Banquo's line </s>
<s> Don't let your London title remind people, by so much as the place of the word "civilisation," of Buckle </s>
<s> It seems a ridiculous caution, but the indolent part of the public (a large part!) on such points tumble into extraordinary mistakes </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>

<s> Concerning the green covers, I find the leaves to be budding--on unquestionable newspaper authority; but, upon my soul, I have no other knowledge of their being in embryo </s>

<s> He was the finest dog I ever saw, and between him and me there was a perfect understanding </s>
<s> But, to adopt the popular phrase, it was so very confidential that it "went no further" </s>

<s> 28th, 1866._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, I have received your letter with the utmost pleasure and we all send our most affectionate love to you, Mrs Macready, Katie, Johnny, and the boy of boys </s>
<s> All good Christmas and New Year greetings are to be understood as included </s>
<s> You will be interested in knowing that, encouraged by the success of summer cricket-matches, I got up a quantity of foot-races and rustic sports in my field here on the 26th last past: as I have never yet had a case of drunkenness, the landlord of The Falstaff had a drinking-booth on the ground </s>
<s> All the prizes I gave were in money, too </s>
<s> We had two thousand people here </s>
<s> Among the crowd were soldiers, navvies, and labourers of all kinds </s>
<s> Not a stake was pulled up, or a rope slackened, or one farthing's-worth of damage done </s>
<s> To every competitor (only) a printed bill of general rules was given, with the concluding words: "Mr Dickens puts every man upon his honour to assist in preserving order" </s>
<s> There was not a dispute all day, and they went away at sunset rending the air with cheers, and leaving every flag on a six hundred yards' course as neat as they found it when the gates were opened at ten in the morning </s>

<s> 1867 </s>
<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> As the London and provincial readings were to be resumed early in the year and continued until the end of March, Charles Dickens took no house in London this spring </s>
<s> He came to his office quarters at intervals, for the series in town; usually starting off again, on his country tour, the day after a London reading </s>
<s> From some passages in his letters to his daughter and sister-in-law during this country course, it will be seen that (though he made very light of the fact) the great exertion of the readings, combined with incessant railway travelling, was beginning to tell upon his health, and he was frequently "heavily beaten" after reading at his best to an enthusiastic audience in a large hall </s>
<s> During the short intervals between his journeys, he was as constantly and carefully at work upon the business of "All the Year Round" as if he had no other work on hand </s>
<s> A proof of this is given in a letter dated "5th February" </s>
<s> It is written to a young man (the son of a friend), who wrote a long novel when far too juvenile for such a task, and had submitted it to Charles Dickens for his opinion, with a view to publication </s>
<s> In the midst of his own hard and engrossing occupation he read the book, and the letter which he wrote on the subject needs no remark beyond this, that the young writer received the adverse criticism with the best possible sense, and has since, in his literary profession, profited by the advice so kindly given </s>
<s> At this time the proposals to Charles Dickens for reading in America, which had been perpetually renewed from the time of his first abandoning the idea, became so urgent and so tempting, that he found at last he must, at all events, give the subject his most serious consideration </s>
<s> He took counsel with his two most confidential friends and advisers, Mr John Forster and Mr W </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Wills </s>
<s> They were both, at first, strongly opposed to the undertaking, chiefly on the ground of the trial to his health and strength which it would involve </s>
<s> But they could not deny the counterbalancing advantages </s>
<s> And, after much deliberation, it was resolved that Mr George Dolby should be sent out by the Messrs </s>
<s> Chappell, to take an impression, on the spot, as to the feeling of the United States about the Readings </s>
<s> His report as to the undoubted enthusiasm and urgency on the other side of the Atlantic it was impossible to resist </s>
<s> Even his friends withdrew their opposition (though still with misgivings as to the effect upon his health, which were but too well founded!), and on the 30th September he telegraphed "Yes" to America </s>
<s> The "Alfred" alluded to in a letter from Glasgow was Charles Dickens's fourth son, Alfred Tennyson, who had gone to Australia two years previously </s>
<s> We give, in April, the last letter to one of the friends for whom Charles Dickens had always a most tender love--Mr Stanfield </s>
<s> He was then in failing health, and in May he died </s>
<s> Another death which affected him very deeply happened this summer </s>
<s> Miss Marguerite Power died in July </s>
<s> She had long been very ill, but, until it became impossible for her to travel, she was a frequent and beloved guest at Gad's Hill </s>
<s> The Mrs Henderson to whom he writes was Miss Power's youngest sister </s>
<s> Before he started for America it was proposed to wish him God-speed by giving him a public dinner at the Freemasons' Hall </s>
<s> The proposal was most warmly and fully responded to </s>
<s> His zealous friend, Mr Charles Kent, willingly undertook the whole work of arrangement of this banquet </s>
<s> It took place on the 2nd November, and Lord Lytton presided </s>
<s> On the 8th he left London for Liverpool, accompanied by his daughters, his sister-in-law, his eldest son, Mr Arthur Chappell, Mr Charles Collins, Mr Wilkie Collins, Mr Kent, and Mr Wills </s>
<s> The next morning the whole party took a final leave of Charles Dickens on board the _Cuba_, which sailed that day </s>
<s> We give a letter which he wrote to Mr J </s>
<s> L </s>
<s> Toole on the morning of the dinner, thanking him for a parting gift and an earnest letter </s>
<s> That excellent comedian was one of his most appreciative admirers, and, in return, he had for Mr Toole the greatest admiration and respect </s>
<s> The Christmas number for this year, "No Thoroughfare," was written by Charles Dickens and Mr Wilkie Collins </s>
<s> It was dramatised by Mr Collins chiefly </s>
<s> But, in the midst of all the work of preparation for departure, Charles Dickens gave minute attention to as much of the play as could be completed before he left England </s>
<s> It was produced, after Christmas, at the Adelphi Theatre, where M </s>
<s> Fechter was then acting, under the management of Mr Benjamin Webster </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _New Year's Day, 1867._ MY DEAR CERJAT, Thoroughly determined to be beforehand with "the middle of next summer," your penitent friend and remorseful correspondent thus addresses you </s>
<s> The big dog, on a day last autumn, having seized a little girl (sister to one of the servants) whom he knew, and was bound to respect, was flogged by his master, and then sentenced to be shot at seven next morning </s>
<s> He went out very cheerfully with the half-dozen men told off for the purpose, evidently thinking that they were going to be the death of somebody unknown </s>
<s> But observing in the procession an empty wheelbarrow and a double-barrelled gun, he became meditative, and fixed the bearer of the gun with his eyes </s>
<s> A stone deftly thrown across him by the village blackguard (chief mourner) caused him to look round for an instant, and he then fell dead, shot through the heart </s>
<s> Two posthumous children are at this moment rolling on the lawn; one will evidently inherit his ferocity, and will probably inherit the gun </s>
<s> The pheasant was a little ailing towards Christmas Day, and was found dead under some ivy in his cage, with his head under his wing, on the morning of the twenty-seventh of December, one thousand eight hundred and sixty-six </s>
<s> I, proprietor of the remains of the two deceased, am working hard, getting up "Barbox" and "The Boy at Mugby," with which I begin a new series of readings in London on the fifteenth </s>
<s> Next morning I believe I start into the country </s>
<s> When I read, I _don't_ write </s>
<s> I only edit, and have the proof-sheets sent me for the purpose </s>
<s> Here are your questions answered </s>
<s> As to the Reform question, it should have been, and could have been, perfectly known to any honest man in England that the more intelligent part of the great masses were deeply dissatisfied with the state of representation, but were in a very moderate and patient condition, awaiting the better intellectual cultivation of numbers of their fellows </s>
<s> The old insolent resource of assailing them and making the most audaciously wicked statements that they are politically indifferent, has borne the inevitable fruit </s>
<s> The perpetual taunt, "Where are they" </s>
<s> has called them out with the answer: "Well then, if you _must_ know, here we are" </s>
<s> The intolerable injustice of vituperating the bribed to an assembly of bribers, has goaded their sense of justice beyond endurance </s>
<s> And now, what they would have taken they won't take, and whatever they are steadily bent upon having they will get </s>
<s> Rely upon it, this is the real state of the case </s>
<s> As to your friend "Punch," you will find him begin to turn at the very selfsame instant when the new game shall manifestly become the losing one </s>
<s> You may notice his shoes pinching him a little already </s>
<s> My dear fellow, I have no more power to stop that mutilation of my books than you have </s>
<s> It is as certain as that every inventor of anything designed for the public good, and offered to the English Government, becomes _ipso facto_ a criminal, to have his heart broken on the circumlocutional wheel </s>
<s> It is as certain as that the whole Crimean story will be retold, whenever this country again goes to war </s>
<s> And to tell the truth, I have such a very small opinion of what the great genteel have done for us, that I am very philosophical indeed concerning what the great vulgar may do, having a decided opinion that they can't do worse </s>
<s> This is the time of year when the theatres do best, there being still numbers of people who make it a sort of religion to see Christmas pantomimes </s>
<s> Having my annual houseful, I have, as yet, seen nothing </s>
<s> Fechter has neither pantomime nor burlesque, but is doing a new version of the old "Trente Ans de la Vie d'un Joueur" </s>
<s> I am afraid he will not find his account in it </s>
<s> On the whole, the theatres, except in the articles of scenery and pictorial effect, are poor enough </s>
<s> But in some of the smaller houses there are actors who, if there were any dramatic head-quarters as a school, might become very good </s>
<s> The most hopeless feature is, that they have the smallest possible idea of an effective and harmonious whole, each "going in" for himself or herself </s>
<s> The music-halls attract an immense public, and don't refine the general taste </s>
<s> But such things as they do are well done of their kind, and always briskly and punctually </s>
<s> The American yacht race is the last sensation </s>
<s> I hope the general interest felt in it on this side will have a wholesome interest on that </s>
<s> It will be a woeful day when John and Jonathan throw their caps into the ring </s>
<s> The French Emperor is indubitably in a dangerous state </s>
<s> His Parisian popularity wanes, and his army are discontented with him </s>
<s> I hear on high authority that his secret police are always making discoveries that render him desperately uneasy </s>
<s> You know how we have been swindling in these parts </s>
<s> But perhaps you don't know that Mr ----, the "eminent" contractor, before he fell into difficulties settled _one million of money_ on his wife </s>
<s> Such a good and devoted husband </s>
<s> My daughter Katie has been very ill of nervous fever </s>
<s> On the 27th of December she was in a condition to be brought down here (old high road and post-horses), and has been steadily getting better ever since </s>
<s> Her husband is here too, and is on the whole as well as he ever is or ever will be, I fear </s>
<s> We played forfeit-games here, last night, and then pool </s>
<s> For a billiard-room has been added to the house since you were here </s>
<s> Come and play a match with me </s>
<s> Always affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] ADELPHI HOTEL, LIVERPOOL, _Monday, Jan </s>
<s> 21st, 1867._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, First I send you my most affectionate wishes for many, many happy returns of your birthday </s>

<s> We have been constantly talking of the terrible Regent's Park accident </s>
<s> I hope and believe that nearly the worst of it is now known </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] CHESTER, _Tuesday, Jan </s>
<s> 22nd, 1867._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, We came over here from Liverpool at eleven this forenoon </s>
<s> There was a heavy swell in the Mersey breaking over the boat; the cold was nipping, and all the roads we saw as we came along were wretched </s>

<s> This seems to be a very nice hotel, but it is an extraordinarily cold one </s>

<s> With amazing perversity the local agent said to Dolby: "They hoped that Mr Dickens _might_ have given them 'The Boy at Mugby'." Barton, the gasman who succeeded the man who sprained his leg, sprained _his_ leg yesterday! </s>
<s> And that, not at his work, but in running downstairs at the hotel </s>
<s> However, he has hobbled through it so far, and I hope will hobble on, for he knows his work </s>
<s> I have seldom seen a place look more hopelessly frozen up than this place does </s>
<s> The hall is like a Methodist chapel in low spirits, and with a cold in its head </s>
<s> A few blue people shiver at the corners of the streets </s>
<s> And this house, which is outside the town, looks like an ornament on an immense twelfth cake baked for 1847 </s>
<s> I am now going to the fire to try to warm myself, but have not the least expectation of succeeding </s>
<s> The sitting-room has two large windows in it, down to the ground and facing due east </s>
<s> The adjoining bedroom (mine) has also two large windows in it, down to the ground and facing due east </s>
<s> The very large doors are opposite the large windows, and I feel as if I were something to eat in a pantry </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] HEN AND CHICKENS, BIRMINGHAM, _Thursday, Jan </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Anonymous.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 5th, 1867._ DEAR SIR, I have looked at the larger half of the first volume of your novel, and have pursued the more difficult points of the story through the other two volumes </s>
<s> You will, of course, receive my opinion as that of an individual writer and student of art, who by no means claims to be infallible </s>
<s> I think you are too ambitious, and that you have not sufficient knowledge of life or character to venture on so comprehensive an attempt </s>
<s> Evidences of inexperience in every way, and of your power being far below the situations that you imagine, present themselves to me in almost every page I have read </s>
<s> It would greatly surprise me if you found a publisher for this story, on trying your fortune in that line, or derived anything from it but weariness and bitterness of spirit </s>
<s> On the evidence thus put before me, I cannot even entirely satisfy myself that you have the faculty of authorship latent within you </s>
<s> If you have not, and yet pursue a vocation towards which you have no call, you cannot choose but be a wretched man </s>
<s> Let me counsel you to have the patience to form yourself carefully, and the courage to renounce the endeavour if you cannot establish your case on a very much smaller scale </s>
<s> You see around you every day, how many outlets there are for short pieces of fiction in all kinds </s>
<s> Try if you can achieve any success within these modest limits (I have practised in my time what I preach to you), and in the meantime put your three volumes away </s>
<s> Faithfully yours </s>
<s> P.S.--Your MS </s>
<s> will be returned separately from this office </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] LIVERPOOL, _Friday, Feb </s>
<s> 15th, 1867._ My short report of myself is that we had an enormous turn-away last night, and do not doubt about having a cram to-night </s>
<s> The day has been very fine, and I have turned it to the wholesomest account by walking on the sands at New Brighton all the morning </s>
<s> I am not quite right, but believe it to be an effect of the railway shaking </s>
<s> There is no doubt of the fact that, after the Staplehurst experience, it tells more and more, instead of (as one might have expected) less and less </s>
<s> The charming room here greatly lessens the fatigue of this fatiguing week </s>
<s> I read last night with no more exertion than if I had been at Gad's, and yet to eleven hundred people, and with astonishing effect </s>
<s> It is "Copperfield" to-night, and Liverpool is the "Copperfield" stronghold </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] GLASGOW, _Sunday, Feb </s>
<s> 17th, 1867._ We arrived here this morning at our time to the moment, five minutes past ten </s>
<s> We turned away great numbers on both nights at Liverpool; and Manchester last night was a splendid spectacle </s>
<s> They cheered to that extent after it was over, that I was obliged to huddle on my clothes (for I was undressing to prepare for the journey), and go back again </s>
<s> After so heavy a week, it _was_ rather stiff to start on this long journey at a quarter to two in the morning; but I got more sleep than I ever got in a railway-carriage before, and it really was not tedious </s>
<s> The travelling was admirable, and a wonderful contrast to my friend the Midland </s>
<s> I am not by any means knocked up, though I have, as I had in the last series of readings, a curious feeling of soreness all round the body, which I suppose to arise from the great exertion of voice </s>
<s> It is a mercy that we were not both made really ill at Liverpool </s>
<s> On Friday morning I was taken so faint and sick, that I was obliged to leave the table </s>
<s> On the same afternoon the same thing happened to Dolby </s>
<s> We then found that a part of the hotel close to us was dismantled for painting, and that they were at that moment painting a green passage leading to our rooms, with a most horrible mixture of white lead and arsenic </s>
<s> On pursuing the enquiry, I found that the four lady book-keepers in the bar were all suffering from the poison </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BRIDGE OF ALLAN, _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 19th, 1867._ I was very glad to get your letter before leaving Glasgow this morning </s>
