<s> I may say, in the best force </s>
<s> The quiet of this little place is sure to do me good </s>
<s> The little inn in which we are established seems a capital house of the best country sort </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] GLASGOW, _Thursday, Feb </s>
<s> 21st, 1867._ After two days' rest at the Bridge of Allan I am in renewed force, and have nothing to complain of but inability to sleep </s>
<s> I have been in excellent air all day since Tuesday at noon, and made an interesting walk to Stirling yesterday, and saw its lions, and (strange to relate) was not bored by them </s>
<s> Indeed, they left me so fresh that I knocked at the gate of the prison, presented myself to the governor, and took Dolby over the jail, to his unspeakable interest </s>
<s> We then walked back again to our excellent country inn </s>
<s> Enclosed is a letter from Alfred, which you and your aunt will be interested in reading, and which I meant to send you sooner but forgot it </s>
<s> Wonderful as it is to mention, the sun shines here to-day </s>
<s> But to counterbalance that phenomenon I am in close hiding from ----, who has christened his infant son in my name, and, consequently, haunts the building </s>
<s> He and Dolby have already nearly come into collision, in consequence of the latter being always under the dominion of the one idea that he is bound to knock everybody down who asks for me </s>
<s> * * * * * The "Jewish lady," wishing to mark her "appreciation of Mr Dickens's nobility of character," presented him with a copy of Benisch's Hebrew and English Bible, with this inscription: "Presented to Charles Dickens, in grateful and admiring recognition of his having exercised the noblest quality man can possess--that of atoning for an injury as soon as conscious of having inflicted it" </s>
<s> The acknowledgment of the gift is the following letter: [Sidenote: Jewish Lady.] BRADFORD, YORKSHIRE, _Friday, March 1st, 1867._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> ----, I am working through a series of readings, widely dispersed through England, Scotland, and Ireland, and am so constantly occupied that it is very difficult for me to write letters </s>
<s> I have received your highly esteemed note (forwarded from my home in Kent), and should have replied to it sooner but that I had a hope of being able to get home and see your present first </s>
<s> As I have not been able to do so, however, and am hardly likely to do so for two months to come, I delay no longer </s>
<s> It is safely awaiting me on my own desk in my own quiet room </s>
<s> I cannot thank you for it too cordially, and cannot too earnestly assure you that I shall always prize it highly </s>
<s> The terms in which you send me that mark of your remembrance are more gratifying to me than I can possibly express to you; for they assure me that there is nothing but goodwill left between you and me and a people for whom I have a real regard, and to whom I would not wilfully have given an offence or done an injustice for any worldly consideration </s>
<s> Believe me, very faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] NEWCASTLE-ON-TYNE, _Wednesday, March 6th, 1867._ The readings have made an immense effect in this place, and it is remarkable that although the people are individually rough, collectively they are an unusually tender and sympathetic audience; while their comic perception is quite up to the high London standard </s>
<s> The atmosphere is so very heavy that yesterday we escaped to Tynemouth for a two hours' sea walk </s>
<s> There was a high north wind blowing and a magnificent sea running </s>
<s> Large vessels were being towed in and out over the stormy bar, with prodigious waves breaking on it; and spanning the restless uproar of the waters was a quiet rainbow of transcendent beauty </s>
<s> The scene was quite wonderful </s>
<s> We were in the full enjoyment of it when a heavy sea caught us, knocked us over, and in a moment drenched us, and filled even our pockets </s>
<s> We had nothing for it but to shake ourselves together (like Doctor Marigold) and dry ourselves as well as we could by hard walking in the wind and sunshine </s>
<s> But we were wet through for all that when we came back here to dinner after half an hour's railway ride </s>
<s> I am wonderfully well, and quite fresh and strong </s>
<s> Have had to doctor Dolby for a bad cold; have not caught it (yet), and have set him on his legs again </s>
<s> Scott is striking the tents and loading the baggages, so I must deliver up my writing-desk </s>
<s> We meet, please God, on Tuesday </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] SHELBOURNE HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Friday, March 15th, 1867._ We made our journey through an incessant snowstorm on Wednesday night; at last got snowed up among the Welsh mountains in a tremendous storm of wind, came to a stop, and had to dig the engine out </s>
<s> We went to bed at Holyhead at six in the morning of Thursday, and got aboard the packet at two yesterday afternoon </s>
<s> It blew hard, but as the wind was right astern, we only rolled and did not pitch much </s>
<s> As I walked about on the bridge all the four hours, and had cold salt beef and biscuit there and brandy-and-water, you will infer that my Channel training has not worn out </s>
<s> Our "business" here is _very bad_, though at Belfast it is enormous </s>
<s> There is no doubt that great alarm prevails here </s>
<s> This hotel is constantly filling and emptying as families leave the country, and set in a current to the steamers </s>
<s> There is apprehension of some disturbance between to-morrow night and Monday night (both inclusive), and I learn this morning that all the drinking-shops are to be closed from to-night until Tuesday </s>
<s> It is rumoured here that the Liverpool people are very uneasy about some apprehended disturbance there at the same time </s>
<s> Very likely you will know more about this than I do, and very likely it may be nothing </s>
<s> There is no doubt whatever that alarm prevails, and the manager of this hotel, an intelligent German, is very gloomy on the subject </s>
<s> On the other hand, there is feasting going on, and I have been asked to dinner-parties by divers civil and military authorities </s>
<s> Don't _you_ be uneasy, I say once again </s>
<s> You may be absolutely certain that there is no cause for it </s>
<s> We are splendidly housed here, and in great comfort </s>
<s> Love to Charley and Katey </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] SHELBOURNE HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Saturday, March 16th, 1867._ I daresay you know already that I held many councils in London about coming to Ireland at all, and was much against it </s>
<s> Everything looked as bad here as need be, but we did very well last night after all </s>
<s> There is considerable alarm here beyond all question, and great depression in all kinds of trade and commerce </s>
<s> To-morrow being St </s>
<s> Patrick's Day, there are apprehensions of some disturbance, and croakers predict that it will come off between to-night and Monday night </s>
<s> Of course there are preparations on all sides, and large musters of soldiers and police, though they are kept carefully out of sight </s>
<s> One would not suppose, walking about the streets, that any disturbance was impending; and yet there is no doubt that the materials of one lie smouldering up and down the city and all over the country </s>
<s> [I have a letter from Mrs Bernal Osborne this morning, describing the fortified way in which she is living in her own house in the County Tipperary.] You may be quite sure that your venerable parent will take good care of himself </s>
<s> If any riot were to break out, I should immediately stop the readings here </s>
<s> Should all remain quiet, I begin to think they will be satisfactorily remunerative after all </s>
<s> At Belfast, we shall have an enormous house </s>
<s> I read "Copperfield" and "Bob" here on Monday; "Marigold" and "Trial" at Belfast, on Wednesday; and "Carol" and "Trial" here, on Friday </s>
<s> This is all my news, except that I am in perfect force </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] SHELBOURNE HOTEL, DUBLIN, _Sunday, March 17th, 1867._ Everything remains in appearance perfectly quiet here </s>
<s> The streets are gay all day, now that the weather is improved, and singularly quiet and deserted at night </s>
<s> But the whole place is secretly girt in with a military force </s>
<s> To-morrow night is supposed to be a critical time; but in view of the enormous preparations, I should say that the chances are at least one hundred to one against any disturbance </s>
<s> I cannot make sure whether I wrote to you yesterday, and told you that we had done very well at the first reading after all, even in money </s>
<s> The reception was prodigious, and the readings are the town talk </s>
<s> But I rather think I did actually write this to you </s>
<s> My doubt on the subject arises from my having deliberated about writing on a Saturday </s>
<s> The most curious, and for facilities of mere destruction, such as firing houses in different quarters, the most dangerous piece of intelligence imparted to me on authority is, that the Dublin domestic men-servants as a class are all Fenians </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BELFAST, _Wednesday, March 20th, 1867._ The post goes out at twelve, and I have only time to report myself </s>
<s> The snow not lying between this and Dublin, we got here yesterday to our time, after a cold but pleasant journey </s>
<s> Fitzgerald came on with us </s>
<s> I had a really charming letter from Mrs Fitzgerald, asking me to stay there </s>
<s> She must be a perfectly unaffected and genuine lady </s>
<s> There are kind messages to you and Mary in it </s>
<s> I have sent it on to Mary, who will probably in her turn show it to you </s>
<s> We had a wonderful crowd at Dublin on Monday, and the greatest appreciation possible </s>
<s> We have a good let, in a large hall, here to-night </s>
<s> But I am perfectly convinced that the worst part of the Fenian business is to come yet </s>
<s> All about the Fitzgeralds and everything else when we meet </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BELFAST, _Thursday, March 21st, 1867._ In spite of public affairs and dismal weather, we are doing wonders in Ireland </s>
<s> That the conspiracy is a far larger and more important one than would seem from what it has done yet, there is no doubt </s>
<s> I have had a good deal of talk with a certain colonel, whose duty it has been to investigate it, day and night, since last September </s>
<s> That it will give a world of trouble, and cost a world of money, I take to be (after what I have thus learned) beyond all question </s>
<s> One regiment has been found to contain five hundred Fenian soldiers every man of whom was sworn in the barrack-yard </s>
<s> How information is swiftly and secretly conveyed all over the country, the Government with all its means and money cannot discover; but every hour it is found that instructions, warnings, and other messages are circulated from end to end of Ireland </s>
<s> It is a very serious business indeed </s>
<s> I have just time to send this off, and to report myself quite well except for a slight cold </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] NORWICH, _Friday, March 29th, 1867._ The reception at Cambridge last night was something to be proud of in such a place </s>
<s> The colleges mustered in full force from the biggest guns to the smallest, and went far beyond even Manchester in the roars of welcome and the rounds of cheers </s>
<s> All through the readings, the whole of the assembly, old men as well as young, and women as well as men, took everything with a heartiness of enjoyment not to be described </s>
<s> The place was crammed, and the success the most brilliant I have ever seen </s>
<s> What we are doing in this sleepy old place I don't know, but I have no doubt it is mild enough </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Walter Thornbury] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Monday, April 1st, 1867._ MY DEAR THORNBURY, I am very doubtful indeed about "Vaux," and have kept it out of the number in consequence </s>
<s> The mere details of such a rascal's proceedings, whether recorded by himself or set down by the Reverend Ordinary, are not wholesome for a large audience, and are scarcely justifiable (I think) as claiming to be a piece of literature </s>
<s> I can understand Barrington to be a good subject, as involving the representation of a period, a style of manners, an order of dress, certain habits of street life, assembly-room life, and coffee-room life, etc; but there is a very broad distinction between this and mere Newgate Calendar </s>
<s> The latter would assuredly damage your book, and be protested against to me </s>
<s> I have a conviction of it, founded on constant observation and experience here </s>
<s> Your kind invitation is extremely welcome and acceptable to me, but I am sorry to add that I must not go a-visiting </s>
<s> For this reason: So incessantly have I been "reading," that I have not once been at home at Gad's Hill since last January, and am little likely to get there before the middle of May </s>
<s> Judge how the master's eye must be kept on the place when it does at length get a look at it after so long an absence </s>
<s> I hope you will descry in this a reason for coming to me again, instead of my coming to you </s>
<s> The extinct prize-fighters, as a body, I take to be a good subject, for much the same reason as George Barrington </s>
<s> Their patrons were a class of men now extinct too, and the whole ring of those days (not to mention Jackson's rooms in Bond Street) is a piece of social history </s>
<s> Now Vaux is not, nor is he even a phenomenon among thieves </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Clarkson Stanfield, R.A.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, _Thursday, April 18th, 1867._ MY DEAR STANNY, The time of year reminds me how the months have gone, since I last heard from you through Mrs Stanfield </s>
<s> I hope you have not thought me unmindful of you in the meanwhile </s>
<s> I have been almost constantly travelling and reading </s>
<s> England, Ireland, and Scotland have laid hold of me by turns, and I have had no rest </s>
<s> As soon as I had finished this kind of work last year, I had to fall to work upon "All the Year Round" and the Christmas number </s>
<s> I was no sooner quit of that task, and the Christmas season was but run out to its last day, when I was tempted into another course of fifty readings that are not yet over </s>
<s> I am here now for two days, and have not seen the place since Twelfth Night </s>
<s> When a reading in London has been done, I have been brought up for it from some great distance, and have next morning been carried back again </s>
<s> But the fifty will be "paid out" (as we say at sea) by the middle of May, and then I hope to see you </s>
<s> Reading at Cheltenham the other day, I saw Macready, who sent his love to you </s>
<s> His face was much more massive and as it used to be, than when I saw him previous to his illness </s>
<s> His wife takes admirable care of him, and is on the happiest terms with his daughter Katie </s>
<s> His boy by the second marriage is a jolly little fellow, and leads a far easier life than the children you and I remember, who used to come in at dessert and have each a biscuit and a glass of water, in which last refreshment I was always convinced that they drank, with the gloomiest malignity, "Destruction to the gormandising grown-up company" </s>
<s> I hope to look up your latest triumphs on the day of the Academy dinner </s>
<s> Of course as yet I have had no opportunity of even hearing of what anyone has done </s>
<s> I have been (in a general way) snowed up for four months </s>
<s> The locomotive with which I was going to Ireland was dug out of the snow at midnight, in Wales </s>
<s> Both passages across were made in a furious snowstorm </s>
<s> The snow lay ankle-deep in Dublin, and froze hard at Belfast </s>
<s> In Scotland it slanted before a perpetual east wind </s>
<s> In Yorkshire, it derived novelty from thunder and lightning </s>
<s> Whirlwinds everywhere I don't mention </s>
<s> God bless you and yours </s>
<s> If I look like some weather-beaten pilot when we meet, don't be surprised </s>
<s> Any mahogany-faced stranger who holds out his hand to you will probably turn out, on inspection, to be the old original Dick </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Stanny, your faithful and affectionate </s>
<s> P.S.--I wish you could have been with me (of course in a snowstorm) one day on the pier at Tynemouth </s>
<s> There was a very heavy sea running, and a perfect fleet of screw merchantmen were plunging in and out on the turn of the tide at high-water </s>
<s> Suddenly there came a golden horizon, and a most glorious rainbow burst out, arching one large ship, as if she were sailing direct for heaven </s>
<s> I was so enchanted by the scene, that I became oblivious of a few thousand tons of water coming on in an enormous roller, and was knocked down and beaten by its spray when it broke, and so completely wetted through and through, that the very pockets in my pocket-book were full of sea </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr George Stanfield.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Sunday, May 19th, 1867._ ON THE DEATH OF HIS FATHER </s>
<s> MY DEAR GEORGE, When I came up to the house this afternoon and saw what had happened, I had not the courage to ring, though I had thought I was fully prepared by what I heard when I called yesterday </s>
<s> No one of your father's friends can ever have loved him more dearly than I always did, or can have better known the worth of his noble character </s>
<s> It is idle to suppose that I can do anything for you; and yet I cannot help saying that I am staying here for some days, and that if I could, it would be a much greater relief to me than it could be a service to you </s>
<s> Your poor mother has been constantly in my thoughts since I saw the quiet bravery with which she preserved her composure </s>
<s> The beauty of her ministration sank into my heart when I saw him for the last time on earth </s>
<s> May God be with her, and with you all, in your great loss </s>
<s> Affectionately yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Wills.] _Thursday, June 6th, 1867._ MY DEAR WILLS, I cannot tell you how warmly I feel your letter, or how deeply I appreciate the affection and regard in which it originates </s>
<s> I thank you for it with all my heart </s>
<s> You will not suppose that I make light of any of your misgivings if I present the other side of the question </s>
<s> Every objection that you make strongly impresses me, and will be revolved in my mind again and again </s>
<s> When I went to America in '42, I was so much younger, but (I think) very much weaker too </s>
<s> I had had a painful surgical operation performed shortly before going out, and had had the labour from week to week of "Master Humphrey's Clock" </s>
<s> My life in the States was a life of continual speech-making (quite as laborious as reading), and I was less patient and more irritable then than I am now </s>
<s> My idea of a course of readings in America is, that it would involve far less travelling than you suppose, that the large first-class rooms would absorb the whole course, and that the receipts would be very much larger than your estimate, unless the demand for the readings is ENORMOUSLY EXAGGERATED ON ALL HANDS </s>
<s> There is considerable reason for this view of the case </s>
<s> And I can hardly think that all the speculators who beset, and all the private correspondents who urge me, are in a conspiracy or under a common delusion </s>
<s> * * * * * I shall never rest much while my faculties last, and (if I know myself) have a certain something in me that would still be active in rusting and corroding me, if I flattered myself that I was in repose </s>
<s> On the other hand, I think that my habit of easy self-abstraction and withdrawal into fancies has always refreshed and strengthened me in short intervals wonderfully </s>
<s> I always seem to myself to have rested far more than I have worked; and I do really believe that I have some exceptional faculty of accumulating young feelings in short pauses, which obliterates a quantity of wear and tear </s>
<s> My worldly circumstances (such a large family considered) are very good </s>
<s> I don't want money </s>
<s> All my possessions are free and in the best order </s>
<s> Still, at fifty-five or fifty-six, the likelihood of making a very great addition to one's capital in half a year is an immense consideration... </s>
<s> I repeat the phrase, because there should be something large to set against the objections </s>
<s> I dine with Forster to-day, to talk it over </s>
<s> I have no doubt he will urge most of your objections and particularly the last, though American friends and correspondents he has, have undoubtedly staggered him more than I ever knew him to be staggered on the money question </s>
<s> Be assured that no one can present any argument to me which will weigh more heartily with me than your kind words, and that whatever comes of my present state of abeyance, I shall never forget your letter or cease to be grateful for it </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Wills, faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Wills.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Sunday, June 13th, 1867._ MY DEAR WILLS, I have read the first three numbers of Wilkie's story this morning, and have gone minutely through the plot of the rest to the last line </s>
<s> It gives a series of "narratives," but it is a very curious story, wild, and yet domestic, with excellent character in it, and great mystery </s>
<s> It is prepared with extraordinary care, and has every chance of being a hit </s>
<s> It is in many respects much better than anything he has done </s>
<s> The question is, how shall we fill up the blank between Mabel's progress and Wilkie </s>
<s> What do you think of proposing to Fitzgerald to do a story three months long </s>
<s> I daresay he has some unfinished or projected something by him </s>
<s> I have an impression that it was not Silvester who tried Eliza Fenning, but Knowles </s>
<s> One can hardly suppose Thornbury to make such a mistake, but I wish you would look into the Annual Register </s>
<s> I have added a final paragraph about the unfairness of the judge, whoever he was </s>
<s> I distinctly recollect to have read of his "putting down" of Eliza Fenning's father when the old man made some miserable suggestion in his daughter's behalf (this is not noticed by Thornbury), and he also stopped some suggestion that a knife thrust into a loaf adulterated with alum would present the appearance that these knives presented </s>
<s> But I may have got both these points from looking up some pamphlets in Upcott's collection which I once had </s>
<s> Your account of your journey reminds me of one of the latest American stories, how a traveller by stage-coach said to the driver: "Did you ever see a snail, sir" </s>
<s> "Yes, sir" </s>
<s> "Where did you meet him, sir" </s>
<s> "I _didn't_ meet him, sir" </s>
<s> "Wa'al, sir, I think you did, if you'll excuse me, for I'm damned if you ever overtook him" </s>
<s> Ever faithfully </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Henderson.] GAD'S HILL, _Thursday, July 4th, 1867._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> HENDERSON, I was more shocked than surprised by the receipt of your mother's announcement of our poor dear Marguerite's death </s>
<s> When I heard of the consultation, and recalled what had preceded it and what I have seen here, my hopes were very slight </s>
<s> Your letter did not reach me until last night, and thus I could not avoid remaining here to-day, to keep an American appointment of unusual importance </s>
<s> You and your mother both know, I think, that I had a great affection for Marguerite, that we had many dear remembrances together, and that her self-reliance and composed perseverance had awakened my highest admiration in later times </s>
<s> No one could have stood by her grave to-day with a better knowledge of all that was great and good in her than I have, or with a more loving remembrance of her through all her phases since she first came to London a pretty timid girl </s>
<s> I do not trouble your mother by writing to her separately </s>
<s> It is a sad, sad task to write at all </s>
<s> God help us </s>
<s> Faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Percy Fitzgerald.] GAD'S HILL, _July 21st, 1867._ MY DEAR FITZGERALD, I am heartily glad to get your letter, and shall be thoroughly well pleased to study you again in the pages of A </s>
<s> Y </s>
<s> R </s>
<s> I have settled nothing yet about America, but am going to send Dolby out on the 3rd of next month to survey the land, and come back with a report on some heads whereon I require accurate information </s>
<s> Proposals (both from American and English speculators) of a very tempting nature have been repeatedly made to me; but I cannot endure the thought of binding myself to give so many readings there whether I like it or no; and if I go at all, am bent on going with Dolby single-handed </s>
<s> I have been doing two things for America; one, the little story to which you refer; the other, four little papers for a child's magazine </s>
<s> I like them both, and think the latter a queer combination of a child's mind with a grown-up joke </s>

<s> You shall have the proof to read, with the greatest pleasure </s>

<s> I will, as I have it here, send it under another cover </s>
<s> When you return it, you shall have the short story </s>
<s> Believe me, always heartily yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Percy Fitzgerald.] EXTRACT </s>
<s> _July 28th, 1867._ I am glad you like the children, and particularly glad you like the pirate </s>
<s> I remember very well when I had a general idea of occupying that place in history at the same age </s>
<s> But I loved more desperately than Boldheart </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] ADELPHI HOTEL, LIVERPOOL, _Friday Night, Aug </s>
<s> 2nd, 1867._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, I cannot get a boot on--wear a slipper on my left foot, and consequently am here under difficulties </s>
<s> My foot is occasionally painful, but not very </s>
<s> I don't think it worth while consulting anybody about it as yet </s>
<s> I make out so many reasons against supposing it to be gouty, that I really do not think it is </s>
<s> Dolby begs me to send all manner of apologetic messages for his going to America </s>
<s> He is very cheerful and hopeful, but evidently feels the separation from his wife and child very much </s>
<s> His sister[17] was at Euston Square this morning, looking very well </s>
<s> Sainton too, very light and jovial </s>
<s> With the view of keeping myself and my foot quiet, I think I will not come to Gad's Hill until Monday </s>
<s> If I don't appear before, send basket to Gravesend to meet me, leaving town by the 12.10 on Monday </s>
<s> This is important, as I couldn't walk a quarter of a mile to-night for five hundred pounds </s>
<s> Love to all at Gad's </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Wills.] GAD'S HILL, _Monday, Sept </s>
<s> 2nd, 1867._ MY DEAR WILLS, Like you, I was shocked when this new discovery burst upon me on Friday, though, unlike you, I never could believe in ----, solely (I think) because, often as I have tried him, I never found him standing by my desk when I was writing a letter without trying to read it </s>
<s> I fear there is no doubt that since ----'s discharge, he (----) has stolen money at the readings </s>
<s> A case of an abstracted shilling seems to have been clearly brought home to him by Chappell's people, and they know very well what _that_ means </s>
<s> I supposed a very clear keeping off from Anne's husband (whom I recommended for employment to Chappell) to have been referable only to ----; but now I see how hopeless and unjust it would be to expect belief from him with two such cases within his knowledge </s>
<s> But don't let the thing spoil your holiday </s>
<s> If we try to do our duty by people we employ, by exacting their proper service from them on the one hand, and treating them with all possible consistency, gentleness, and consideration on the other, we know that we do right </s>
<s> Their doing wrong cannot change our doing right, and that should be enough for us </s>
<s> So I have given _my_ feathers a shake, and am all right again </s>
<s> Give _your_ feathers a shake, and take a cheery flutter into the air of Hertfordshire </s>
<s> Great reports from Dolby and also from Fields </s>
<s> But I keep myself quite calm, and hold my decision in abeyance until I shall have book, chapter, and verse before me </s>
<s> Dolby hoped he could leave Uncle Sam on the 11th of this month </s>
<s> Sydney has passed as a lieutenant, and appeared at home yesterday, all of a sudden, with the consequent golden garniture on his sleeve, which I, God forgive me, stared at without the least idea that it meant promotion </s>
<s> I am glad you see a certain unlikeness to anything in the American story </s>
<s> Upon myself it has made the strangest impression of reality and originality! </s>
<s> And I feel as if I had read something (by somebody else), which I should never get out of my mind!! </s>
<s> The main idea of the narrator's position towards the other people was the idea that I _had_ for my next novel in A </s>
<s> Y </s>
<s> R </s>
<s> But it is very curious that I did not in the least see how to begin his state of mind until I walked into Hoghton Towers one bright April day with Dolby </s>
<s> Faithfully ever </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr F </s>
<s> D </s>
<s> Finlay.] CONTRADICTING A NEWSPAPER REPORT OF HIS BEING IN A CRITICAL STATE OF HEALTH </s>
<s> GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, Sept </s>
<s> 3rd, 1867._ This is to certify that the undersigned victim of a periodical paragraph-disease, which usually breaks out once in every seven years (proceeding to England by the overland route to India and per Cunard line to America, where it strikes the base of the Rocky Mountains, and, rebounding to Europe, perishes on the steppes of Russia), is _not_ in a "critical state of health," and has _not_ consulted "eminent surgeons," and never was better in his life, and is _not_ recommended to proceed to the United States for "cessation from literary labour," and has not had so much as a headache for twenty years </s>
<s> CHARLES DICKENS </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> Charles Fechter.] "ALL THE YEAR ROUND" OFFICE, _Monday, Sept </s>
<s> 16th, 1867._ MY DEAR FECHTER, Going over the prompt-book carefully, I see one change in your part to which (on Lytton's behalf) I positively object, as I am quite certain he would not consent to it </s>
<s> It is highly injudicious besides, as striking out the best known line in the play </s>
<s> Turn to your part in Act III., the speech beginning Pauline, _by pride Angels have fallen ere thy time_: by pride---- You have made a passage farther on stand: _Then did I seek to rise Out of my mean estate </s>
<s> Thy bright image, etc_ I must stipulate for your restoring it thus: Then did I seek to rise Out of the prison of my mean estate; And, with such jewels as the exploring mind Brings from the caves of knowledge, buy my ransom From those twin jailers of the daring heart-- Low birth and iron fortune </s>
<s> Thy bright image, etc etc The last figure has been again and again quoted; is identified with the play; is fine in itself; and above all, I KNOW that Lytton would not let it go </s>
<s> In writing to him to-day, fully explaining the changes in detail, and saying that I disapprove of nothing else, I have told him that I notice this change and that I immediately let you know that it must not be made </s>
<s> (There will not be a man in the house from any newspaper who would not detect mutilations in that speech, moreover.) Ever </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] ABOARD THE "CUBA," QUEENSTOWN HARBOUR, _Sunday, Nov </s>
<s> 10th, 1867._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, We arrived here at seven this morning, and shall probably remain awaiting our mail, until four or five this afternoon </s>
<s> The weather in the passage here was delightful, and we had scarcely any motion beyond that of the screw </s>
<s> We are nearly but not quite full of passengers </s>
<s> At table I sit next the captain, on his right, on the outside of the table and close to the door </s>
<s> My little cabin is big enough for everything but getting up in and going to bed in </s>
<s> As it has a good window which I can leave open all night, and a door which I can set open too, it suits my chief requirements of it--plenty of air--admirably </s>
<s> On a writing-slab in it, which pulls out when wanted, I now write in a majestic manner </s>
<s> Many of the passengers are American, and I am already on the best terms with nearly all the ship </s>
<s> We began our voyage yesterday a very little while after you left us, which was a great relief </s>
<s> The wind is S.E </s>
<s> this morning, and if it would keep so we should go along nobly </s>
<s> My dearest love to your aunt, and also to Katie and all the rest </s>
<s> I am in very good health, thank God, and as well as possible </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] ABOARD THE "CUBA," FIVE DAYS OUT, _Wednesday, Nov </s>
<s> 13th, 1867._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, As I wrote to Mamie last, I now write to you, or mean to do it, if the motion of the ship will let me </s>
<s> We are very nearly halfway to-day </s>
<s> The weather was favourable for us until yesterday morning, when we got a head-wind which still stands by us </s>
<s> We have rolled and pitched, of course; but on the whole have been wonderfully well off </s>
<s> I have had headache and have felt faint once or twice, _but have not been sick at all_ </s>
<s> My spacious cabin is very noisy at night, as the most important working of the ship goes on outside my window and over my head; but it is very airy, and if the weather be bad and I can't open the window, I can open the door all night </s>
<s> If the weather be fine (as it is now), I can open both door and window, and write between them </s>
<s> Last night, I got a foot-bath under the dignified circumstances of sitting on a camp-stool in my cabin, and having the bath (and my feet) in the passage outside </s>
<s> The officers' quarters are close to me, and, as I know them all, I get reports of the weather and the way we are making when the watch is changed, and I am (as I usually am) lying awake </s>
<s> The motion of the screw is at its slightest vibration in my particular part of the ship </s>
<s> The silent captain, reported gruff, is a very good fellow and an honest fellow </s>
<s> Kelly has been ill all the time, and not of the slightest use, and is ill now </s>
<s> Scott always cheerful, and useful, and ready; a better servant for the kind of work there never can have been </s>
<s> Young Lowndes has been fearfully sick until mid-day yesterday </s>
<s> His cabin is pitch dark, and full of blackbeetles </s>
<s> He shares mine until nine o'clock at night, when Scott carries him off to bed </s>
<s> He also dines with me in my magnificent chamber </s>
<s> This passage in winter time cannot be said to be an enjoyable excursion, but I certainly am making it under the best circumstances </s>
<s> (I find Dolby to have been enormously popular on board, and to have known everybody and gone everywhere.) So much for my news, except that I have been constantly reading, and find that "Pierra" that Mrs Hogge sent me by Katie to be a very remarkable book, not only for its grim and horrible story, but for its suggestion of wheels within wheels, and sad human mysteries </s>
<s> Baker's second book not nearly so good as his first, but his first anticipated it </s>
<s> We hope to get to Halifax either on Sunday or Monday, and to Boston either on Tuesday or Wednesday </s>
<s> The glass is rising high to-day, and everybody on board is hopeful of an easterly wind </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] _Saturday, 16th._ Last Thursday afternoon a heavy gale of wind sprang up and blew hard until dark, when it seemed to lull </s>
<s> But it then came on again with great violence, and blew tremendously all night </s>
<s> The noise, and the rolling and plunging of the ship, were awful </s>
<s> Nobody on board could get any sleep, and numbers of passengers were rolled out of their berths </s>
<s> Having a side-board to mine to keep me in, like a baby, I lay still </s>
<s> But it was a dismal night indeed, and it was curious to see the change it had made in the faces of all the passengers yesterday </s>
<s> It cannot be denied that these winter crossings are very trying and startling; while the personal discomfort of not being able to wash, and the miseries of getting up and going to bed, with what small means there are all sliding, and sloping, and slopping about, are really in their way distressing </s>
<s> This forenoon we made Cape Race, and are now running along at full speed with the land beside us </s>
<s> Kelly still useless, and positively declining to show on deck </s>
<s> Scott, with an eight-day-old moustache, more super like than ever </s>
<s> My foot (I hope from walking on the boarded deck) in a very shy condition to-day, and rather painful </s>
<s> I shaved this morning for the first time since Liverpool; dodging at the glass, very much like Fechter's imitation of ---- </s>
<s> The white cat that came off with us in the tender a general favourite </s>
<s> She belongs to the daughter of a Southerner, returning with his wife and family from a two-years' tour in Europe </s>
<s> _Sunday, 17th._ At four o'clock this morning we got into bad weather again, and the state of things at breakfast-time was unutterably miserable </s>
<s> Nearly all the passengers in their berths--no possibility of standing on deck--sickness and groans--impracticable to pass a cup of tea from one pair of hands to another </s>
<s> It has slightly moderated since (between two and three in the afternoon I write), and the sun is shining, but the rolling of the ship surpasses all imagination or description </s>
<s> We expect to be at Halifax about an hour after midnight, and this letter shall be posted there, to make certain of catching the return mail on Wednesday </s>
<s> Boston is only thirty hours from Halifax </s>
<s> Best love to Mamie, and to Katie and Charley </s>
<s> I know you will report me and my love to Forster and Mrs Forster </s>
<s> I write with great difficulty, wedged up in a corner, and having my heels on the paper as often as the pen </s>
<s> Kelly worse than ever, and Scott better than ever </s>
<s> My desk and I have just arisen from the floor </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, _Thursday, Nov </s>
<s> 21st, 1867._ I arrived here on Tuesday night, after a very slow passage from Halifax against head-winds </s>
<s> All the tickets for the first four readings here (all yet announced) were sold immediately on their being issued </s>
<s> You know that I begin on the 2nd of December with "Carol" and "Trial" </s>
<s> Shall be heartily glad to begin to count the readings off </s>
<s> This is an immense hotel, with all manner of white marble public passages and public rooms </s>
<s> I live in a corner high up, and have a hot and cold bath in my bedroom (communicating with the sitting-room), and comforts not in existence when I was here before </s>
<s> The cost of living is enormous, but happily we can afford it </s>
<s> I dine to-day with Longfellow, Emerson, Holmes, and Agassiz </s>
<s> Longfellow was here yesterday </s>
<s> Perfectly white in hair and beard, but a remarkably handsome and notable-looking man </s>
<s> The city has increased enormously in five-and-twenty years </s>
<s> It has grown more mercantile--is like Leeds mixed with Preston, and flavoured with New Brighton; but for smoke and fog you substitute an exquisitely bright light air </s>
<s> I found my rooms beautifully decorated (by Mrs Fields) with choice flowers, and set off by a number of good books </s>
<s> I am not much persecuted by people in general, as Dolby has happily made up his mind that the less I am exhibited for nothing the better </s>
<s> So our men sit outside the room door and wrestle with mankind </s>
<s> We had speech-making and singing in the saloon of the _Cuba_ after the last dinner of the voyage </s>
<s> I think I have acquired a higher reputation from drawing out the captain, and getting him to take the second in "All's Well," and likewise in "There's not in the wide world" (your parent taking first), than from anything previously known of me on these shores </s>
<s> I hope the effect of these achievements may not dim the lustre of the readings </s>
<s> We also sang (with a Chicago lady, and a strong-minded woman from I don't know where) "Auld Lang Syne," with a tender melancholy, expressive of having all four been united from our cradles </s>
<s> The more dismal we were, the more delighted the company were </s>
<s> Once (when we paddled i' the burn) the captain took a little cruise round the compass on his own account, touching at the "Canadian Boat Song," and taking in supplies at "Jubilate," "Seas between us braid ha' roared," and roared like the seas themselves </s>
<s> Finally, I proposed the ladies in a speech that convulsed the stewards, and we closed with a brilliant success </s>
<s> But when you dine with Mr Forster, ask him to read to you how we got on at church in a heavy sea </s>
<s> Hillard has just been in and sent his love "to those dear girls" </s>
<s> He has grown much older </s>
<s> He is now District Attorney of the State of Massachusetts, which is a very good office </s>
<s> Best love to your aunt and Katie, and Charley and all his house, and all friends </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, _Monday, Nov </s>
<s> 25th, 1867._ I cannot remember to whom I wrote last, but it will not much matter if I make a mistake; this being generally to report myself so well, that I am constantly chafing at not having begun to-night instead of this night week </s>
<s> The tickets being all sold for next week, and no other announcement being yet made, there is nothing new in that way to tell of </s>
<s> Dolby is over at New York, where we are at our wits' end how to keep tickets out of the hands of speculators </s>
<s> Morgan is staying with me; came yesterday to breakfast, and goes home to-morrow </s>
<s> Fields and Mrs Fields also dined yesterday </s>
<s> She is a very nice woman, with a rare relish for humour and a most contagious laugh </s>
<s> The Bostonians having been duly informed that I wish to be quiet, really leave me as much so as I should be in Manchester or Liverpool </s>
<s> This I cannot expect to last elsewhere; but it is a most welcome relief here, as I have all the readings to get up </s>
<s> The people are perfectly kind and perfectly agreeable </s>
<s> If I stop to look in at a shop-window, a score of passers-by stop; and after I begin to read, I cannot expect in the natural course of things to get off so easily </s>
<s> But I every day take from seven to ten miles in peace </s>
<s> Communications about readings incessantly come in from all parts of the country </s>
<s> We take no offer whatever, lying by with our plans until after the first series in New York, and designing, if we make a furore there, to travel as little as possible </s>
<s> I fear I shall have to take Canada at the end of the whole tour </s>
<s> They make such strong representations from Montreal and Toronto, and from Nova Scotia--represented by St </s>
<s> John's and Halifax--of the slight it would be to them, if I wound up with the States, that I am shaken </s>
<s> It is sad to see Longfellow's house (the house in which his wife was burnt) with his young daughters in it, and the shadow of that terrible story </s>
<s> The young undergraduates of Cambridge (he is a professor there) have made a representation to him that they are five hundred strong, and cannot get one ticket </s>
<s> I don't know what is to be done for them; I suppose I must read there somehow </s>
<s> We are all in the clouds until I shall have broken ground in New York, as to where readings will be possible and where impossible </s>
<s> Agassiz is one of the most natural and jovial of men </s>
<s> I go out a-visiting as little as I can, but still have to dine, and what is worse, sup pretty often </s>
<s> Socially, I am (as I was here before) wonderfully reminded of Edinburgh when I had many friends in it </s>
<s> Your account and Mamie's of the return journey to London gave me great pleasure </s>
<s> I was delighted with your report of Wilkie, and not surprised by Chappell's coming out gallantly </s>
<s> My anxiety to get to work is greater than I can express, because time seems to be making no movement towards home until I shall be reading hard </s>
<s> Then I shall begin to count and count and count the upward steps to May </s>
<s> If ever you should be in a position to advise a traveller going on a sea voyage, remember that there is some mysterious service done to the bilious system when it is shaken, by baked apples </s>
<s> Noticing that they were produced on board the _Cuba_, every day at lunch and dinner, I thought I would make the experiment of always eating them freely </s>
<s> I am confident that they did wonders, not only at the time, but in stopping the imaginary pitching and rolling after the voyage is over, from which many good amateur sailors suffer </s>
<s> I have hardly had the sensation at all, except in washing of a morning </s>
<s> At that time I still hold on with one knee to the washing-stand, and could swear that it rolls from left to right </s>
<s> The _Cuba_ does not return until Wednesday, the 4th December </s>
<s> You may suppose that every officer on board is coming on Monday, and that Dolby has provided extra stools for them </s>
<s> His work is very hard indeed </s>
<s> Cards are brought to him every minute in the day; his correspondence is immense; and he is jerked off to New York, and I don't know where else, on the shortest notice and the most unreasonable times </s>
<s> Moreover, he has to be at "the bar" every night, and to "liquor up with all creation" in the small hours </s>
<s> He does it all with the greatest good humour, and flies at everybody who waylays the Chief, furiously </s>
<s> We have divided our men into watches, so that one always sits outside the drawing-room door </s>
<s> Dolby knows the whole Cunard line, and as we could not get good English gin, went out in a steamer yesterday and got two cases (twenty-four bottles) out of Cunard officers </s>
<s> Osgood and he were detached together last evening for New York, whence they telegraph every other hour about some new point in this precious sale of tickets </s>
<s> So distracted a telegram arrived at three that I have telegraphed back, "Explain yourselves," and am now waiting for the explanation </s>
<s> I think you know that Osgood is a partner in Ticknor and Fields' </s>
<s> Tuesday morning.--Dolby has come back from New York, where the prospects seem immense </s>
<s> We sell tickets there next Friday and Saturday, and a tremendous rush is expected </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Charles Dickens.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, U.S., _Saturday, Nov </s>
<s> 30th, 1867._ MY DEAR CHARLEY, You will have heard before now how fortunate I was on my voyage, and how I was not sick for a moment </s>
<s> These screws are tremendous ships for carrying on, and for rolling, and their vibration is rather distressing </s>
<s> But my little cabin, being for'ard of the machinery, was in the best part of the vessel, and I had as much air in it, night and day, as I chose </s>
<s> The saloon being kept absolutely without air, I mostly dined in my own den, in spite of my being allotted the post of honour on the right hand of the captain </s>
<s> The tickets for the first four readings here (the only readings announced) were all sold immediately, and many are now re-selling at a large premium </s>
<s> The tickets for the first four readings in New York (the only readings announced there also) were on sale yesterday, and were all sold in a few hours </s>
<s> The receipts are very large indeed; but engagements of any kind and every kind I steadily refuse, being resolved to take what is to be taken myself </s>
<s> Dolby is nearly worked off his legs, is now at New York, and goes backwards and forwards between this place and that (about the distance from London to Liverpool, though they take nine hours to do it) incessantly </s>
<s> Nothing can exceed his energy and good humour, and he is extremely popular everywhere </s>
<s> My great desire is to avoid much travelling, and to try to get the people to come to me, instead of my going to them </s>
<s> If I can effect this to any moderate extent, I shall be saved a great deal of knocking about </s>
<s> My original purpose was not to go to Canada at all; but Canada is so up in arms on the subject that I think I shall be obliged to take it at last </s>
<s> In that case I should work round to Halifax, Nova Scotia, and then take the packet for home </s>
<s> As they don't seem (Americans who have heard me on their travels excepted) to have the least idea here of what the readings are like, and as they are accustomed to mere readings out of a book, I am inclined to think the excitement will increase when I shall have begun </s>
<s> Everybody is very kind and considerate, and I have a number of old friends here, at the Bar and connected with the University </s>
<s> I am now negotiating to bring out the dramatic version of "No Thoroughfare" at New York </s>
<s> It is quite upon the cards that it may turn up trumps </s>
<s> I was interrupted in that place by a call from my old secretary in the States, Mr Putnam </s>
<s> It was quite affecting to see his delight in meeting his old master again </s>
<s> And when I told him that Anne was married, and that I had (unacknowledged) grandchildren, he laughed and cried together </s>
<s> I suppose you don't remember Longfellow, though he remembers you in a black velvet frock very well </s>
<s> He is now white-haired and white-bearded, but remarkably handsome </s>
<s> He still lives in his old house, where his beautiful wife was burnt to death </s>
<s> I dined with him the other day, and could not get the terrific scene out of my imagination </s>
<s> She was in a blaze in an instant, rushed into his arms with a wild cry, and never spoke afterwards </s>
<s> My love to Bessie, and to Mekitty, and all the babbies </s>
<s> I will lay this by until Tuesday morning, and then add a final line to it </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Charley, your affectionate Father </s>

<s> 3rd, 1867._ Success last night beyond description or exaggeration </s>
<s> The whole city is quite frantic about it to-day, and it is impossible that prospects could be more brilliant </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, _Sunday, Dec </s>
<s> 1st, 1867._ I received yours of the 18th November, yesterday </s>
<s> As I left Halifax in the _Cuba_ that very day, you probably saw us telegraphed in _The Times_ on the 19th </s>
<s> Dolby came back from another run to New York, this morning </s>
<s> The receipts are very large indeed, far exceeding our careful estimate made at Gad's </s>
<s> I think you had best in future (unless I give you intimation to the contrary) address your letters to me, at the Westminster Hotel, Irving Place, New York City </s>
<s> It is a more central position than this, and we are likely to be much more there than here </s>
<s> I am going to set up a brougham in New York, and keep my rooms at that hotel </s>
<s> The account of Matilda is a very melancholy one, and really distresses me </s>
<s> What she must sink into, it is sad to consider </s>
<s> However, there was nothing for it but to send her away, that is quite clear </s>
<s> They are said to be a very quiet audience here, appreciative but not demonstrative </s>
<s> I shall try to change their character a little </s>
<s> I have been going on very well </s>
<s> A horrible custom obtains in these parts of asking you to dinner somewhere at half-past two, and to supper somewhere else about eight </s>
<s> I have run this gauntlet more than once, and its effect is, that there is no day for any useful purpose, and that the length of the evening is multiplied by a hundred </s>
<s> Yesterday I dined with a club at half-past two, and came back here at half-past eight, with a general impression that it was at least two o'clock in the morning </s>
<s> Two days before I dined with Longfellow at half-past two, and came back at eight, supposing it to be midnight </s>
<s> To-day we have a state dinner-party in our rooms at six, Mr and Mrs Fields, and Mr and Mrs Bigelow </s>
<s> (He is a friend of Forster's, and was American Minister in Paris) </s>
<s> There are no negro waiters here, all the servants are Irish--willing, but not able </s>
<s> The dinners and wines are very good </s>
<s> I keep our own rooms well ventilated by opening the windows, but no window is ever opened in the halls or passages, and they are so overheated by a great furnace, that they make me faint and sick </s>
<s> The air is like that of a pre-Adamite ironing-day in full blast </s>
<s> Your respected parent is immensely popular in Boston society, and its cordiality and unaffected heartiness are charming </s>
<s> I wish I could carry it with me </s>
<s> The leading New York papers have sent men over for to-morrow night with instructions to telegraph columns of descriptions </s>
<s> Great excitement and expectation everywhere </s>
<s> Fields says he has looked forward to it so long that he knows he will die at five minutes to eight </s>
<s> At the New York barriers, where the tickets are on sale and the people ranged as at the Paris theatres, speculators went up and down offering "twenty dollars for anybody's place" </s>
<s> The money was in no case accepted </s>
<s> One man sold two tickets for the second, third, and fourth night for "one ticket for the first, fifty dollars" (about seven pounds ten shillings), "and a brandy cocktail," which is an iced bitter drink </s>
<s> The weather has been rather muggy and languid until yesterday, when there was the coldest wind blowing that I ever felt </s>
<s> In the night it froze very hard, and to-day the sky is beautiful </s>
<s> _Tuesday, Dec </s>
<s> 3rd._ Most magnificent reception last night, and most signal and complete success </s>
<s> Nothing could be more triumphant </s>
<s> The people will hear of nothing else and talk of nothing else </s>
<s> Nothing that was ever done here, they all agree, evoked any approach to such enthusiasm </s>
<s> I was quite as cool and quick as if I were reading at Greenwich, and went at it accordingly </s>

<s> That will be from New York </s>

<s> Great reception </s>
<s> Great, "Carol" and "Trial," on the first night; still greater, "Copperfield" and "Bob," on the second </s>
<s> Dolby sends you a few papers by this post </s>
<s> You will see from their tone what a success it is </s>
<s> I cannot pay this letter, because I give it at the latest moment to the mail-officer, who is going on board the Cunard packet in charge of the mails, and who is staying in this house </s>

<s> All night long Dolby and our man have been stamping tickets </s>
<s> (Immediately over my head, by-the-bye, and keeping me awake.) This hotel is quite as quiet as Mivart's, in Brook Street </s>
<s> It is not very much larger </s>
<s> There are American hotels close by, with five hundred bedrooms, and I don't know how many boarders; but this is conducted on what is called "the European principle," and is an admirable mixture of a first-class French and English house </s>
<s> I keep a very smart carriage and pair; and if you were to behold me driving out, furred up to the moustache, with furs on the coach-boy and on the driver, and with an immense white, red, and yellow striped rug for a covering, you would suppose me to be of Hungarian or Polish nationality </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, IRVING PLACE, NEW YORK CITY, _Monday, Dec </s>
<s> 16th, 1867._ We have been snowed up here, and the communication with Boston is still very much retarded </s>
<s> Thus we have received no letters by the Cunard steamer that came in last Wednesday, and are in a grim state of mind on that subject </s>
<s> Last night I was getting into bed just at twelve o'clock, when Dolby came to my door to inform me that the house was on fire (I had previously smelt fire for two hours) </s>
<s> I got Scott up directly, told him to pack the books and clothes for the readings first, dressed, and pocketed my jewels and papers, while Dolby stuffed himself out with money </s>
<s> Meanwhile the police and firemen were in the house, endeavouring to find where the fire was </s>
<s> For some time it baffled their endeavours, but at last, bursting out through some stairs, they cut the stairs away, and traced it to its source in a certain fire-grate </s>
<s> By this time the hose was laid all through the house from a great tank on the roof, and everybody turned out to help </s>
<s> It was the oddest sight, and people had put the strangest things on </s>
<s> After a little chopping and cutting with axes and handing about of water, the fire was confined to a dining-room in which it had originated, and then everybody talked to everybody else, the ladies being particularly loquacious and cheerful </s>
<s> And so we got to bed again at about two </s>
<s> The excitement of the readings continues unabated, the tickets for readings are sold as soon as they are ready, and the public pay treble prices to the speculators who buy them up </s>
<s> They are a wonderfully fine audience, even better than Edinburgh, and almost, if not quite, as good as Paris </s>
<s> Dolby continues to be the most unpopular man in America (mainly because he can't get four thousand people into a room that holds two thousand), and is reviled in print daily </s>
<s> Yesterday morning a newspaper proclaims of him: "Surely it is time that the pudding-headed Dolby retired into the native gloom from which he has emerged" </s>
<s> He takes it very coolly, and does his best </s>
<s> Mrs Morgan sent me, the other night, I suppose the finest and costliest basket of flowers ever seen, made of white camellias, yellow roses, pink roses, and I don't know what else </s>
<s> It is a yard and a half round at its smallest part </s>
<s> I must bring this to a close, as I have to go to the hall to try an enlarged background </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BOSTON, _Sunday, Dec </s>
<s> 22nd, 1867._ Coming here from New York last night (after a detestable journey), I was delighted to find your letter of the 6th </s>
<s> I read it at my ten o'clock dinner with the greatest interest and pleasure, and then we talked of home till we went to bed </s>
<s> Our tour is now being made out, and I hope to be able to send it in my next letter home, which will be to Mamie, from whom I have _not_ heard (as you thought I had) by the mail that brought out yours </s>
<s> After very careful consideration I have reversed Dolby's original plan, and have decided on taking Baltimore, Washington, Cincinnati, _Chicago_ (!), St </s>
<s> Louis, and a few other places nearer here, instead of staying in New York </s>
<s> My reason is that we are doing immensely, both at New York and here, and that I am sure it is in the peculiar character of the people to prize a thing the more the less easily attainable it is made </s>
<s> Therefore, I want, by absence, to get the greatest rush and pressure upon the five farewell readings in New York in April </s>
<s> All our announced readings are already crammed </s>

<s> She is one of the dearest little women in the world </s>
<s> The homely Christmas look of the place quite affected us </s>
<s> Yesterday we dined at her house, and there was a plum-pudding, brought on blazing, and not to be surpassed in any house in England </s>
<s> There is a certain Captain Dolliver, belonging to the Boston Custom House, who came off in the little steamer that brought me ashore from the _Cuba_ </s>
<s> He took it into his head that he would have a piece of English mistletoe brought out in this week's Cunard, which should be laid upon my breakfast-table </s>
<s> And there it was this morning </s>
<s> In such affectionate touches as this, these New England people are especially amiable </s>
<s> As a general rule, you may lay it down that whatever you see about me in the papers is not true </s>
<s> But although my voyage out was of that highly hilarious description that you first made known to me, you may _generally_ lend a more believing ear to the Philadelphia correspondent of _The Times_ </s>
<s> I don't know him, but I know the source from which he derives his information, and it is a very respectable one </s>
<s> Did I tell you in a former letter from here, to tell Anne, with her old master's love, that I had seen Putnam, my old secretary </s>
<s> Grey, and with several front teeth out, but I would have known him anywhere </s>
<s> He is coming to "Copperfield" to-night, accompanied by his wife and daughter, and is in the seventh heaven at having his tickets given him </s>
<s> Our hotel in New York was on fire _again_ the other night </s>
<s> But fires in this country are quite matters of course </s>
<s> There was a large one there at four this morning, and I don't think a single night has passed since I have been under the protection of the Eagle, but I have heard the fire bells dolefully clanging all over the city </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, IRVING PLACE, NEW YORK CITY, _Thursday, Dec </s>
<s> 26th, 1867._ I got your aunt's last letter at Boston yesterday, Christmas Day morning, when I was starting at eleven o'clock to come back to this place </s>
<s> I wanted it very much, for I had a frightful cold (English colds are nothing to those of this country), and was exceedingly depressed and miserable </s>
<s> Not that I had any reason but illness for being so, since the Bostonians had been quite astounding in their demonstrations </s>
<s> I never saw anything like them on Christmas Eve </s>
<s> But it is a bad country to be unwell and travelling in; you are one of say a hundred people in a heated car, with a great stove in it, and all the little windows closed, and the hurrying and banging about are indescribable </s>
<s> The atmosphere is detestable, and the motion often all but intolerable </s>
<s> However, we got our dinner here at eight o'clock, and plucked up a little, and I made some hot gin punch to drink a merry Christmas to all at home in </s>
<s> But it must be confessed that we were both very dull </s>
<s> I have been in bed all day until two o'clock, and here I am now (at three o'clock) a little better </s>
<s> But I am not fit to read, and I must read to-night </s>
<s> After watching the general character pretty closely, I became quite sure that Dolby was wrong on the length of the stay and the number of readings we had proposed in this place </s>
<s> I am quite certain that it is one of the national peculiarities that what they want must be difficult of attainment </s>
<s> I therefore a few days ago made a _coup d'état_, and altered the whole scheme </s>
<s> We shall go to Philadelphia, Baltimore, Washington, also some New England towns between Boston and this place, away to the falls of Niagara, and off far west to Chicago and St </s>
<s> Louis, before coming back for ten farewell readings here, preceded by farewells at Boston, leaving Canada altogether </s>
<s> This will not prolong the list beyond eighty-four readings, the exact original number, and will, please God, work it all out in April </s>

<s> If I do not send a letter to Katie by this mail, it will be because I shall probably be obliged to go across the water to Brooklyn to-morrow to see a church, in which it is proposed that I shall read!! </s>
<s> Horrible visions of being put in the pulpit already beset me </s>
<s> And whether the audience will be in pews is another consideration which greatly disturbs my mind </s>
<s> No paper ever comes out without a leader on Dolby, who of course reads them all, and never can understand why I don't, in which he is called all the bad names in (and not in) the language </s>

<s> H </s>
