<s> 1868 </s>
<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> Charles Dickens remained in America through the winter, returning home from New York in the _Russia_, on the 19th of April </s>
<s> His letters show how entirely he gave himself up to the business of the readings, how severely his health suffered from the climate, and from the perpetual travelling and hard work, and yet how he was able to battle through to the end </s>
<s> These letters are also full of allusions to the many kind and dear friends who contributed so largely to the pleasure of this American visit, and whose love and attention gave a touch of _home_ to his private life, and left such affection and gratitude in his heart as he could never forget </s>
<s> Many of these friends paid visits to Gad's Hill; the first to come during this summer being Mr Longfellow, his daughters, and Mr Appleton, brother-in-law of Mr Longfellow, and Mr and Mrs Charles Eliot Norton, of Cambridge </s>
<s> For the future, there were to be no more Christmas numbers of "All the Year Round" </s>
<s> Observing the extent to which they were now copied in all directions, Charles Dickens supposed them likely to become tiresome to the public, and so determined that in his journal they should be discontinued </s>
<s> While still in America, he made an agreement with the Messrs </s>
<s> Chappell to give a series of farewell readings in England, to commence in the autumn of this year </s>
<s> So, in October, Charles Dickens started off again for a tour in the provinces </s>
<s> He had for some time been planning, by way of a novelty for this series, a reading from the murder in "Oliver Twist," but finding it so very horrible, he was fearful of trying its effect for the first time on a public audience </s>
<s> It was therefore resolved, that a trial of it should be made to a limited private audience in St </s>
<s> James's Hall, on the evening of the 18th of November </s>
<s> This trial proved eminently successful, and "The Murder from Oliver Twist" became one of the most popular of his selections </s>
<s> But the physical exertion it involved was far greater than that of any of his previous readings, and added immensely to the excitement and exhaustion which they caused him </s>
<s> One of the first letters of the year from America is addressed to Mr Samuel Cartwright, of surgical and artistic reputation, and greatly esteemed by Charles Dickens, both in his professional capacity and as a private friend </s>
<s> The letter written to Mrs Cattermole, in May, tells of the illness of Mr George Cattermole </s>
<s> This dear old friend, so associated with Charles Dickens and his works, died soon afterwards, and the letter to his widow shows that Charles Dickens was exerting himself in her behalf </s>
<s> The play of "No Thoroughfare" having been translated into French under the title of "L'Abîme," Charles Dickens went over to Paris to be present at the first night of its production </s>
<s> On the 26th of September, his youngest son, Edward Bulwer Lytton (the "Plorn" so often mentioned), started for Australia, to join his brother Alfred Tennyson, who was already established there </s>
<s> It will be seen by his own words how deeply and how sadly Charles Dickens felt this parting </s>
<s> In October of this year, his son Henry Fielding entered Trinity Hall, Cambridge, as an undergraduate </s>
<s> The Miss Forster mentioned in the letter to his sister-in-law, and for whom the kind and considerate arrangements were suggested, was a sister of Mr John Forster, and a lady highly esteemed by Charles Dickens </s>
<s> The illness from which she was then suffering was a fatal one </s>
<s> She died in this same year, a few days before Christmas </s>
<s> Mr J </s>
<s> C </s>
<s> Parkinson, to whom a letter is addressed, was a gentleman holding a Government appointment, and contributing largely to journalism and periodical literature </s>
<s> As our last letter for this year, we give one which Charles Dickens wrote to his youngest son on his departure for Australia </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, IRVING PLACE, NEW YORK, _Friday, Jan </s>
<s> 3rd, 1868._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, I received yours of the 19th from Gad's and the office this morning </s>
<s> I read here to-night, and go back to Boston to-morrow, to read there Monday and Tuesday </s>
<s> To-night, I read out the first quarter of my list </s>
<s> Our houses have been very fine here, but have never quite recovered the Dolby uproar </s>
<s> It seems impossible to devise any scheme for getting the tickets into the people's hands without the intervention of speculators </s>
<s> The people _will not_ help themselves; and, of course, the speculators and all other such prowlers throw as great obstacles in Dolby's way (an Englishman's) as they possibly can </s>
<s> He may be a little injudicious into the bargain </s>
<s> Last night, for instance, he met one of the "ushers" (who show people to their seats) coming in with Kelly </s>
<s> It is against orders that anyone employed in front should go out during the readings, and he took this man to task in the British manner </s>
<s> Instantly the free and independent usher put on his hat and walked off </s>
<s> Seeing which, all the other free and independent ushers (some twenty in number) put on _their_ hats and walked off, leaving us absolutely devoid and destitute of a staff for to-night </s>
<s> One has since been improvised; but it was a small matter to raise a stir and ill will about, especially as one of our men was equally in fault </s>
<s> We have a regular clerk, a Bostonian whose name is Wild </s>
<s> He, Osgood, Dolby, Kelly, Scott, George the gasman, and perhaps a boy or two, constitute my body-guard </s>
<s> It seems a large number of people, but the business cannot be done with fewer </s>
<s> The speculators buying the front seats to sell at a premium (and we have found instances of this being done by merchants in good position!), and the public perpetually pitching into Dolby for selling them back seats, the result is that they won't have the back seats, send back their tickets, write and print volumes on the subject, and deter others from coming </s>
<s> You may get an idea of the staff's work, by what is in hand now </s>
<s> They are preparing, numbering, and stamping six thousand tickets for Philadelphia, and eight thousand tickets for Brooklyn </s>
<s> The moment those are done, another eight thousand tickets will be wanted for Baltimore, and probably another six thousand for Washington </s>
<s> This in addition to the correspondence, advertisements, accounts, travellings, and the mighty business of the reading four times a week </s>
<s> The Cunard steamers being now removed from Halifax, I have decided _not_ to go there, or to St </s>
<s> John's, New Brunswick </s>
<s> And as there would be a perfect uproar if I picked out such a place in Canada as Quebec or Montreal, and excluded those two places (which would guarantee three hundred pounds a night), and further, as I don't want places, having more than enough for my list of eighty-four, I have finally resolved not to go to Canada either </s>
<s> This will enable me to embark for home in April instead of May </s>
<s> Tell Plorn, with my love, that I think he will find himself much interested at that college,[20] and that it is very likely he may make some acquaintances there that will thereafter be pleasant and useful to him </s>
<s> Sir Sydney Dacres is the best of friends </s>
<s> I have a letter from Mrs Hulkes by this post, wherein the boy encloses a violet, now lying on the table before me </s>
<s> Let her know that it arrived safely, and retaining its colour </s>
<s> I took it for granted that Mary would have asked Chorley for Christmas Day, and am very glad she ultimately did so </s>
<s> I am sorry that Harry lost his prize, but believe it was not his fault </s>
<s> Let _him_ know _that_, with my love </s>
<s> I would have written to him by this mail in answer to his, but for other occupation </s>
<s> Did I tell you that my landlord made me a drink (brandy, rum, and snow the principal ingredients) called a "Rocky Mountain sneezer" </s>
<s> Or that the favourite drink before you get up is an "eye-opener" </s>
<s> Or that Roberts (second landlord), no sooner saw me on the night of the first fire, than, with his property blazing, he insisted on taking me down into a roomful of hot smoke to drink brandy and water with him </s>
<s> We have not been on fire again, by-the-bye, more than once </s>
<s> There has been another fall of snow, succeeded by a heavy thaw </s>
<s> I have laid down my sledge, and taken up my carriage again, in consequence </s>
<s> I am nearly all right, but cannot get rid of an intolerable cold in the head </s>
<s> No more news </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] PARKER HOUSE, BOSTON, U.S., _Jan </s>
<s> 4th, 1868._ I write to you by this opportunity, though I really have nothing to tell you </s>
<s> The work is hard and the climate is hard </s>
<s> We made a tremendous hit last night with "Nickleby" and "Boots," which the Bostonians certainly on the whole appreciate more than "Copperfield" </s>
<s> Dolby is always going about with an immense bundle that looks like a sofa cushion, but it is in reality paper money; and always works like a Trojan </s>
<s> His business at night is a mere nothing, for these people are so accustomed to take care of themselves, that one of these immense audiences will fall into their places with an ease amazing to a frequenter of St </s>
<s> James's Hall </s>
<s> And the certainty with which they are all in, before I go on, is a very acceptable mark of respect </s>
<s> I must add, too, that although there is a conventional familiarity in the use of one's name in the newspapers as "Dickens," "Charlie," and what not, I do not in the least see that familiarity in the writers themselves </s>
<s> An inscrutable tone obtains in journalism, which a stranger cannot understand </s>
<s> If I say in common courtesy to one of them, when Dolby introduces, "I am much obliged to you for your interest in me," or so forth, he seems quite shocked, and has a bearing of perfect modesty and propriety </s>
<s> I am rather inclined to think that they suppose their printed tone to be the public's love of smartness, but it is immensely difficult to make out </s>
<s> All I can as yet make out is, that my perfect freedom from bondage, and at any moment to go on or leave off, or otherwise do as I like, is the only safe position to occupy </s>
<s> Again; there are two apparently irreconcilable contrasts here </s>
<s> Down below in this hotel every night are the bar loungers, dram drinkers, drunkards, swaggerers, loafers, that one might find in a Boucicault play </s>
<s> Within half an hour is Cambridge, where a delightful domestic life--simple, self-respectful, cordial, and affectionate--is seen in an admirable aspect </s>
<s> All New England is primitive and puritanical </s>
<s> All about and around it is a puddle of mixed human mud, with no such quality in it </s>
<s> Perhaps I may in time sift out some tolerably intelligible whole, but I certainly have not done so yet </s>
<s> It is a good sign, may be, that it all seems immensely more difficult to understand than it was when I was here before </s>
<s> Felton left two daughters </s>
<s> I have only seen the eldest, a very sensible, frank, pleasant girl of eight-and-twenty, perhaps, rather like him in the face </s>
<s> A striking-looking daughter of Hawthorn's (who is also dead) came into my room last night </s>
<s> The day has slipped on to three o'clock, and I must get up "Dombey" for to-night </s>
<s> Hence this sudden break off </s>
<s> Best love to Mamie, and to Katie and Charley Collins </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> Wilkie Collins.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, NEW YORK, _Sunday, Jan </s>
<s> 12th, 1868._ MY DEAR WILKIE, First, of the play.[21] I am truly delighted to learn that it made so great a success, and I hope I may yet see it on the Adelphi boards </s>
<s> You have had a world of trouble and work with it, but I hope will be repaid in some degree by the pleasure of a triumph </s>
<s> Even for the alteration at the end of the fourth act (of which you tell me in your letter received yesterday), I was fully prepared, for I COULD NOT see the original effect in the reading of the play, and COULD NOT make it go </s>
<s> I agree with Webster in thinking it best that Obenreizer should die on the stage; but no doubt that point is disposed of </s>
<s> In reading the play before the representation, I felt that it was too long, and that there was a good deal of unnecessary explanation </s>
<s> Those points are, no doubt, disposed of too by this time </s>
<s> We shall do nothing with it on this side </s>
<s> Pirates are producing their own wretched versions in all directions, thus (as Wills would say) anticipating and glutting "the market" </s>
<s> I registered one play as the property of Ticknor and Fields, American citizens </s>
<s> But, besides that the law on the point is extremely doubtful, the manager of the Museum Theatre, Boston, instantly announced his version </s>
<s> (You may suppose what it is and how it is done, when I tell you that it was playing within ten days of the arrival out of the Christmas number.) Thereupon, Ticknor and Fields gave him notice that he mustn't play it </s>
<s> Unto which he replied, that he meant to play it and would play it </s>
<s> Of course he knew very well that if an injunction were applied for against him, there would be an immediate howl against my persecution of an innocent, and he played it </s>
<s> Then the noble host of pirates rushed in, and it is being done, in some mangled form or other, everywhere </s>
<s> It touches me to read what you write of your poor mother </s>
<s> But, of course, at her age, each winter counts heavily </s>
<s> Do give her my love, and tell her that I asked you about her </s>
<s> I am going on here at the same great rate, but am always counting the days that lie between me and home </s>
<s> I got through the first fourth of my readings on Friday, January 3rd </s>
<s> I leave for two readings at Philadelphia this evening </s>
<s> Being at Boston last Sunday, I took it into my head to go over the medical school, and survey the holes and corners in which that extraordinary murder was done by Webster </s>
<s> There was the furnace--stinking horribly, as if the dismembered pieces were still inside it--and there are all the grim spouts, and sinks, and chemical appliances, and what not </s>
<s> At dinner, afterwards, Longfellow told me a terrific story </s>
<s> He dined with Webster within a year of the murder, one of a party of ten or twelve </s>
<s> As they sat at their wine, Webster suddenly ordered the lights to be turned out, and a bowl of some burning mineral to be placed on the table, that the guests might see how ghostly it made them look </s>
<s> As each man stared at all the rest in the weird light, all were horrified to see Webster _with a rope round his neck_, holding it up, over the bowl, with his head jerked on one side, and his tongue lolled out, representing a man being hanged </s>
<s> Poking into his life and character, I find (what I would have staked my head upon) that he was always a cruel man </s>
<s> So no more at present from, My dear Wilkie, yours ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, NEW YORK, _Sunday, Jan </s>
<s> 12th, 1868._ As I am off to Philadelphia this evening, I may as well post my letter here </s>
<s> I have scarcely a word of news </s>
<s> My cold steadily refuses to leave me; but otherwise I am as right as one can hope to be under this heavy work </s>
<s> My New York readings are over (except four farewell nights in April), and I look forward to the relief of being out of my hardest hall </s>
<s> Last Friday night, though it was only "Nickleby" and "Boots," I was again dead beat at the end, and was once more laid upon a sofa </s>
<s> But the faintness went off after a little while </s>
<s> We have now cold, bright, frosty weather, without snow--the best weather for me </s>
<s> Having been in great trepidation about the play, I am correspondingly elated by the belief that it really _is_ a success </s>
<s> No doubt the unnecessary explanations will have been taken out, and the flatness of the last act fetched up </s>
<s> At some points I could have done wonders to it, in the way of screwing it up sharply and picturesquely, if I could have rehearsed it </s>
<s> Your account of the first night interested me immensely, but I was afraid to open the letter until Dolby rushed in with the opened _Times_ </s>
<s> On Wednesday I come back here for my four church readings at Brooklyn </s>
<s> Each evening an enormous ferryboat will convey me and my state carriage (not to mention half-a-dozen waggons, and any number of people, and a few score of horses) across the river, and will bring me back again </s>
<s> The sale of tickets there was an amazing scene </s>
<s> The noble army of speculators are now furnished (this is literally true, and I am quite serious), each man with a straw mattress, a little bag of bread and meat, two blankets, and a bottle of whisky </s>
<s> With this outfit _they lie down in line on the pavement_ the whole night before the tickets are sold, generally taking up their position at about ten </s>
<s> It being severely cold at Brooklyn, they made an immense bonfire in the street--a narrow street of wooden houses!--which the police turned out to extinguish </s>
<s> A general fight then took place, out of which the people farthest off in the line rushed bleeding when they saw a chance of displacing others near the door, and put their mattresses in those places, and then held on by the iron rails </s>
<s> At eight in the morning Dolby appeared with the tickets in a portmanteau </s>
<s> He was immediately saluted with a roar of "Halloa, Dolby </s>
<s> So Charley has let you have the carriage, has he, Dolby </s>
<s> How is he, Dolby </s>
<s> Don't drop the tickets, Dolby </s>
<s> Look alive, Dolby" </s>
<s> etc etc etc, in the midst of which he proceeded to business, and concluded (as usual) by giving universal dissatisfaction </s>
<s> He is now going off upon a little journey "to look over the ground and cut back again" </s>
<s> This little journey (to Chicago) is fifteen hundred miles on end, by railway, and back again </s>
<s> We have an excellent gasman, who is well up to that department </s>
<s> We have enlarged the large staff by another clerk, yet even now the preparation of such an immense number of new tickets constantly, and the keeping and checking of the accounts, keep them hard at it </s>
<s> And they get so oddly divided </s>
<s> Kelly is at Philadelphia, another man at Baltimore, two others are stamping tickets at the top of this house, another is cruising over New England, and Osgood will come on duty to-morrow (when Dolby starts off) to pick me up after the reading, and take me to the hotel, and mount guard over me, and bring me back here </s>
<s> You see that even such wretched domesticity as Dolby and self by a fireside is broken up under these conditions </s>
<s> Dolby has been twice poisoned, and Osgood once </s>
<s> Morgan's sharpness has discovered the cause </s>
<s> When the snow is deep upon the ground, and the partridges cannot get their usual food, they eat something (I don't know what, if anybody does) which does not poison _them_, but which poisons the people who eat them </s>
<s> The symptoms, which last some twelve hours, are violent sickness, cold perspiration, and the formation of some detestable mucus in the stomach </s>
<s> You may infer that partridges have been banished from our bill of fare </s>
<s> The appearance of our sufferers was lamentable in the extreme </s>
<s> Did I tell you that the severity of the weather, and the heat of the intolerable furnaces, dry the hair and break the nails of strangers </s>
<s> There is not a complete nail in the whole British suite, and my hair cracks again when I brush it </s>
<s> (I am losing my hair with great rapidity, and what I don't lose is getting very grey.) The _Cuba_ will bring this </s>
<s> She has a jolly new captain--Moody, of the _Java_--and her people rushed into the reading, the other night, captain-headed, as if I were their peculiar property </s>
<s> Please God I shall come home in her, in my old cabin; leaving here on the 22nd of April, and finishing my eighty-fourth reading on the previous night </s>
<s> It is likely enough that I shall read and go straight on board </s>
<s> I think this is all my poor stock of intelligence </s>
<s> By-the-bye, on the last Sunday in the old year, I lost my old year's pocket-book, "which," as Mr Pepys would add, "do trouble me mightily" </s>
<s> Give me Katie's new address; I haven't got it </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PHILADELPHIA, _Monday, Jan </s>
<s> 13th, 1868._ I write you this note, a day later than your aunt's, not because I have anything to add to the little I have told her, but because you may like to have it </s>
<s> We arrived here last night towards twelve o'clock, more than an hour after our time </s>
<s> This is one of the immense American hotels (it is called the Continental); but I find myself just as quiet here as elsewhere </s>
<s> Everything is very good indeed, the waiter is German, and the greater part of the house servants seem to be coloured people </s>
<s> The town is very clean, and the day as blue and bright as a fine Italian day </s>
<s> But it freezes very hard </s>
<s> All the tickets being sold here for six nights (three visits of two nights each), the suite complain of want of excitement already, having been here ten hours </s>
<s> Mr and Mrs Barney Williams, with a couple of servants, and a pretty little child-daughter, were in the train each night, and I talked with them a good deal </s>
<s> They are reported to have made an enormous fortune by acting among the Californian gold-diggers </s>
<s> My cold is no better, for the cars are so intolerably hot, that I was often obliged to go and stand upon the break outside, and then the frosty air was biting indeed </s>
<s> The great man of this place is one Mr Childs, a newspaper proprietor, and he is so exactly like Mr Esse in all conceivable respects except being an inch or so taller, that I was quite confounded when I saw him waiting for me at the station (always called depôt here) with his carriage </s>
<s> During the last two or three days, Dolby and I have been making up accounts, which are excellently kept by Mr Osgood, and I find them amazing, quite, in their results </s>
<s> I was very much interested in the home accounts of Christmas Day </s>
<s> I think I have already mentioned that we were in very low spirits on that day </s>
<s> I began to be unwell with my cold that morning, and a long day's travel did not mend the matter </s>
<s> We scarcely spoke (except when we ate our lunch), and sat dolefully staring out of window </s>
<s> I had a few affectionate words from Chorley, dated from my room, on Christmas morning, and will write him, probably by this mail, a brief acknowledgment </s>
<s> I find it necessary (so oppressed am I with this American catarrh, as they call it) to dine at three o'clock instead of four, that I may have more time to get voice, so that the days are cut short, and letter-writing is not easy </s>
<s> My best love to Katie, and to Charley, and to our Charley, and to all friends </s>
<s> If I could only get to the point of being able to hold my head up and dispense with my pocket-handkerchief for five minutes, I should be all right </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Charles Dickens.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, IRVING PLACE, NEW YORK, _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 15th, 1868._ MY DEAR CHARLEY, Finding your letter here this afternoon on my return from Philadelphia (where I have been reading two nights), I take advantage of a spare half-hour in which to answer it at once, though it will not leave here until Saturday </s>
<s> I had previously heard of the play, and had _The Times_ </s>
<s> It was a great relief and delight to me, for I had no confidence in its success; being reduced to the confines of despair by its length </s>
<s> If I could have rehearsed it, I should have taken the best part of an hour out of it </s>
<s> Fechter must be very fine, and I should greatly like to see him play the part </s>
<s> I have not been very well generally, and am oppressed (and I begin to think that I probably shall be until I leave) by a true American cold, which I hope, for the comfort of human nature, may be peculiar to only one of the four quarters of the world </s>
<s> The work, too, is very severe </s>
<s> But I am going on at the same tremendous rate everywhere </s>
<s> The staff, too, has had to be enlarged </s>
<s> Dolby was at Baltimore yesterday, is at Washington to-day, and will come back in the night, and start away again on Friday </s>
<s> We find it absolutely necessary for him to go on ahead </s>
<s> We have not printed or posted a single bill here, and have just sold ninety pounds' worth of paper we had got ready for bills </s>
<s> In such a rush a short newspaper advertisement is all we want </s>
<s> "Doctor Marigold" made a great hit here, and is looked forward to at Boston with especial interest </s>
<s> I go to Boston for another fortnight, on end, the 24th of February </s>
<s> The railway journeys distress me greatly </s>
<s> I get out into the open air (upon the break), and it snows and blows, and the train bumps, and the steam flies at me, until I am driven in again </s>
<s> I have finished here (except four farewell nights in April), and begin four nights at Brooklyn, on the opposite side of the river, to-night; and thus oscillate between Philadelphia, Baltimore, and Washington, and then cut into New England, and so work my way back to Boston for a fortnight, after which come Chicago, Cincinnati, Detroit and Cleveland, and Buffalo, and then Philadelphia, Boston, and New York farewells </s>
<s> I will not pass my original bound of eighty-four readings in all </s>
<s> My mind was made up as to that long ago </s>
<s> It will be quite enough </s>
<s> Chicago is some fifteen hundred miles from here </s>
<s> What with travelling, and getting ready for reading, and reading, the days are pretty fully occupied </s>
<s> Not the less so because I rest very indifferently at night </s>
<s> The people are exceedingly kind and considerate, and desire to be most hospitable besides </s>
<s> But I cannot accept hospitality, and never go out, except at Boston, or I should not be fit for the labour </s>
<s> If Dolby holds out well to the last it will be a triumph, for he has to see everybody, drink with everybody, sell all the tickets, take all the blame, and go beforehand to all the places on the list </s>
<s> I shall not see him after to-night for ten days or a fortnight, and he will be perpetually on the road during the interval </s>
<s> When he leaves me, Osgood, a partner in Ticknor and Fields' publishing firm, mounts guard over me, and has to go into the hall from the platform door every night, and see how the public are seating themselves </s>
<s> It is very odd to see how hard he finds it to look a couple of thousand people in the face, on which head, by-the-bye, I notice the papers to take "Mr Dickens's extraordinary composure" (their great phrase) rather ill, and on the whole to imply that it would be taken as a suitable compliment if I would stagger on to the platform and instantly drop, overpowered by the spectacle before me </s>

<s> P.S.--Your paper is remarkably good </s>
<s> There is not the least doubt that you can write constantly for A </s>
<s> Y </s>
<s> R </s>
<s> I am very pleased with it </s>

<s> My "true American catarrh" (the people seem to have a national pride in it) sticks to me, but I am otherwise well </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WESTMINSTER HOTEL, NEW YORK, _Tuesday, Jan </s>
<s> 21st, 1868._ I finished my church to-night </s>
<s> It is Mrs Stowe's brother's, and a most wonderful place to speak in </s>
<s> We had it enormously full last night ("Marigold" and "Trial"), but it scarcely required an effort </s>
<s> Mr Ward Beecher (Mrs Stowe's brother's name) being present in his pew </s>
<s> I sent to invite him to come round before he left; and I found him to be an unostentatious, straightforward, and agreeable fellow </s>
<s> My cold sticks to me, and I can scarcely exaggerate what I sometimes undergo from sleeplessness </s>
<s> The day before yesterday I could get no rest until morning, and could not get up before twelve </s>
<s> This morning the same </s>
<s> I rarely take any breakfast but an egg and a cup of tea, not even toast or bread-and-butter </s>
<s> My dinner at three, and a little quail or some such light thing when I come home at night, is my daily fare </s>
<s> At the Hall I have established the custom of taking an egg beaten up in sherry before going in, and another between the parts </s>
<s> I think that pulls me up; at all events, I have since had no return of faintness </s>
<s> As the men work very hard, and always with their hearts cheerfully in the business, I cram them into and outside of the carriage, to bring them back from Brooklyn with me </s>
<s> The other night, Scott (with a portmanteau across his knees and a wideawake hat low down upon his nose) told me that he had presented himself for admission in the circus (as good as Franconi's, by-the-bye), and had been refused </s>
<s> "The only theayter," he said in a melancholy way, "as I was ever in my life turned from the door of" </s>

<s> Go again, Scott" </s>
<s> "No, I thank you, Kelly," says Scott, more melancholy than before, "I'm not a-going to put myself in the position of being refused again </s>
<s> It's the only theayter as I was ever turned from the door of, and it shan't be done twice </s>
<s> But it's a beastly country" </s>
<s> "Scott," interposed Majesty, "don't you express your opinions about the country" </s>
<s> "No, sir," says Scott, "I never do, please, sir, but when you are turned from the door of the only theayter you was ever turned from, sir, and when the beasts in railway cars spits tobacco over your boots, you (privately) find yourself in a beastly country" </s>
<s> I expect shortly to get myself snowed up on some railway or other, for it is snowing hard now, and I begin to move to-morrow </s>
<s> There is so much floating ice in the river that we are obliged to leave a pretty wide margin of time for getting over the ferry to read </s>
<s> The dinner is coming in, and I must leave off </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PHILADELPHIA, _Thursday, Jan </s>
<s> 23rd, 1868._ When I wrote to your aunt by the last mail, I accidentally omitted to touch upon the question of helping Anne </s>
<s> So I will begin in this present writing with reference to her sad position </s>
<s> I think it will be best for you to be guided by an exact knowledge of her _wants_ </s>
<s> Try to ascertain from herself what means she has, whether her sick husband gets what he ought to have, whether she is pinched in the articles of necessary clothing, bedding, or the like of that; add to this intelligence your own observation of the state of things about her, and supply what she most wants, and help her where you find the greatest need </s>
<s> The question, in the case of so old and faithful a servant, is not one of so much or so little money on my side, but how _most efficiently_ to ease her mind and help _her_ </s>
<s> To do this at once kindly and sensibly is the only consideration by which you have to be guided </s>
<s> Take _carte blanche_ from me for all the rest </s>
<s> My Washington week is the first week in February, beginning on Monday, 3rd </s>
<s> The tickets are sold, and the President is coming, and the chief members of the Cabinet, and the leaders of parties, and so forth, are coming; and, as the Holly Tree Boots says: "That's where it is, don't you see" </s>
<s> In my Washington doubts I recalled Dolby for conference, and he joined me yesterday afternoon, and we have been in great discussion ever since on the possibility of giving up the Far West, and avoiding such immense distances and fatigues as would be involved in travelling to Chicago and Cincinnati </s>
<s> We have sketched another tour for the last half of March, which would be infinitely easier for me, though on the other hand less profitable, the places and the halls being smaller </s>
<s> The worst of it is, that everybody one advises with has a monomania respecting Chicago </s>
<s> "Good heaven, sir," the great Philadelphian authority said to me this morning, "if you don't read in Chicago, the people will go into fits" </s>
<s> In reference to fatigue, I answered: "Well, I would rather they went into fits than I did" </s>
<s> But he didn't seem to see it at all </s>
<s> ---- alone constantly writes me: "Don't go to the West; you can get what you want so much more easily" </s>
<s> How we shall finally decide, I don't yet know </s>
<s> My Brooklyn church has been an immense success, and I found its minister was a bachelor, a clever, unparsonic, and straightforward man, and a man with a good knowledge of art into the bargain </s>
<s> We are not a bit too soon here, for the whole country is beginning to be stirred and shaken by the presidential election, and trade is exceedingly depressed, and will be more so </s>
<s> Fanny Kemble lives near this place, but had gone away a day before my first visit here </s>
<s> _She_ is going to read in February or March </s>
<s> Du Chaillu has been lecturing out West about the gorilla, and has been to see me; I saw the Cunard steamer _Persia_ out in the stream, yesterday, beautifully smart, her flags flying, all her steam up, and she only waiting for her mails to slip away </s>
<s> She gave me a horrible touch of home-sickness </s>
<s> When the 1st of March arrives, and I can say "next month," I shall begin to grow brighter </s>
<s> A fortnight's reading in Boston, too (last week of February and first week of March), will help me on gaily, I hope (the work so far off tells) </s>
<s> It is impossible for the people to be more affectionately attached to a third, I really believe, than Fields and his wife are to me; and they are a landmark in the prospect </s>
<s> Dolby sends kindest regards, and wishes it to be known that he has not been bullied lately </s>
<s> We do _not_ go West at all, but take the easier plan </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BALTIMORE, _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 29th, 1868._ As I have an hour to spare, before starting to Philadelphia, I begin my letter this morning </s>
<s> It has been snowing hard for four-and-twenty hours, though this place is as far south as Valentia in Spain; and Dolby, being on his way to New York, has a good chance of being snowed up somewhere </s>
<s> They are a bright responsive people here, and very pleasant to read to </s>
<s> I have rarely seen so many fine faces in an audience </s>
<s> I read here in a charming little opera-house built by a society of Germans, quite a delightful place for the purpose </s>
<s> I stand on the stage, with a drop curtain down, and my screen before it </s>
<s> The whole scene is very pretty and complete, and the audience have a "ring" in them that sounds in the ear </s>
<s> I go from here to Philadelphia to read to-morrow night and Friday, come through here again on Saturday on my way to Washington, come back here on Saturday week for two finishing nights, then go to Philadelphia for two farewells, and so turn my back on the southern part of the country </s>
<s> Distances and travelling have obliged us to reduce the list of readings by two, leaving eighty-two in all </s>
<s> Of course we afterwards discovered that we had finally settled the list on a Friday </s>
<s> I shall be halfway through it at Washington, of course, on a Friday also, and my birthday </s>
<s> Dolby and Osgood, who do the most ridiculous things to keep me in spirits (I am often very heavy, and rarely sleep much), have decided to have a walking-match at Boston, on Saturday, February 29th </s>
<s> Beginning this design in joke, they have become tremendously in earnest, and Dolby has actually sent home (much to his opponent's terror) for a pair of seamless socks to walk in </s>
<s> Our men are hugely excited on the subject, and continually make bets on "the men" </s>
<s> Fields and I are to walk out six miles, and "the men" are to turn and walk round us </s>
<s> Neither of them has the least idea what twelve miles at a pace is </s>
<s> Being requested by both to give them "a breather" yesterday, I gave them a stiff one of five miles over a bad road in the snow, half the distance uphill </s>
<s> I took them at a pace of four miles and a half an hour, and you never beheld such objects as they were when we got back; both smoking like factories, and both obliged to change everything before they could come to dinner </s>
<s> They have the absurdest ideas of what are tests of walking power, and continually get up in the maddest manner and see _how high they can kick_ the wall </s>
<s> The wainscot here, in one place, is scored all over with their pencil-marks </s>
<s> To see them doing this--Dolby, a big man, and Osgood, a very little one, is ridiculous beyond description </s>
<s> PHILADELPHIA, _Same Night._ We came on here through a snowstorm all the way, but up to time </s>
<s> Fanny Kemble (who begins to read shortly) is coming to "Marigold" and "Trial" to-morrow night </s>
<s> I have written her a note, telling her that if it will at all assist _her_ movements to know _mine_, my list is at her service </s>
<s> Probably I shall see her to-morrow </s>
<s> Tell Mamie (to whom I will write next), with my love, that I found her letter of the 10th of this month awaiting me here </s>
<s> The _Siberia_ that brought it is a new Cunarder, and made an unusually slow passage out </s>
<s> Probably because it would be dangerous to work new machinery too fast on the Atlantic </s>
<s> _Thursday, 30th._ My cold still sticks to me </s>
<s> The heat of the railway cars and their unventilated condition invariably brings it back when I think it going </s>
<s> This morning my head is as stuffed and heavy as ever </s>
<s> A superb sledge and four horses have been offered me for a ride, but I am afraid to take it, lest I should make the "true American catarrh" worse, and should get hoarse </s>
<s> So I am going to give Osgood another "breather" on foot instead </s>
<s> The communication with New York is not interrupted, so we consider the zealous Dolby all right </s>
<s> You may imagine what his work is, when you hear that he goes three times to every place we visit </s>
<s> Firstly, to look at the hall, arrange the numberings, and make five hundred acquaintances, whom he immediately calls by their christian-names; secondly, to sell the tickets--a very nice business, requiring great tact and temper; thirdly, with me </s>
<s> He will probably turn up at Washington next Sunday, but only for a little while; for as soon as I am on the platform on Monday night, he will start away again, probably to be seen no more until we pass through New York in the middle of February </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Samuel Cartwright] BALTIMORE, _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 29th, 1868._ MY DEAR CARTWRIGHT, As I promised to report myself to you from this side of the Atlantic, and as I have some leisure this morning, I am going to lighten my conscience by keeping my word </s>
<s> I am going on at a great pace and with immense success </s>
<s> Next week, at Washington, I shall, please God, have got through half my readings </s>
<s> The remaining half are all arranged, and they will carry me into the third week of April </s>
<s> It is very hard work, but it is brilliantly paid </s>
<s> The changes that I find in the country generally (this place is the least changed of any I have yet seen) exceed my utmost expectations </s>
<s> I had been in New York a couple of days before I began to recognise it at all; and the handsomest part of Boston was a black swamp when I saw it five-and-twenty years ago </s>
<s> Considerable advances, too, have been made socially </s>
<s> Strange to say, the railways and railway arrangements (both exceedingly defective) seem to have stood still while all other things have been moving </s>
<s> One of the most comical spectacles I have ever seen in my life was "church," with a heavy sea on, in the saloon of the Cunard steamer coming out </s>
<s> The officiating minister, an extremely modest young man, was brought in between two big stewards, exactly as if he were coming up to the scratch in a prize-fight </s>
<s> The ship was rolling and pitching so, that the two big stewards had to stop and watch their opportunity of making a dart at the reading-desk with their reverend charge, during which pause he held on, now by one steward and now by the other, with the feeblest expression of countenance and no legs whatever </s>
<s> At length they made a dart at the wrong moment, and one steward was immediately beheld alone in the extreme perspective, while the other and the reverend gentleman _held on by the mast_ in the middle of the saloon--which the latter embraced with both arms, as if it were his wife </s>
<s> All this time the congregation was breaking up into sects and sliding away; every sect (as in nature) pounding the other sect </s>
<s> And when at last the reverend gentleman had been tumbled into his place, the desk (a loose one, put upon the dining-table) deserted from the church bodily, and went over to the purser </s>
<s> The scene was so extraordinarily ridiculous, and was made so much more so by the exemplary gravity of all concerned in it, that I was obliged to leave before the service began </s>
<s> This is one of the places where Butler carried it with so high a hand in the war, and where the ladies used to spit when they passed a Northern soldier </s>
<s> It still wears, I fancy, a look of sullen remembrance </s>
<s> (The ladies are remarkably handsome, with an Eastern look upon them, dress with a strong sense of colour, and make a brilliant audience.) The ghost of slavery haunts the houses; and the old, untidy, incapable, lounging, shambling black serves you as a free man </s>
<s> Free of course he ought to be; but the stupendous absurdity of making him a voter glares out of every roll of his eye, stretch of his mouth, and bump of his head </s>
<s> I have a strong impression that the race must fade out of the States very fast </s>
<s> It never can hold its own against a striving, restless, shifty people </s>
<s> In the penitentiary here, the other day, in a room full of all blacks (too dull to be taught any of the work in hand), was one young brooding fellow, very like a black rhinoceros </s>
<s> He sat glowering at life, as if it were just endurable at dinner time, until four of his fellows began to sing, most unmelodiously, a part song </s>
<s> He then set up a dismal howl, and pounded his face on a form </s>
<s> I took him to have been rendered quite desperate by having learnt anything </s>
<s> I send my kind regard to Mrs Cartwright, and sincerely hope that she and you have no new family distresses or anxieties </s>
<s> My standing address is the Westminster Hotel, Irving Place, New York City </s>
<s> And I am always, my dear Cartwright, Cordially yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PHILADELPHIA, _Friday, Jan </s>
<s> 31st, 1868._ Since writing to your aunt I have received yours of the 7th, and am truly glad to have the last news of you confirmed by yourself </s>
<s> From a letter Wilkie has written to me, it seems there can be no doubt that the "No Thoroughfare" drama is a real, genuine, and great success </s>
<s> It is drawing immensely, and seems to "go" with great effect and applause </s>
<s> "Doctor Marigold" here last night (for the first time) was an immense success, and all Philadelphia is going to rush at once for tickets for the two Philadelphian farewells the week after next </s>
<s> The tickets are to be sold to-morrow, and great excitement is anticipated in the streets </s>
<s> Dolby not being here, a clerk will sell, and will probably wish himself dead before he has done with it </s>
<s> It appears to me that Chorley[22] writes to you on the legacy question because he wishes you to understand that there is no danger of his changing his mind, and at the bottom I descry an honest desire to pledge himself as strongly as possible </s>
<s> You may receive it in that better spirit, or I am much mistaken </s>
<s> Tell your aunt, with my best love, that I wrote to Chauncey weeks ago, in answer to a letter from him </s>
<s> I am now going out in a sleigh (and four) with unconceivable dignity and grandeur; mentioning which reminds me that I am informed by trusty scouts that ---- intends to waylay me at Washington, and may even descend upon me in the train to-morrow </s>
<s> Best love to Katie, the two Charleys, and all </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] WASHINGTON, _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 4th, 1868._ I began here last night with great success </s>
<s> The hall being small, the prices were raised to three dollars each ticket </s>
<s> The audience was a superior one, composed of the foremost public men and their families </s>
<s> At the end of the "Carol" they gave a great break out, and applauded, I really believe, for five minutes </s>
<s> You would suppose them to be Manchester shillings instead of Washington half-sovereigns </s>
<s> Immense enthusiasm </s>
<s> A devoted adherent in this place (an Englishman) had represented to Dolby that if I were taken to an hotel here it would be impossible to secure me a minute's rest, and he undertook to get one Wheleker, a German, who keeps a little Vérey's, to furnish his private dining-rooms for the illustrious traveller's reception </s>
<s> Accordingly here we are, on the first and second floor of a small house, with no one else in it but our people, a French waiter, and a very good French cuisine </s>
<s> Perfectly private, in the city of all the world (I should say) where the hotels are intolerable, and privacy the least possible, and quite comfortable </s>
<s> "Wheleker's Restaurant" is our rather undignified address for the present week </s>
<s> I dined (against my rules) with Charles Sumner on Sunday, he having been an old friend of mine </s>
<s> Mr Secretary Staunton (War Minister) was there </s>
<s> He is a man of a very remarkable memory, and famous for his acquaintance with the minutest details of my books </s>
<s> Give him any passage anywhere, and he will instantly cap it and go on with the context </s>
<s> He was commander-in-chief of all the Northern forces concentrated here, and never went to sleep at night without first reading something from my books, which were always with him </s>
<s> I put him through a pretty severe examination, but he was better up than I was </s>
<s> The gas was very defective indeed last night, and I began with a small speech, to the effect that I must trust to the brightness of their faces for the illumination of mine; this was taken greatly </s>
<s> In the "Carol," a most ridiculous incident occurred all of a sudden </s>
<s> I saw a dog look out from among the seats into the centre aisle, and look very intently at me </s>
<s> The general attention being fixed on me, I don't think anybody saw the dog; but I felt so sure of his turning up again and barking, that I kept my eye wandering about in search of him </s>
<s> He was a very comic dog, and it was well for me that I was reading a very comic part of the book </s>
<s> But when he bounced out into the centre aisle again, in an entirely new place (still looking intently at me) and tried the effect of a bark upon my proceedings, I was seized with such a paroxysm of laughter, that it communicated itself to the audience, and we roared at one another loud and long </s>
<s> The President has sent to me twice, and I am going to see him to-morrow </s>
<s> He has a whole row for his family every night </s>
<s> Dolby rejoined his chief yesterday morning, and will probably remain in the august presence until Sunday night </s>
<s> He and Osgood, "training for the match," are ludicrous beyond belief </s>
<s> I saw them just now coming up a street, each trying to pass the other, and immediately fled </s>
<s> Since I have been writing this, they have burst in at the door and sat down on the floor to blow </s>
<s> Dolby is now writing at a neighbouring table, with his bald head smoking as if he were on fire </s>
<s> Kelly (his great adherent) asked me, when he was last away, whether it was quite fair that I should take Mr Osgood out for "breathers" when Mr Dolby had no such advantage </s>
<s> I begin to expect that half Boston will turn out on the 29th to see the match </s>
<s> In which case it will be unspeakably droll </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] WASHINGTON, _my Birthday_, 1868 </s>
<s> (_And my cold worse than ever._) This will be but a short letter, as I have been to see the President this morning, and have little time before the post goes </s>
<s> He had sent a gentleman to me, most courteously begging me to make my own appointment, and I did so </s>
<s> A man of very remarkable appearance indeed, of tremendous firmness of purpose </s>
<s> Not to be turned or trifled with </s>
<s> As I mention my cold's being so bad, I will add that I have never had anything the matter with me since I came here _but_ the cold </s>
<s> It is now in my throat, and slightly on my chest </s>
<s> It occasions me great discomfort, and you would suppose, seeing me in the morning, that I could not possibly read at night </s>
<s> But I have always come up to the scratch, have not yet missed one night, and have gradually got used to that </s>
<s> I had got much the better of it; but the dressing-room at the hall here is singularly cold and draughty, and so I have slid back again </s>
<s> The papers here having written about this being my birthday, the most exquisite flowers came pouring in at breakfast time from all sorts of people </s>
<s> The room is covered with them, made up into beautiful bouquets, and arranged in all manner of green baskets </s>
<s> Probably I shall find plenty more at the hall to-night </s>
<s> This is considered the dullest and most apathetic place in America </s>
<s> _My_ audiences have been superb </s>
<s> I mentioned the dog on the first night here </s>
<s> Next night I thought I heard (in "Copperfield") a suddenly suppressed bark </s>
<s> It happened in this wise: Osgood, standing just within the door, felt his leg touched, and looking down beheld the dog staring intently at me, and evidently just about to bark </s>
<s> In a transport of presence of mind and fury, he instantly caught him up in both hands and threw him over his own head out into the entry, where the check-takers received him like a game at ball </s>
<s> Last night he came again _with another dog_; but our people were so sharply on the look-out for him that he didn't get in </s>
<s> He had evidently promised to pass the other dog free </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BALTIMORE, U.S., _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 11th, 1868._ The weather has been desperately severe, and my cold quite as bad as ever </s>
<s> I couldn't help laughing at myself on my birthday at Washington </s>
<s> It was observed as much as though I were a little boy </s>
<s> Flowers and garlands (of the most exquisite kind) bloomed all over the room; letters radiant with good wishes poured in; a shirt pin, a handsome silver travelling bottle, a set of gold shirt studs, and a set of gold sleeve links were on the dinner-table </s>
<s> After "Boots," at night, the whole audience rose and remained (Secretaries of State, President's family, Judges of Supreme Court, and so forth) standing and cheering until I went back to the table and made them a little speech </s>
<s> On the same august day of the year I was received by the President, a man with a very remarkable and determined face </s>
<s> Each of us looked at each other very hard, and each of us managed the interview (I think) to the satisfaction of the other </s>
<s> In the outer room was sitting a certain sunburnt General Blair, with many evidences of the war upon him </s>
<s> He got up to shake hands with me, and then I found he had been out in the prairie with me five-and-twenty years ago </s>
<s> That afternoon my "catarrh" was in such a state that Charles Sumner, coming in at five o'clock and finding me covered with mustard poultice, and apparently voiceless, turned to Dolby and said: "Surely, Mr Dolby, it is impossible that he can read to-night" </s>
<s> Says Dolby: "Sir, I have told the dear Chief so four times to-day, and I have been very anxious </s>

<s> After five minutes of the little table, I was not (for the time) even hoarse </s>

<s> I wish you would get from Homan and report to me, as near as he can make, an approximate estimate is the right term in the trade, I believe, of the following work: 1 </s>
<s> To re-cover, with red leather, all the dining-room chairs </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> To ditto, with green leather, all the library chairs and the couch </s>
<s> 3 </s>
<s> To provide and lay down new _Brussels_ carpets in the front spare and the two top spares </s>

<s> I have some doubts about the state of the hall floor-cloth, and also the floor-cloth in the dining-room </s>

<s> It would seem that "No Thoroughfare" has really developed as a drama into an amazing success </s>
<s> I begin to think that I shall see it </s>
<s> Dolby is away this morning, to conquer or die in a terrific struggle with the Mayor of Newhaven (where I am to read next week), who has assailed him on a charge of false play in selling tickets </s>
<s> Osgood, my other keeper, stands at the table to take me out, and have a "breather" for the walking-match, so I must leave off </s>
<s> Think of my dreaming of Mrs Bouncer each night!! </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry Fielding Dickens.] BALTIMORE, U.S., _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 11th, 1868._ MY DEAR HARRY, I should have written to you before now, but for constant and arduous occupation </s>
<s> In reference to the cricket club's not being what it might be, I agree with you in the main </s>
<s> There are some things to be considered, however, which you have hardly taken into account </s>
<s> The first thing to be avoided is, the slightest appearance of patronage (one of the curses of England) </s>
<s> The second thing to be avoided is, the deprival of the men of their just right to manage their own affairs </s>
<s> I would rather have no club at all, than have either of these great mistakes made </s>
<s> The way out of them is this: Call the men together, and explain to them that the club might be larger, richer, and better </s>
<s> Say that you think that more of the neighbouring gentlemen could be got to be playing members </s>
<s> That you submit to them that it would be better to have a captain who could correspond with them, and talk to them, and in some sort manage them; and that, being perfectly acquainted with the game, and having long played it at a great public school, you propose yourself as captain, for the foregoing reasons </s>
<s> That you propose to them to make the subscription of the gentlemen members at least double that of the working men, for no other reason than that the gentlemen can afford it better; but that both classes of members shall have exactly the same right of voting equally in all that concerns the club </s>
<s> Say that you have consulted me upon the matter, and that I am of these opinions, and am ready to become chairman of the club, and to preside at their meetings, and to overlook its business affairs, and to give it five pounds a year, payable at the commencement of each season </s>
<s> Then, having brought them to this point, draw up the club's rules and regulations, amending them where they want amendment </s>
<s> Discreetly done, I see no difficulty in this </s>
<s> But it can only be honourably and hopefully done by having the men together </s>
<s> And I would not have them at The Falstaff, but in the hall or dining-room--the servants' hall, an excellent place </s>
<s> Whatever you do, let the men ratify; and let them feel their little importance, and at once perceive how much better the business begins to be done </s>
<s> I am very glad to hear of the success of your reading, and still more glad that you went at it in downright earnest </s>
<s> I should never have made my success in life if I had been shy of taking pains, or if I had not bestowed upon the least thing I have ever undertaken exactly the same attention and care that I have bestowed upon the greatest </s>
<s> Do everything at your best </s>
<s> It was but this last year that I set to and learned every word of my readings; and from ten years ago to last night, I have never read to an audience but I have watched for an opportunity of striking out something better somewhere </s>
<s> Look at such of my manuscripts as are in the library at Gad's, and think of the patient hours devoted year after year to single lines </s>
<s> * * * * * The weather is very severe here, and the work is very hard </s>
<s> Dolby, having been violently pitched into by the Mayor of Newhaven (a town at which I am to read next week), has gone bodily this morning with defiant written instructions from me to inform the said mayor that, if he fail to make out his case, he (Dolby) is to return all the money taken, and to tell him that I will not set foot in his jurisdiction; whereupon the Newhaven people will probably fall upon the mayor in his turn, and lead him a pleasant life </s>
<s> Ever, my dear Harry, your affectionate Father </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] PHILADELPHIA, _Thursday, Feb </s>
<s> 13th, 1868._ We have got into an immense difficulty with the people of Newhaven </s>
<s> I have a strong suspicion that one of our men (who sold there) has been speculating all this while, and that he must have put front seats in his pockets, and sold back ones </s>
<s> He denies what the mayor charges, but the mayor holds on grimly </s>
<s> Dolby set off from Baltimore as soon as we found out what was amiss, to examine and report; but some new feature of difficulty must have come out, for this morning he telegraphs from New York (where he had to sleep last night on his way to Newhaven), that he is coming back for further consultation with the Chief </s>
<s> It will certainly hurt us, and will of course be distorted by the papers into all manner of shapes </s>
<s> My suspicion _may not_ be correct, but I have an instinctive belief that it is </s>
<s> We shall probably have the old New York row (and loss) over again, unless I can catch this mayor tripping in an assertion </s>
<s> In this very place, we are half-distracted by the speculators </s>
<s> They have been holding out for such high prices, that the public have held out too; and now (frightened at what they have done) the speculators are trying to sell their worst seats at half the cost price, so that we are in the ridiculous situation of having sold the room out, and yet not knowing what empty seats there may be </s>
<s> _We_ could sell at our box-office to any extent; but _we_ can't buy back of the speculators, because we informed the public that all the tickets were gone </s>
<s> And if we bought _under_ our own price and _sold_ at our own price, we should at once be in treaty with the speculators, and should be making money by it </s>
<s> Dolby, the much bullied, will come back here presently, half bereft of his senses; and I should be half bereft of mine, if the situation were not comically disagreeable </s>
<s> Nothing will induce the people to believe in the farewells </s>
<s> At Baltimore on Tuesday night (a very brilliant night indeed), they asked as they came out: "When will Mr Dickens read here again" </s>
<s> "Never" </s>
<s> "Nonsense </s>
<s> Not come back, after such houses as these </s>
<s> Come </s>
<s> Say when he'll read again" </s>
<s> Just the same here </s>
<s> We could as soon persuade them that I am the President, as that I am going to read here, for the last time, to-morrow night </s>
<s> There is a child of the Barney Williams's in this house--a little girl--to whom I presented a black doll when I was here last </s>
<s> I have seen her eye at the keyhole since I began writing this, and I think she and the doll are outside still </s>
<s> "When you sent it up to me by the coloured boy," she said after receiving it (coloured boy is the term for black waiter), "I gave such a cream that ma came running in and creamed too, 'cos she fort I'd hurt myself </s>
<s> But I creamed a cream of joy" </s>
<s> _She_ had a friend to play with her that day, and brought the friend with her, to my infinite confusion </s>
<s> A friend all stockings, and much too tall, who sat on the sofa very far back, with her stockings sticking stiffly out in front of her, and glared at me and never spake word </s>
<s> Dolby found us confronted in a sort of fascination, like serpent and bird </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] NEW YORK, _Monday, Feb </s>
<s> 17th, 1868._ I got your letter of the 3rd of February here this morning </s>
<s> As I am off at seven to-morrow morning, I answer it at once, though indeed I have nothing to say </s>
<s> "True American" still sticking to me </s>
<s> But I am always ready for my work, and therefore don't much mind </s>
<s> Dolby and the Mayor of Newhaven alternately embrace and exchange mortal defiances </s>

<s> The walking-match (next Saturday week) is already in the Boston papers </s>
<s> I suppose half Boston will turn out on the occasion </s>
<s> As a sure way of not being conspicuous, "the men" are going to walk in flannel </s>

<s> Yesterday being a bright cool day, I took Dolby for a "buster" of eight miles </s>

<s> No doubt _that_ will be in the papers to-morrow </s>

<s> Mr and Mrs Fields, Do </s>

<s> My ship will not be the _Cuba_ after all </s>
<s> She is to go into dock, and the _Russia_ (a larger ship, and the latest built for the Cunard line) is to take her place </s>

<s> Best love to Mamie </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> Charles Fechter.] WASHINGTON, _February 24th, 1868._ MY DEAR FECHTER, Your letter reached me here yesterday </s>
<s> I have sent you a telegram (addressed to the theatre) this morning, and I write this by the earliest return mail </s>
<s> My dear fellow, consider yourself my representative </s>
<s> Whatever you do, or desire to do, about the play, I fully authorise beforehand </s>
<s> Tell Webster, with my regard, that I think his proposal honest and fair; that I think it, in a word, like himself; and that I have perfect confidence in his good faith and liberality </s>
<s> As to making money of the play in the United States here, Boucicault has filled Wilkie's head with golden dreams that have _nothing_ in them </s>
<s> He makes no account of the fact that, wherever I go, the theatres (with my name in big letters) instantly begin playing versions of my books, and that the moment the Christmas number came over here they pirated it and played "No Thoroughfare" </s>
<s> Now, I have enquired into the law, and am extremely doubtful whether I _could_ have prevented this </s>
<s> Why should they pay for the piece as you act it, when they have no actors, and when all they want is my name, and they can get that for nothing </s>
<s> Wilkie has uniformly written of you enthusiastically </s>
<s> In a letter I had from him, dated the 10th of January, he described your conception and execution of the part in the most glowing terms </s>
<s> "Here Fechter is magnificent" </s>
<s> "Here his superb playing brings the house down" </s>
<s> "I should call even his exit in the last act one of the subtlest and finest things he does in the piece" </s>
<s> "You can hardly imagine what he gets out of the part, or what he makes of his passionate love for Marguerite" </s>
<s> These expressions, and many others like them, crowded his letter </s>
<s> I never did so want to see a character played on the stage as I want to see you play Obenreizer </s>
<s> As the play was going when I last heard of it, I have some hopes that I MAY see it yet </s>

<s> Even in this place, I am really almost as much my own master as if I were in an English country town </s>

<s> They do not (I think) perceive touches of art to _be_ art; but they are responsive to the broad results of such touches </s>
<s> "Doctor Marigold" is a great favourite, and they laugh so unrestrainedly at "The Trial" from "Pickwick" (which you never heard), that it has grown about half as long again as it used to be </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BOSTON, _Tuesday, Feb </s>
<s> 25th, 1868._ It is so very difficult to know, by any exercise of common sense, what turn or height the political excitement may take next, and it may so easily, and so soon, swallow up all other things, that I think I shall suppress my next week's readings here (by good fortune not yet announced) and watch the course of events </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BOSTON, _Thursday, Feb </s>
<s> 27th, 1868._ This morning at breakfast I received yours of the 11th from Palace Gate House </s>
<s> I have very little news to give you in return for your budget </s>
<s> The walking-match is to come off on Saturday, and Fields and I went over the ground yesterday to measure the miles </s>
<s> We went at a tremendous pace </s>
<s> The condition of the ground is something indescribable, from half-melted snow, running water, and sheets and blocks of ice </s>
<s> The two performers have not the faintest notion of the weight of the task they have undertaken </s>

<s> After carefully considering the subject, I decided to take advantage of the fact that next week's four readings here have not yet been announced, and to abolish them altogether </s>

<s> The Boston audiences have come to regard the readings and the reader as their peculiar property; and you would be at once amused and pleased if you could see the curious way in which they seem to plume themselves on both </s>
<s> They have taken to applauding too whenever they laugh or cry, and the result is very inspiriting </s>
<s> I shall remain here until Saturday, the 7th, but shall not read here, after to-morrow night, until the 1st of April, when I begin my Boston farewells, six in number </s>
<s> _Friday, 28th._ It has been snowing all night, and the city is in a miserable condition </s>
<s> We had a fine house last night for "Carol" and "Trial," and such an enthusiastic one that they persisted in a call after the "Carol," and, while I was out, covered the little table with flowers </s>
<s> The "True American" has taken a fresh start, as if it were quite a novelty, and is on the whole rather worse than ever to-day </s>
<s> The Cunard packet, the _Australasian_ (a poor ship), is some days overdue, and Dolby is anxiously looking out for her </s>
<s> There is a lull in the excitement about the President, but the articles of impeachment are to be produced this afternoon, and then it may set in again </s>

<s> Some of those halls turn out to be smaller than represented, but I have no doubt, to use an American expression, that we shall "get along" </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BOSTON, _Monday, March 2nd, 1868._ A heavy gale of wind and a snowstorm oblige me to write suddenly for the Cunard steamer a day earlier than usual </s>
<s> The railroad between this and New York will probably be stopped somewhere </s>
<s> After all the hard weather we have had, this is the worst day we have seen </s>

<s> Charles Fechter.] SYRACUSE, U.S </s>
<s> OF AMERICA, _Sunday Night, March 8th, 1868._ MY DEAR FECHTER, I am here in a most wonderful out-of-the-world place, which looks as if it had begun to be built yesterday, and were going to be imperfectly knocked together with a nail or two the day after to-morrow </s>
<s> I am in the worst inn that ever was seen, and outside is a thaw that places the whole country under water </s>
<s> I have looked out of window for the people, and I can't find any people </s>
<s> I have tried all the wines in the house, and there are only two wines, for which you pay six shillings a bottle, or fifteen, according as you feel disposed to change the name of the thing you ask for </s>
<s> (The article never changes.) The bill of fare is "in French," and the principal article (the carte is printed) is "Paettie de shay" </s>
<s> I asked the Irish waiter what this dish was, and he said: "It was the name the steward giv' to oyster patties--the Frinch name" </s>
<s> These are the drinks you are to wash it down with: "Mooseux," "Abasinthe," "Curacco," "Marschine," "Annise," and "Margeaux" </s>
<s> I am growing very home-sick, and very anxious for the 22nd of April; on which day, please God, I embark for home </s>
<s> I am beginning to be tired, and have been depressed all the time (except when reading), and have lost my appetite </s>
<s> I cannot tell you--but you know, and therefore why should I?--how overjoyed I shall be to see you again, my dear boy, and how sorely I miss a dear friend, and how sorely I miss all art, in these parts </s>
<s> No disparagement to the country, which has a great future in reserve, or to its people, who are very kind to me </s>
<s> I mean to take my leave of readings in the autumn and winter, in a final series in England with Chappell </s>
<s> This will come into the way of literary work for a time, for, after I have rested--don't laugh--it is a grim reality--I shall have to turn my mind to--ha </s>
<s> ha </s>
<s> ha!--to--ha </s>
<s> ha </s>
<s> ha </s>
<s> (more sepulchrally than before)--the--the CHRISTMAS NUMBER!! </s>
<s> I feel as if I had murdered a Christmas number years ago (perhaps I did!) and its ghost perpetually haunted me </s>
<s> Nevertheless in some blessed rest at Gad's, we will talk over stage matters, and all matters, in an even way, and see what we can make of them, please God </s>
<s> Be sure that I shall not be in London one evening, after disembarking, without coming round to the theatre to embrace you, my dear fellow </s>
<s> I have had an American cold (the worst in the world) since Christmas Day </s>
<s> I read four times a week, with the most tremendous energy I can bring to bear upon it </s>
<s> I travel about pretty heavily </s>
<s> I am very resolute about calling on people, or receiving people, or dining out, and so save myself a great deal </s>
<s> I read in all sorts of places--churches, theatres, concert rooms, lecture halls </s>
<s> Every night I read I am described (mostly by people who have not the faintest notion of observing) from the sole of my boot to where the topmost hair of my head ought to be, but is not </s>
<s> Sometimes I am described as being "evidently nervous;" sometimes it is rather taken ill that "Mr Dickens is so extraordinarily composed" </s>
<s> My eyes are blue, red, grey, white, green, brown, black, hazel, violet, and rainbow-coloured </s>
<s> I am like "a well-to-do American gentleman," and the Emperor of the French, with an occasional touch of the Emperor of China, and a deterioration from the attributes of our famous townsman, Rufus W </s>
<s> B </s>
<s> D </s>
<s> Dodge Grumsher Pickville </s>
