<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> C </s>
<s> Macready.] SPRINGFIELD, MASS., _Saturday, March 21st, 1868._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, What with perpetual reading and travelling, what with a "true American catarrh" (on which I am complimented almost boastfully), and what with one of the severest winters ever known, your coals of fire received by the last mail did not burn my head so much as they might have done under less excusatory circumstances </s>
<s> But they scorched it too </s>
<s> You would find the general aspect of America and Americans decidedly much improved </s>
<s> You would find immeasurably greater consideration and respect for your privacy than of old </s>
<s> You would find a steady change for the better everywhere, except (oddly enough) in the railroads generally, which seem to have stood still, while everything else has moved </s>
<s> But there is an exception westward </s>
<s> There the express trains have now a very delightful carriage called a "drawing-room car," literally a series of little private drawing-rooms, with sofas and a table in each, opening out of a little corridor </s>
<s> In each, too, is a large plate-glass window, with which you can do as you like </s>
<s> As you pay extra for this luxury, it may be regarded as the first move towards two classes of passengers </s>
<s> When the railroad straight away to San Francisco (in six days) shall be opened through, it will not only have these drawing-rooms, but sleeping-rooms too; a bell in every little apartment communicating with a steward's pantry, a restaurant, a staff of servants, marble washing-stands, and a barber's shop </s>
<s> I looked into one of these cars a day or two ago, and it was very ingeniously arranged and quite complete </s>
<s> I left Niagara last Sunday, and travelled on to Albany, through three hundred miles of flood, villages deserted, bridges broken, fences drifting away, nothing but tearing water, floating ice, and absolute wreck and ruin </s>
<s> The train gave in altogether at Utica, and the passengers were let loose there for the night </s>
<s> As I was due at Albany, a very active superintendent of works did all he could to "get Mr Dickens along," and in the morning we resumed our journey through the water, with a hundred men in seven-league boots pushing the ice from before us with long poles </s>
<s> How we got to Albany I can't say, but we got there somehow, just in time for a triumphal "Carol" and "Trial" </s>
<s> All the tickets had been sold, and we found the Albanians in a state of great excitement </s>
<s> You may imagine what the flood was when I tell you that we took the passengers out of two trains that had their fires put out by the water four-and-twenty hours before, and cattle from trucks that had been in the water I don't know how long, but so long that the sheep had begun to eat each other </s>
<s> It was a horrible spectacle, and the haggard human misery of their faces was quite a new study </s>
<s> There was a fine breath of spring in the air concurrently with the great thaw; but lo and behold </s>
<s> last night it began to snow again with a strong wind, and to-day a snowdrift covers this place with all the desolation of winter once more </s>
<s> I never was so tired of the sight of snow </s>
<s> As to sleighing, I have been sleighing about to that extent, that I am sick of the sound of a sleigh-bell </s>
<s> I have seen all our Boston friends, except Curtis </s>
<s> Ticknor is dead </s>
<s> The rest are very little changed, except that Longfellow has a perfectly white flowing beard and long white hair </s>
<s> But he does not otherwise look old, and is infinitely handsomer than he was </s>
<s> I have been constantly with them all, and they have always talked much of you </s>
<s> It is the established joke that Boston is my "native place," and we hold all sorts of hearty foregatherings </s>
<s> They all come to every reading, and are always in a most delightful state of enthusiasm </s>
<s> They give me a parting dinner at the club, on the Thursday before Good Friday </s>
<s> To pass from Boston personal to New York theatrical, I will mention here that one of the proprietors of my New York hotel is one of the proprietors of Niblo's, and the most active </s>
<s> Consequently I have seen the "Black Crook" and the "White Fawn," in majesty, from an arm-chair in the first entrance, P.S., more than once </s>
<s> Of these astonishing dramas, I beg to report (seriously) that I have found no human creature "behind" who has the slightest idea what they are about (upon my honour, my dearest Macready!), and that having some amiable small talk with a neat little Spanish woman, who is the _première danseuse_, I asked her, in joke, to let me measure her skirt with my dress glove </s>
<s> Holding the glove by the tip of the forefinger, I found the skirt to be just three gloves long, and yet its length was much in excess of the skirts of two hundred other ladies, whom the carpenters were at that moment getting into their places for a transformation scene, on revolving columns, on wires and "travellers" in iron cradles, up in the flies, down in the cellars, on every description of float that Wilmot, gone distracted, could imagine </s>
<s> I have taken my passage for Liverpool from New York in the Cunarder _Russia_, on the 22nd of April </s>
<s> I had the second officer's cabin on deck coming out, and I have the chief steward's cabin on deck going home, because it will be on the sunny side of the ship </s>
<s> I have experienced nothing here but good humour and cordiality </s>
<s> In the autumn and winter I have arranged with Chappells to take my farewell of reading in the United Kingdom for ever and ever </s>
<s> I am delighted to hear of Benvenuta's marriage, and I think her husband a very lucky man </s>
<s> Johnnie has my profound sympathy under his examinatorial woes </s>
<s> The noble boy will give me Gavazzi revised and enlarged, I expect, when I next come to Cheltenham </s>
<s> I will give you and Mrs Macready all my American experiences when you come to London, or, better still, to Gad's </s>
<s> Meanwhile I send my hearty love to all, not forgetting dear Katie </s>
<s> Niagara is not at all spoiled by a very dizzy-looking suspension bridge </s>
<s> Is to have another still nearer to the Horse-shoe opened in July </s>
<s> My last sight of that scene (last Sunday) was thus: We went up to the rapids above the Horse-shoe--say two miles from it--and through the great cloud of spray </s>
<s> Everything in the magnificent valley--buildings, forest, high banks, air, water, everything--was _made of rainbow_ </s>
<s> Turner's most imaginative drawing in his finest day has nothing in it so ethereal, so gorgeous in fancy, so celestial </s>
<s> We said to one another (Dolby and I), "Let it for evermore remain so," and shut our eyes and came away </s>
<s> God bless you and all dear to you, my dear old Friend </s>
<s> I am ever your affectionate and loving </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] PORTLAND, _Sunday, March 29th, 1868._ I should have written to you by the last mail, but I really was too unwell to do it </s>
<s> The writing day was last Friday, when I ought to have left Boston for New Bedford (fifty-five miles) before eleven in the morning </s>
<s> But I was so exhausted that I could not be got up, and had to take my chance of an evening's train producing me in time to read, which it just did </s>
<s> With the return of snow, nine days ago, the "true American" (which had lulled) came back as bad as ever </s>
<s> I have coughed from two or three in the morning until five or six, and have been absolutely sleepless </s>
<s> I have had no appetite besides, and no taste </s>
<s> Last night here I took some laudanum, and it is the only thing that has done me good </s>
<s> But the life in this climate is so very hard </s>
<s> When I did manage to get from Boston to New Bedford, I read with my utmost force and vigour </s>
<s> Next morning, well or ill, I must turn out at seven to get back to Boston on my way here </s>
<s> I dine at Boston at three, and at five must come on here (a hundred and thirty miles or so), for to-morrow night; there being no Sunday train </s>
<s> To-morrow night I read here in a very large place, and Tuesday morning at six I must start again to get back to Boston once more </s>
<s> But after to-morrow night, I have only the Boston and New York farewells, thank God </s>
<s> I am most grateful to think that when we came to devise the details of the tour, I foresaw that it could never be done, as Dolby and Osgood proposed, by one unassisted man, as if he were a machine </s>
<s> If I had not cut out the work, and cut out Canada, I could never have gone there, I am quite sure </s>
<s> Even as it is, I have just now written to Dolby (who is in New York), to see my doctor there, and ask him to send me some composing medicine that I can take at night, inasmuch as without sleep I cannot get through </s>
<s> However sympathetic and devoted the people are about me, they _can not_ be got to comprehend that one's being able to do the two hours with spirit when the time comes round, may be co-existent with the consciousness of great depression and fatigue </s>
<s> I don't mind saying all this, now that the labour is so nearly over </s>
<s> You shall have a brighter account of me, please God, when I close this at Boston </s>
<s> _Monday, March 30th._ Without any artificial aid, I got a splendid night's rest last night, and consequently am very much freshened up to-day </s>
<s> Yesterday I had a fine walk by the sea, and to-day I have had another on the heights overlooking it </s>
<s> BOSTON, _Tuesday, 31st._ I have safely arrived here, just in time to add a line to that effect, and get this off by to-morrow's English mail from New York </s>
<s> Catarrh rather better </s>
<s> Everything triumphant last night, except no sleep again </s>
<s> I suppose Dolby to be now on his way back to join me here </s>
<s> I am much mistaken if the political crisis do not damage the farewells by almost one half </s>
<s> I hope that I am certainly better altogether </s>
<s> My room well decorated with flowers, of course, and Mr and Mrs Fields coming to dinner </s>
<s> They are the most devoted of friends, and never in the way and never out of it </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BOSTON, _Wednesday, April 1st, 1868._ I received your letter of from the 14th to the 17th of March, here, last night </s>
<s> My New York doctor has prescribed for me promptly, and I hope I am better </s>
<s> I am certainly no worse </s>
<s> We shall do (to the best of my belief) _very well_ with the farewells here and at New York, but not greatly </s>
<s> Everything is at a standstill, pending the impeachment and the next presidential election </s>
<s> I forgot whether I told you that the New York press are going to give me a public dinner, on Saturday, the 18th </s>
<s> I hear (but not from himself) that Wills has had a bad fall in hunting, and is, or has been, laid up </s>
<s> I am supposed, I take it, not to know this until I hear it from himself </s>
<s> _Thursday._ My notion of the farewells is pretty certain now to turn out right </s>
<s> It is not at all probable that we shall do anything enormous </s>
<s> Every pulpit in Massachusetts will resound to violent politics to-day and to-night </s>
<s> You remember the Hutchinson family?[24] I have had a grateful letter from John Hutchinson </s>
<s> He speaks of "my sister Abby" as living in New York </s>
<s> The immediate object of his note is to invite me to the marriage of his daughter, twenty-one years of age </s>
<s> You will see by the evidence of this piece of paper that I am using up my stationery </s>
<s> Scott has just been making anxious calculations as to our powers of holding out in the articles of tooth-powder, etc The calculations encourage him to believe that we shall just hold out, and no more </s>
<s> I think I am still better to-day than I was yesterday; but I am far from strong, and have no appetite </s>
<s> To see me at my little table at night, you would think me the freshest of the fresh </s>
<s> And this is the marvel of Fields' life </s>

<s> _Friday Afternoon, 3rd._ Catarrh worse than ever </s>
<s> And we don't know (at four) whether I can read to-night or must stop </s>
<s> Otherwise all well </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] BOSTON, _Tuesday, April 7th, 1868._ I not only read last Friday, when I was doubtful of being able to do so, but read as I never did before, and astonished the audience quite as much as myself </s>
<s> You never saw or heard such a scene of excitement </s>
<s> Longfellow and all the Cambridge men urged me to give in </s>
<s> I have been very near doing so, but feel stronger to-day </s>
<s> I cannot tell whether the catarrh may have done me any lasting injury in the lungs or other breathing organs, until I shall have rested and got home </s>
<s> I hope and believe not </s>
<s> Consider the weather </s>
<s> There have been two snowstorms since I wrote last, and to-day the town is blotted out in a ceaseless whirl of snow and wind </s>
<s> I cannot eat (to anything like the ordinary extent), and have established this system: At seven in the morning, in bed, a tumbler of new cream and two tablespoonsful of rum </s>
<s> At twelve, a sherry cobbler and a biscuit </s>
<s> At three (dinner time), a pint of champagne </s>
<s> At five minutes to eight, an egg beaten up with a glass of sherry </s>
<s> Between the parts, the strongest beef tea that can be made, drunk hot </s>
<s> At a quarter-past ten, soup, and anything to drink that I can fancy </s>
<s> I don't eat more than half a pound of solid food in the whole four-and-twenty hours, if so much </s>
<s> If I hold out, as I hope to do, I shall be greatly pressed in leaving here and getting over to New York before next Saturday's mail from there </s>
<s> Do not, therefore, _if all be well_, expect to hear from me by Saturday's mail, but look for my last letter from America by the mail of the following Wednesday, the 15th </s>
<s> _Be sure_ that you shall hear, however, by Saturday's mail, if I should knock up as to reading </s>
<s> I am tremendously "beat," but I feel really and unaffectedly so much stronger to-day, both in my body and hopes, that I am much encouraged </s>
<s> I have a fancy that I turned my worst time last night </s>
<s> Dolby is as tender as a woman and as watchful as a doctor </s>
<s> He never leaves me during the reading now, but sits at the side of the platform and keeps his eye upon me all the time </s>
<s> Ditto George, the gasman, steadiest and most reliable man I ever employed </s>
<s> I am the more hopeful of my not having to relinquish a reading, because last night was "Copperfield" and "Bob"--by a quarter of an hour the longest, and, in consideration of the storm, by very much the most trying </s>
<s> Yet I was far fresher afterwards than I have been these three weeks </s>
<s> I have "Dombey" to do to-night, and must go through it carefully; so here ends my report </s>
<s> The personal affection of the people in this place is charming to the last </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The Hon </s>
<s> Mrs Watson.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, _Monday, May 11th, 1868._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> WATSON, I am delighted to have your letter </s>
<s> It comes to me like a faithful voice from dear old Rockingham, and awakens many memories </s>
<s> The work in America has been so very hard, and the winter there has been so excessively severe, that I really have been very unwell for some months </s>
<s> But I had not been at sea three days on the passage home when I became myself again </s>
<s> If you will arrange with Mary Boyle any time for coming here, we shall be charmed to see you, and I will adapt my arrangements accordingly </s>
<s> I make this suggestion because she generally comes here early in the summer season </s>
<s> But if you will propose yourself _anyhow_, giving me a margin of a few days in case of my being pre-engaged for this day or that, we will (as my American friends say) "fix it" </s>
<s> What with travelling, reading night after night, and speech-making day after day, I feel the peace of the country beyond all expression </s>
<s> On board ship coming home, a "deputation" (two in number, of whom only one could get into my cabin, while the other looked in at my window) came to ask me to read to the passengers that evening in the saloon </s>
<s> I respectfully replied that sooner than do it, I would assault the captain, and be put in irons </s>
<s> Ever affectionately yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs George Cattermole.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Saturday, May 16th, 1868._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> CATTERMOLE, On my return from America just now, I accidentally heard that George had been ill </s>
<s> My sister-in-law had heard it from Forster, but vaguely </s>
<s> Until I received your letter of Wednesday's date, I had no idea that he had been very ill; and should have been greatly shocked by knowing it, were it not for the hopeful and bright assurance you give me that he is greatly better </s>
<s> My old affection for him has never cooled </s>
<s> The last time he dined with me, I asked him to come again that day ten years, for I was perfectly certain (this was my small joke) that I should not set eyes upon him sooner </s>
<s> The time being fully up, I hope you will remind him, with my love, that he is due </s>
<s> His hand is upon these walls here, so I should like him to see for himself, and _you_ to see for _yourself_, and in this hope I shall pursue his complete recovery </s>
<s> I heartily sympathise with you in your terrible anxiety, and in your vast relief; and, with many thanks for your letter, am ever, my dear Mrs Cattermole, Affectionately yours </s>

<s> Macready.] GAD'S HILL, _Wednesday, June 10th, 1868._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, Since my return from America, I have been so overwhelmed with business that I have not had time even to write to you </s>
<s> You may imagine what six months of arrear are to dispose of; added to this, Wills has received a concussion of the brain (from an accident in the hunting-field), and is sent away by the doctors, and strictly prohibited from even writing a note </s>
<s> Consequently all the business and money details of "All the Year Round" devolve upon me </s>
<s> And I have had to get them up, for I have never had experience of them </s>
<s> Then I am suddenly entreated to go to Paris, to look after the French version of "No Thoroughfare" on the stage </s>
<s> And I go, and come back, leaving it a great success </s>
<s> I hope Mrs Macready and you have not abandoned the idea of coming here </s>
<s> The expression of this hope is the principal, if not the only, object of this present note </s>
<s> May the amiable secretary vouchsafe a satisfactory reply </s>
<s> Katie, Mary, and Georgina send their very best love to your Katie and Mrs Macready </s>
<s> The undersigned is in his usual brilliant condition, and indeed has greatly disappointed them at home here, by coming back "so brown and looking so well" </s>
<s> They expected a wreck, and were, at first, much mortified </s>
<s> But they are getting over it now </s>
<s> To my particular friends, the noble boy and Johnny, I beg to be warmly remembered </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mrs Henry Austin.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Tuesday, July 21st, 1868._ ON THE DEATH OF MR </s>
<s> HENRY AUSTIN.[25] MY DEAR LETITIA, You will have had a telegram from me to-day </s>
<s> I received your sad news by this morning's post </s>
<s> They never, without express explanation, mind "Immediate" on a letter addressed to the office, because half the people who write there on business that does not press, or on no business at all, so mark their letters </s>
<s> On Thursday I have people to see and matters to attend to, both at the office and at Coutts', which, in Wills's absence, I cannot forego or depute to another </s>
<s> But, _between ourselves_, I must add something else: I have the greatest objection to attend a funeral in which my affections are not strongly and immediately concerned </s>
<s> I have no notion of a funeral as a matter of form or ceremony </s>
<s> And just as I should expressly prohibit the summoning to my own burial of anybody who was not very near or dear to me, so I revolt from myself appearing at that solemn rite unless the deceased were very near or dear to me </s>
<s> I cannot endure being dressed up by an undertaker as part of his trade show </s>
<s> I was not in this poor good fellow's house in his lifetime, and I feel that I have no business there when he lies dead in it </s>
<s> My mind is penetrated with sympathy and compassion for the young widow, but that feeling is a real thing, and my attendance as a mourner would not be--to myself </s>
<s> It would be to you, I know, but it would not be to myself </s>
<s> I know full well that you cannot delegate to me your memories of and your associations with the deceased, and the more true and tender they are the more invincible is my objection to become a form in the midst of the most awful realities </s>
<s> With love and condolence from Georgina, Mary, and Katie, Believe me, ever your affectionate Brother </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> H </s>
<s> Wills.] _Friday, July 31st, 1868._ MY DEAR WILLS, I had such a hard day at the office yesterday, that I had not time to write to you before I left </s>
<s> So I write to-day </s>
<s> I am very unwilling to abandon the Christmas number, though even in the case of my little Christmas books (which were immensely profitable) I let the idea go when I thought it was wearing out </s>
<s> Ever since I came home, I have hammered at it, more or less, and have been uneasy about it </s>
<s> I have begun something which is very droll, but it manifestly shapes itself towards a book, and could not in the least admit of even that shadowy approach to a congruous whole on the part of other contributors which they have ever achieved at the best </s>
<s> I have begun something else (aboard the American mail-steamer); but I don't like it, because the stories must come limping in after the old fashion, though, of course, what I _have_ done will be good for A </s>
<s> Y </s>
<s> R </s>
<s> In short, I have cast about with the greatest pains and patience, and I have been wholly unable to find what I want </s>
<s> And yet I cannot quite make up my mind to give in without another fight for it </s>
<s> I offered one hundred pounds reward at Gad's to anybody who could suggest a notion to satisfy me </s>
<s> Charles Collins suggested one yesterday morning, in which there is _something_, though not much </s>
<s> I will turn it over and over, and try a few more starts on my own account </s>
<s> Finally, I swear I will not give it up until August is out </s>
<s> Vow registered </s>
<s> I am clear that a number by "various writers" would not do </s>
<s> If we have not the usual sort of number, we must call the current number for that date the Christmas number, and make it as good as possible </s>
<s> I sit in the Châlet,[26] like Mariana in the Moated Grange, and to as much purpose </s>
<s> I am buying the freehold of the meadow at Gad's, and of an adjoining arable field, so that I shall now have about eight-and-twenty freehold acres in a ring-fence </s>
<s> No more now </s>
<s> I made up a very good number yesterday </s>
<s> You will see in it a very short article that I have called "Now" </s>
<s> which is a highly remarkable piece of description </s>
<s> It is done by a new man, from whom I have accepted another article; but he will never do anything so good again </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Wednesday, Aug </s>
<s> 26th, 1868._ MY DEAR CERJAT, I was happy to receive your esteemed letter a few days ago </s>
<s> The severity of the winter in America (which was quite exceptional even in that rigorous climate), combined with the hard work I had to do, tried me a good deal </s>
<s> Neuralgia and colds beset me, either by turns or both together, and I had often much to do to get through at night </s>
<s> But the sea voyage home again did wonders in restoring me, and I have been very well indeed, though a little fatigued, ever since </s>
<s> I am now preparing for a final reading campaign in England, Scotland, and Ireland </s>
<s> It will begin on the 6th of October, and will probably last, with short occasional intermissions, until June </s>
<s> The great subject in England for the moment is the horrible accident to the Irish mail-train </s>
<s> It is now supposed that the petroleum (known to be a powerful anæsthetic) rendered the unfortunate people who were burnt almost instantly insensible to any sensation </s>
<s> My escape in the Staplehurst accident of three years ago is not to be obliterated from my nervous system </s>
<s> To this hour I have sudden vague rushes of terror, even when riding in a hansom cab, which are perfectly unreasonable but quite insurmountable </s>
<s> I used to make nothing of driving a pair of horses habitually through the most crowded parts of London </s>
<s> I cannot now drive, with comfort to myself, on the country roads here; and I doubt if I could ride at all in the saddle </s>
<s> My reading secretary and companion knows so well when one of these odd momentary seizures comes upon me in a railway carriage, that he instantly produces a dram of brandy, which rallies the blood to the heart and generally prevails </s>
<s> I forget whether I ever told you that my watch (a chronometer) has never gone exactly since the accident </s>
<s> So the Irish catastrophe naturally revives the dreadful things I saw that day </s>
<s> The only other news here you know as well as I; to wit, that the country is going to be ruined, and that the Church is going to be ruined, and that both have become so used to being ruined, that they will go on perfectly well </s>
<s> * * * * * [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," NO </s>
<s> 26, WELLINGTON STREET, STRAND, LONDON, W.C., _Saturday, Sept </s>
<s> 26th, 1868._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, I will add a line to this at the Athenæum, after seeing Plorn off, to tell you how he went away </s>
<s> ATHENÆUM, _Quarter to Six._ I can honestly report that he went away, poor dear fellow, as well as could possibly be expected </s>
<s> He was pale, and had been crying, and (Harry said) had broken down in the railway carriage after leaving Higham station; but only for a short time </s>
<s> Just before the train started he cried a good deal, but not painfully </s>
<s> (Tell dear Georgy that I bought him his cigars.) These are hard, hard things, but they might have to be done without means or influence, and then they would be far harder </s>

<s> REPLY TO A PROPOSAL MADE THROUGH ALEXANDER RUSSEL, OF "THE SCOTSMAN," THAT HE SHOULD ALLOW HIMSELF TO BE PUT FORWARD AS A CANDIDATE FOR THE REPRESENTATION OF EDINBURGH </s>

<s> D </s>
<s> Finlay.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Sunday, Oct </s>
<s> 4th, 1868._ MY DEAR FINLAY, I am much obliged to you in all friendship and sincerity for your letter </s>
<s> I have a great respect for your father-in-law and his paper, and I am much attached to the Edinburgh people </s>
<s> You may suppose, therefore, that if my mind were not fully made up on the parliamentary question, I should waver now </s>
<s> But my conviction that I am more useful and more happy as I am than I could ever be in Parliament is not to be shaken </s>
<s> I considered it some weeks ago, when I had a stirring proposal from the Birmingham people, and I then set it up on a rock for ever and a day </s>
<s> Do tell Mr Russel that I truly feel this mark of confidence, and that I hope to acknowledge it in person in Edinburgh before Christmas </s>
<s> There is no man in Scotland from whom I should consider his suggestion a greater honour </s>
<s> Ever yours </s>

<s> We had a very fine and enthusiastic audience in the Free Trade Hall, at Manchester, on Saturday; but our first nights there never count up in money, as the rest do </s>
<s> Yesterday, "Charlotte," Sainton, and Piatti stayed with us here; and they went on to Hull this morning </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr Henry Fielding Dickens.] ADELPHI HOTEL, LIVERPOOL, _Thursday, Oct </s>
<s> 15th, 1868._ MY DEAR HARRY, I have your letter here this morning </s>
<s> I enclose you another cheque for twenty-five pounds, and I write to London by this post, ordering three dozen sherry, two dozen port, and three dozen light claret, to be sent down to you </s>
<s> Now, observe attentively </s>
<s> We must have no shadow of debt </s>
<s> Square up everything whatsoever that it has been necessary to buy </s>
<s> Let not a farthing be outstanding on any account, when we begin together with your allowance </s>
<s> Be particular in the minutest detail </s>
<s> I wish to have no secret from you in the relations we are to establish together, and I therefore send you Joe Chitty's letter bodily </s>
<s> Reading it, you will know exactly what I know, and will understand that I treat you with perfect confidence </s>
<s> It appears to me that an allowance of two hundred and fifty pounds a year will be handsome for all your wants, if I send you your wines </s>
<s> I mean this to include your tailor's bills as well as every other expense; and I strongly recommend you to buy nothing in Cambridge, and to take credit for nothing but the clothes with which your tailor provides you </s>
<s> As soon as you have got your furniture accounts in, let us wipe all those preliminary expenses clean out, and I will then send you your first quarter </s>
<s> We will count in it October, November, and December; and your second quarter will begin with the New Year </s>
<s> If you dislike, at first, taking charge of so large a sum as sixty-two pounds ten shillings, you can have your money from me half-quarterly </s>
<s> You know how hard I work for what I get, and I think you know that I never had money help from any human creature after I was a child </s>
<s> You know that you are one of many heavy charges on me, and that I trust to your so exercising your abilities and improving the advantages of your past expensive education, as soon to diminish _this_ charge </s>
<s> I say no more on that head </s>
<s> Whatever you do, above all other things keep out of debt and confide in me </s>
<s> If you ever find yourself on the verge of any perplexity or difficulty, come to me </s>
<s> You will never find me hard with you while you are manly and truthful </s>
<s> As your brothers have gone away one by one, I have written to each of them what I am now going to write to you </s>
<s> You know that you have never been hampered with religious forms of restraint, and that with mere unmeaning forms I have no sympathy </s>
<s> But I most strongly and affectionately impress upon you the priceless value of the New Testament, and the study of that book as the one unfailing guide in life </s>
<s> Deeply respecting it, and bowing down before the character of our Saviour, as separated from the vain constructions and inventions of men, you cannot go very wrong, and will always preserve at heart a true spirit of veneration and humility </s>
<s> Similarly I impress upon you the habit of saying a Christian prayer every night and morning </s>
<s> These things have stood by me all through my life, and remember that I tried to render the New Testament intelligible to you and lovable by you when you were a mere baby </s>
<s> And so God bless you </s>
<s> Ever your affectionate Father </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr William Charles Kent.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Monday, Nov </s>
<s> 16th, 1868._ MY DEAR KENT, I was on the eve of writing to you </s>
<s> We thought of keeping the trial private; but Oxenford has suggested to Chappell that he would like to take the opportunity of to-morrow night's reading, of saying something about "Oliver" in _Wednesday's paper_ </s>
<s> Chappell has told Levy of this, and also Mr Tompkin, of _The Post_, who was there </s>
<s> Consequently, on Wednesday evening your charming article can come out to the best advantage </s>
<s> You have no idea of the difficulty of getting in the end of Sikes </s>
<s> As to the man with the invaluable composition </s>
<s> my dear fellow, believe me, no audience on earth could be held for ten minutes after the girl's death </s>
<s> Give them time, and they would be revengeful for having had such a strain put upon them </s>
<s> Trust me to be right </s>
<s> I stand there, and I know </s>
<s> Concerning Harry, I like to guide the boys to a distinct choice, rather than to press it on them </s>
<s> That will be my course as to the Middle Temple, of which I think as you do </s>
<s> With cordial thanks for every word in your letter, Affectionately yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mrs F </s>
<s> Lehmann.] KENNEDY'S HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Sunday, Dec </s>
<s> 6th, 1868._ MY DEAR MRS </s>
<s> LEHMANN, I hope you will see Nancy with the light of a great audience upon her some time between this and May; always supposing that she should not prove too weird and woeful for the general public </s>
<s> You know the aspect of this city on a Sunday, and how gay and bright it is </s>
<s> The merry music of the blithe bells, the waving flags, the prettily-decorated houses with their draperies of various colours, and the radiant countenances at the windows and in the streets, how charming they are </s>
<s> The usual preparations are making for the band in the open air, in the afternoon; and the usual pretty children (selected for that purpose) are at this moment hanging garlands round the Scott monument, preparatory to the innocent Sunday dance round that edifice, with which the diversions invariably close </s>
<s> It is pleasant to think that these customs were themselves of the early Christians, those early birds who _didn't_ catch the worm--and nothing else--and choke their young with it </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] KENNEDY'S HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Sunday, Dec </s>
<s> 6th, 1868._ We got down here to our time to the moment; and, considering the length of the journey, very easily </s>
<s> I made a calculation on the road, that the railway travelling over such a distance involves something more than thirty thousand shocks to the nerves </s>
<s> Dolby didn't like it at all </s>
<s> The signals for a gale were up at Berwick, and along the road between there and here </s>
<s> It came on just as we arrived, and blew tremendously hard all night </s>
<s> The wind is still very high, though the sky is bright and the sun shining </s>
<s> We couldn't sleep for the noise </s>
<s> We are very comfortably quartered </s>
<s> I fancy that the "business" will be on the whole better here than in Glasgow, where trade is said to be very bad </s>
<s> But I think I shall be pretty correct in both places as to the run being on the final readings </s>
<s> We are going up Arthur's Seat presently, which will be a pull for our fat friend </s>
<s> Scott, in a new Mephistopheles hat, baffles imagination and description </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr W </s>
<s> Wilkie Collins.] KENNEDY'S HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Tuesday, Dec </s>
<s> 8th, 1868._ MY DEAR WILKIE, I am hard at it here as usual, though with an audience so finely perceptive that the labour is much diminished </s>
<s> I have got together in a very short space the conclusion of "Oliver Twist" that you suggested, and am trying it daily with the object of rising from that blank state of horror into a fierce and passionate rush for the end </s>
<s> As yet I cannot make a certain effect of it; but when I shall have gone over it as many score of times as over the rest of that reading, perhaps I may strike one out </s>
<s> I shall be very glad to hear when you have done your play, and I _am_ glad to hear that you like the steamer </s>
<s> I agree with you about the reading perfectly </s>
<s> In No </s>
<s> 3 you will see an exact account of some places I visited at Ratcliffe </s>
<s> There are two little instances in it of something comic rising up in the midst of the direst misery, that struck me very humorously at the time </s>
<s> As I have determined not to do the "Oliver Murder" until after the 5th of January, when I shall ascertain its effect on a great audience, it is curious to notice how the shadow of its coming affects the Scotch mind </s>
<s> There was such a disposition to hold back for it here (until I return to finish in February) that we had next to no "let" when we arrived </s>
<s> It all came with a rush yesterday </s>
<s> They gave me a most magnificent welcome back from America last night </s>
<s> I am perpetually counting the weeks before me to be "read" through, and am perpetually longing for the end of them; and yet I sometimes wonder whether I shall miss something when they are over </s>
<s> It is a very, very bad day here, very dark and very wet </s>
<s> Dolby is over at Glasgow, and I am sitting at a side window looking up the length of Prince's Street, watching the mist change over the Castle and murdering Nancy by turns </s>
<s> Ever affectionately </s>
<s> P.S.--I have read the whole of Fitzgerald's "Zero," and the idea is exceedingly well wrought out </s>

<s> 12th, 1868._ I send another _Scotsman_ by this post, because it is really a good newspaper, well written, and well managed </s>

<s> We have four guests to dinner to-day: Peter Fraser, Ballantyne, John Blackwood, and Mr Russel </s>
<s> Immense preparations are making in the establishment, "on account," Mr Kennedy says, "of a' four yon chiels being chiels wha' ken a guid dinner" </s>

<s> My voice holds out splendidly so far, and I have had no return of the American </s>
<s> But I sleep very indifferently indeed </s>
<s> It blew appallingly here the night before last, but the wind has since shifted northward, and it is now bright and cold </s>
<s> The _Star of Hope_, that picked up those shipwrecked people in the boat, came into Leith yesterday, and was received with tremendous cheers </s>
<s> Her captain must be a good man and a noble fellow </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The same.] KENNEDY'S HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Monday, Dec </s>
<s> 14th, 1868._ The dinner-party of Saturday last was an immense success </s>
<s> Russel swore on the occasion that he would go over to Belfast expressly to dine with me at the Finlays' </s>
<s> Ballantyne informed me that he was going to send you some Scotch remembrance (I don't know what) at Christmas </s>
<s> The Edinburgh houses are very fine </s>
<s> The Glasgow room is a big wandering place, with five prices in it, which makes it the more aggravating, as the people get into knots which they can't break, as if they were afraid of one another </s>
<s> Forgery of my name is becoming popular </s>
<s> You sent me, this morning, a letter from Russell Sturgis, answering a supposed letter of mine (presented by "Miss Jefferies"), and assuring me of his readiness to give not only the ten pounds I asked for, but any contribution I wanted, towards sending that lady and her family back to Boston </s>
<s> I wish you would take an opportunity of forewarning Lady Tennent that the first night's reading she will attend is an experiment quite out of the way, and that she may find it rather horrible </s>
<s> The keeper of the Edinburgh Hall, a fine old soldier, presented me, on Friday night, with the finest red camellia for my button-hole that ever was seen </s>
<s> Nobody can imagine how he came by it, as the florists had had a considerable demand for that colour from ladies in the stalls, and could get no such thing </s>
<s> The day is dark, wet, and windy </s>
<s> The weather is likely to be vile indeed at Glasgow, where it always rains, and where the sun is never seen through the smoke </s>
<s> We go over there to-morrow at ten </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] CARRICK'S ROYAL HOTEL, GLASGOW, _Tuesday, Dec </s>
<s> 15th, 1868._ It occurs to me that my table at St </s>
<s> James's Hall might be appropriately ornamented with a little holly next Tuesday </s>
<s> If the two front legs were entwined with it, for instance, and a border of it ran round the top of the fringe in front, with a little sprig by way of bouquet at each corner, it would present a seasonable appearance </s>
<s> If you will think of this, and will have the materials ready in a little basket, I will call for you at the office at half-past twelve on Tuesday, and take you up to the hall, where the table will be ready for you </s>
<s> No news, except that we had a great crush and a wonderful audience in Edinburgh last night </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] CARRICK'S ROYAL HOTEL, GLASGOW, _Wednesday, Dec </s>
<s> 16th, 1868._ This is to report all well, except that I have wretched nights </s>
<s> The weather is diabolical here, and times are very bad </s>
<s> I cut "Copperfield" with a bold dexterity that amazed myself and utterly confounded George at the wing; knocking off that and "Bob" by ten minutes to ten </s>
<s> I don't know anything about the Liverpool banquet, except from _The Times_ </s>
<s> As I don't finish there in February (as they seem to have supposed), but in April, it may, perhaps, stand over or blow over altogether </s>
<s> Such a thing would be a serious addition to the work, and yet refusal on my part would be too ungracious </s>
<s> The density and darkness of this atmosphere are fearful </s>
<s> I shall be heartily glad to start for Edinburgh again on Friday morning </s>
<s> [Sidenote: The same.] KENNEDY'S HOTEL, EDINBURGH, _Friday, Dec </s>
<s> 18th, 1868._ I am heartily glad to get back here this afternoon </s>
<s> The day is bright and cheerful, and the relief from Glasgow inexpressible </s>
<s> The affectionate regard of the people exceeds all bounds, and is shown in every way </s>
<s> The manager of the railway being at the reading the other night, wrote to me next morning, saying that a large saloon should be prepared for my journey up, if I would let him know when I purposed making the journey </s>
<s> On my accepting the offer he wrote again, saying that he had inspected "our Northern saloons," and not finding them so convenient for sleeping in as the best English, had sent up to King's Cross for the best of the latter; which I would please consider my own carriage as long as I wanted it </s>
<s> The audiences do everything but embrace me, and take as much pains with the readings as I do </s>
<s> I find your Christmas present (just arrived) to be a haggis and shortbread </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr J </s>
<s> C </s>
<s> Parkinson.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Christmas Day, 1868._ MY DEAR PARKINSON, When your letter was delivered at "All the Year Round" Office yesterday, I was attending a funeral </s>
<s> It comes to hand here consequently to-day </s>
<s> I am diffident of addressing Mr Gladstone on the subject of your desire to be appointed to the vacant Commissionership of Inland Revenue, because, although my respect for him and confidence in him are second to those of no man in England (a bold word at this time, but a truthful one), my personal acquaintance with him is very slight </s>
<s> But you may make, through any of your friends, any use you please of this letter, towards the end of bringing its contents under Mr Gladstone's notice </s>
<s> In expressing my conviction that you deserve the place, and are in every way qualified for it, I found my testimony upon as accurate a knowledge of your character and abilities as anyone can possibly have acquired </s>
<s> In my editorship both of "Household Words" and "All the Year Round," you know very well that I have invariably offered you those subjects of political and social interest to write upon, in which integrity, exactness, a remarkable power of generalising evidence and balancing facts, and a special clearness in stating the case, were indispensable on the part of the writer </s>
<s> My confidence in your powers has never been misplaced, and through all our literary intercourse you have never been hasty or wrong </s>
<s> Whatever trust you have undertaken has been so completely discharged, that it has become my habit to read your proofs rather for my own edification than (as in other cases) for the detection of some slip here or there, or the more pithy presentation of the subject </s>
<s> That your literary work has never interfered with the discharge of your official duties, I may assume to be at least as well known to your colleagues as it is to me </s>
<s> It is idle to say that if the post were in my gift you should have it, because you have had, for some years, most of the posts of high trust that have been at my disposal </s>
<s> An excellent public servant in your literary sphere of action, I should be heartily glad if you could have this new opportunity of distinguishing yourself in the same character </s>
<s> And this is at least unselfish in me, for I suppose I should then lose you </s>
<s> Always faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Edward Bulwer Lytton Dickens.] LETTER TO HIS YOUNGEST SON ON HIS DEPARTURE FOR AUSTRALIA IN 1868.[27] MY DEAREST PLORN, I write this note to-day because your going away is much upon my mind, and because I want you to have a few parting words from me to think of now and then at quiet times </s>
<s> I need not tell you that I love you dearly, and am very, very sorry in my heart to part with you </s>
<s> But this life is half made up of partings, and these pains must be borne </s>
<s> It is my comfort and my sincere conviction that you are going to try the life for which you are beat fitted </s>
<s> I think its freedom and wildness more suited to you than any experiment in a study or office would ever have been; and without that training, you could have followed no other suitable occupation </s>
<s> What you have already wanted until now has been a set, steady, constant purpose </s>
<s> I therefore exhort you to persevere in a thorough determination to do whatever you have to do as well as you can do it </s>
<s> I was not so old as you are now when I first had to win my food, and do this out of this determination, and I have never slackened in it since </s>
<s> Never take a mean advantage of anyone in any transaction, and never be hard upon people who are in your power </s>
<s> Try to do to others, as you would have them do to you, and do not be discouraged if they fail sometimes </s>
<s> It is much better for you that they should fail in obeying the greatest rule laid down by our Saviour, than that you should </s>
<s> I put a New Testament among your books, for the very same reasons, and with the very same hopes that made me write an easy account of it for you, when you were a little child; because it is the best book that ever was or will be known in the world, and because it teaches you the best lessons by which any human creature who tries to be truthful and faithful to duty can possibly be guided </s>
<s> As your brothers have gone away, one by one, I have written to each such words as I am now writing to you, and have entreated them all to guide themselves by this book, putting aside the interpretations and inventions of men </s>
<s> You will remember that you have never at home been wearied about religious observances or mere formalities </s>
<s> I have always been anxious not to weary my children with such things before they are old enough to form opinions respecting them </s>
<s> You will therefore understand the better that I now most solemnly impress upon you the truth and beauty of the Christian religion, as it came from Christ Himself, and the impossibility of your going far wrong if you humbly but heartily respect it </s>
<s> Only one thing more on this head </s>
<s> The more we are in earnest as to feeling it, the less we are disposed to hold forth about it </s>
<s> Never abandon the wholesome practice of saying your own private prayers, night and morning </s>
<s> I have never abandoned it myself, and I know the comfort of it </s>
<s> I hope you will always be able to say in after life, that you had a kind father </s>
<s> You cannot show your affection for him so well, or make him so happy, as by doing your duty </s>
<s> Your affectionate Father </s>

<s> NARRATIVE </s>
<s> The "Farewell Readings" in town and country were resumed immediately after the beginning of this year, and were to have been continued until the end of May </s>
<s> The work was even harder than it had ever been </s>
<s> Charles Dickens began his country tour in Ireland early in January, and read continuously in all parts of England and Scotland until the end of April </s>
<s> A public dinner (in commemoration of his last readings in the town) was given to him at Liverpool on the 10th April </s>
<s> Besides all this severe country work, he was giving a series of readings at St </s>
<s> James's Hall, and reading the "Murder" from "Oliver Twist," in London and in the country, frequently four times a week </s>
<s> In the second week of February, a sudden and unusually violent attack of the old trouble in his foot made it imperatively necessary to postpone a reading at St </s>
<s> James's Hall, and to delay for a day or two his departure for Scotland </s>
<s> The foot continued to cause him pain and inconvenience, but, as will be seen from his letters, he generally spoke of himself as otherwise well, until he arrived at Preston, where he was to read on the 22nd of April </s>
<s> The day before this appointed reading, he writes home of some grave symptoms which he had observed in himself, and had reported to his doctor, Mr F </s>
<s> Carr Beard </s>
<s> That gentleman, taking alarm at what he considered "indisputable evidences of overwork," wisely resolved not to content himself with written consultations, but went down to Preston on the day appointed for the reading there, and, after seeing his patient, peremptorily stopped it, carried him off to Liverpool, and the next day to London </s>
<s> There he consulted Sir Thomas Watson, who entirely corroborated Mr Beard's opinion </s>
<s> And the two doctors agreed that the course of readings must be stopped for this year, and that reading, _combined with travelling_, must be stopped _for ever_ </s>
<s> Charles Dickens had no alternative but to acquiesce in this verdict; but he felt it keenly, not only for himself, but for the sake of the Messrs </s>
<s> Chappell, who showed the most disinterested kindness and solicitude on the occasion </s>
<s> He at once returned home to Gad's Hill, and the rest and quiet of the country restored him, for the time, to almost his usual condition of health and spirits </s>
<s> But it was observed, by all who loved him, that from this time forth he never regained his old vigour and elasticity </s>
<s> The attack at Preston was the "beginning of the end" </s>
<s> During the spring and summer of this year, he received visits from many dearly valued American friends </s>
<s> In May, he stayed with his daughter and sister-in-law for two or three weeks at the St </s>
<s> James's Hotel, Piccadilly, having promised to be in London at the time of the arrival of Mr and Mrs Fields, of Boston, who visited Europe, accompanied by Miss Mabel Lowell (the daughter of the famous American poet) this year </s>
<s> Besides these friends, Mr and Mrs Childs, of Philadelphia--from whom he had received the greatest kindness and hospitality, and for whom he had a hearty regard--Dr </s>
<s> Fordyce Barker and his son, Mr Eytinge (an illustrator of an American edition of Charles Dickens's works), and Mr Bayard Taylor paid visits to Gad's Hill, which were thoroughly enjoyed by Charles Dickens and his family </s>
<s> This last summer was a very happy one </s>
<s> He had the annual summer visitors and parties of his friends in the neighbourhood </s>
<s> He was, as usual, projecting improvements in his beloved country home; one, which he called the "crowning improvement of all," was a large conservatory, which was to be added during the absence of the family in London in the following spring </s>
<s> The state of Mr Wills's health made it necessary for him now to retire altogether from the editorship of "All the Year Round" </s>
<s> Charles Dickens's own letters express the regret which he felt at the dissolution of this long and always pleasant association </s>
<s> Mr Wills's place at the office was filled by Charles Dickens's eldest son, now sole editor and proprietor of the journal </s>
<s> In September Charles Dickens went to Birmingham, accompanied by his son Harry, and presided at the opening of the session of (what he calls in his letter to Mr Arthur Ryland, "_our_ Institution") the Midland Institute </s>
<s> He made a speech on education to the young students, and promised to go back early in the following year and distribute the prizes </s>
<s> In one of the letters which we give to Mr Ryland, he speaks of himself as "being in full force again," and "going to finish his farewell readings soon after Christmas" </s>
<s> He had obtained the sanction of Sir Thomas Watson to giving twelve readings, _in London only_, which he had fixed for the beginning of the following year </s>
<s> The letter to his friend Mr Finlay, which opens the year, was in reply to a proposal for a public banquet at Belfast, projected by the Mayor of that town, and conveyed through Mr Finlay </s>
<s> This gentleman was at that time proprietor of _The Northern Whig_ newspaper at Belfast, and he was son-in-law to Mr Alexander Russel, editor of _The Scotsman_ </s>
<s> Charles Dickens's letter this New Year to M </s>
<s> de Cerjat was his last </s>
<s> That faithful and affectionate friend died very shortly afterwards </s>
<s> To Miss Mary Boyle he writes to acknowledge a New Year's gift, which he had been much touched by receiving from her, at a time when he knew she was deeply afflicted by the sudden death of her brother, Captain Cavendish Boyle, for whom Charles Dickens had a true regard and friendship </s>
<s> While he was giving his series of London readings in the spring, he received a numerously signed circular letter from actors and actresses of the various London theatres </s>
<s> They were very curious about his new reading of the "Oliver Twist" murder, and representing to him the impossibility of their attending an evening, requested him to give a morning reading, for their especial benefit </s>
<s> We give his answer, complying with the request </s>
<s> And the occasion was, to him, a most gratifying and deeply interesting one </s>
<s> The letter to Mr Edmund Ollier was in answer to an invitation to be present at the inauguration of a bust of Mr Leigh Hunt, which was to be placed over his grave at Kensal Green </s>
<s> The letter to Mr Shirley Brooks, the well-known writer, who succeeded Mr Mark Lemon as editor of "Punch," and for whom Charles Dickens had a cordial regard, was on the subject of a memorial on behalf of Mrs Peter Cunningham, whose husband had recently died </s>
<s> The "remarkable story," of which he writes to his daughter in August, was called "An Experience" </s>
<s> It was written by a lady (who prefers to be anonymous) who had been a contributor to "Household Words" from its first starting, and was always highly valued in this capacity by Charles Dickens </s>
<s> Our latest letters for this year are in October </s>
<s> One to Mr Charles Kent, sympathising with him on a disappointment which he had experienced in a business undertaking, and one to Mr Macready, in which he tells him of his being in the "preliminary agonies" of a new book </s>
<s> The first number of "Edwin Drood" was to appear before the end of his course of readings in March; and he was at work so long beforehand with a view to sparing himself, and having some numbers ready before the publication of the first one </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr F </s>
<s> D </s>
<s> Finlay.] THE ATHENÆUM (CLUB), _New Year's Day, 1869._ MY DEAR FINLAY, First my heartfelt wishes for many prosperous and happy years </s>
<s> Next, as to the mayor's kind intentions </s>
<s> I feel really grateful to him and gratified by the whole idea, but acceptance of the distinction on my part would be impracticable </s>
<s> My time in Ireland is all anticipated, and I could not possibly prolong my stay, because I _must_ be back in London to read on Tuesday fortnight, and then must immediately set forth for the West of England </s>
<s> It is not likely, besides, that I shall get through these farewells before the end of May </s>
<s> And the work is so hard, and my voice is so precious, that I fear to add an ounce to the fatigue, or I might be overweighted </s>
<s> The avoidance of gas and crowds when I am not in the act of being cooked before those lights of mine, is an essential part of the training to which (as I think you know) I strictly adhere, and although I have accepted the Liverpool invitation, I have done so as an exception; the Liverpool people having always treated me in our public relations with a kind of personal affection </s>
<s> I am sincerely anxious that the Mayor of Belfast should know how the case stands with me </s>
<s> If you will kindly set me straight and right, I shall be truly obliged to you </s>
<s> My sister-in-law has been very unwell (though she is now much better), and is recommended a brisk change </s>
<s> As she is a good sailor, I mean to bring her to Ireland with me; at which she is highly delighted </s>
<s> Faithfully yours ever </s>
<s> [Sidenote: M </s>
<s> de Cerjat.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, Jan </s>
<s> 4th, 1869._ MY DEAR CERJAT, I will answer your question first </s>
<s> Have I done with my farewell readings </s>
<s> Lord bless you, no; and I shall think myself well out of it if I get done by the end of May </s>
<s> I have undertaken one hundred and six, and have as yet only vanquished twenty-eight </s>
<s> To-morrow night I read in London for the first time the "Murder" from "Oliver Twist," which I have re-arranged for the purpose </s>
<s> Next day I start for Dublin and Belfast </s>
<s> I am just back from Scotland for a few Christmas holidays </s>
<s> I go back there next month; and in the meantime and afterwards go everywhere else </s>
<s> Take my guarantee for it, you may be quite comfortable on the subject of papal aspirations and encroachments </s>
<s> The English people are in unconquerable opposition to that church </s>
<s> They have the animosity in the blood, derived from the history of the past, though perhaps unconsciously </s>
<s> But they do sincerely want to win Ireland over if they can </s>
<s> They know that since the Union she has been hardly used </s>
<s> They know that Scotland has _her_ religion, and a very uncomfortable one </s>
<s> They know that Scotland, though intensely anti-papal, perceives it to be unjust that Ireland has not _her_ religion too, and has very emphatically declared her opinion in the late elections </s>
<s> They know that a richly-endowed church, forced upon a people who don't belong to it, is a grievance with these people </s>
<s> They know that many things, but especially an artfully and schemingly managed institution like the Romish Church, thrive upon a grievance, and that Rome has thriven exceedingly upon this, and made the most of it </s>
<s> Lastly, the best among them know that there is a gathering cloud in the West, considerably bigger than a man's hand, under which a powerful Irish-American body, rich and active, is always drawing Ireland in that direction; and that these are not times in which other powers would back our holding Ireland by force, unless we could make our claim good in proving fair and equal government </s>
<s> Poor Townshend charged me in his will "to publish without alteration his religious opinions, which he sincerely believed would tend to the happiness of mankind" </s>
<s> To publish them without alteration is absolutely impossible; for they are distributed in the strangest fragments through the strangest note-books, pocket-books, slips of paper and what not, and produce a most incoherent and tautological result </s>
<s> I infer that he must have held some always-postponed idea of fitting them together </s>
<s> For these reasons I would certainly publish nothing about them, if I had any discretion in the matter </s>
<s> Having none, I suppose a book must be made </s>
<s> His pictures and rings are gone to the South Kensington Museum, and are now exhibiting there </s>
<s> Charley Collins is no better and no worse </s>
<s> Katie looks very young and very pretty </s>
<s> Her sister and Miss Hogarth (my joint housekeepers) have been on duty this Christmas, and have had enough to do </s>
<s> My boys are now all dispersed in South America, India, and Australia, except Charley, whom I have taken on at "All the Year Round" Office, and Henry, who is an undergraduate at Trinity Hall, and I hope will make his mark there </s>
<s> All well </s>
<s> The Thames Embankment is (faults of ugliness in detail apart) the finest public work yet done </s>
<s> From Westminster Bridge to near Waterloo it is now lighted up at night, and has a fine effect </s>
<s> They have begun to plant it with trees, and the footway (not the road) is already open to the Temple </s>
<s> Besides its beauty, and its usefulness in relieving the crowded streets, it will greatly quicken and deepen what is learnedly called the "scour" of the river </s>
<s> But the Corporation of London and some other nuisances have brought the weirs above Twickenham into a very bare and unsound condition, and they already begin to give and vanish, as the stream runs faster and stronger </s>
<s> Your undersigned friend has had a few occasional reminders of his "true American catarrh" </s>
<s> Although I have exerted my voice very much, it has not yet been once touched </s>
<s> In America I was obliged to patch it up constantly </s>
<s> I like to read your patriarchal account of yourself among your Swiss vines and fig-trees </s>
<s> You wouldn't recognise Gad's Hill now; I have so changed it, and bought land about it </s>
<s> And yet I often think that if Mary were to marry (which she won't) I should sell it and go genteelly vagabondising over the face of the earth </s>
<s> Then indeed I might see Lausanne again </s>
<s> But I don't seem in the way of it at present, for the older I get, the more I do and the harder I work </s>
<s> Yours ever affectionately </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Mary Boyle.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 6th, 1869._ MY DEAR MARY, I was more affected than you can easily believe, by the sight of your gift lying on my dressing-table on the morning of the new year </s>
<s> To be remembered in a friend's heart when it is sore is a touching thing; and that and the remembrance of the dead quite overpowered me, the one being inseparable from the other </s>
<s> You may be sure that I shall attach a special interest and value to the beautiful present, and shall wear it as a kind of charm </s>
<s> God bless you, and may we carry the friendship through many coming years </s>
<s> My preparations for a certain murder that I had to do last night have rendered me unfit for letter-writing these last few days, or you would have heard from me sooner </s>
<s> The crime being completely off my mind and the blood spilled, I am (like many of my fellow-criminals) in a highly edifying state to-day </s>
<s> Ever believe me, your affectionate Friend </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] TORQUAY, _Wednesday, Jan </s>
<s> 27th, 1869._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, We have been doing immensely </s>
<s> This place is most beautiful, though colder now than one would expect </s>
<s> This hotel, an immense place, built among picturesque broken rocks out in the blue sea, is quite delicious </s>
<s> There are bright green trees in the garden, and new peas a foot high </s>
<s> Our rooms are _en suite_, all commanding the sea, and each with two very large plate-glass windows </s>
<s> Everything good and well served </s>
<s> A _pantomime_ was being done last night, in the place where I am to read to-night </s>
<s> It is something between a theatre, a circus, a riding-school, a Methodist chapel, and a cow-house </s>
<s> I was so disgusted with its acoustic properties on going in to look at it, that the whole unfortunate staff have been all day, and now are, sticking up baize and carpets in it to prevent echoes </s>
<s> I have rarely seen a more uncomfortable edifice than I thought it last night </s>
<s> At Clifton, on Monday night, we had a contagion of fainting </s>
<s> And yet the place was not hot </s>
<s> I should think we had from a dozen to twenty ladies borne out, stiff and rigid, at various times </s>
<s> It became quite ridiculous </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Miss Hogarth.] BATH, _Friday, Jan </s>
<s> 29th, 1869._ MY DEAREST GEORGY, You must not trust blank places in my list, because many have been, and will be, gradually filled up </s>
<s> After the Tuesday's reading in London, I have TWO for that same week in the country--Nottingham and Leicester </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Miss Dickens.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," NO </s>

<s> 3rd, 1869._ MY DEAREST MAMIE, I send you the second chapter of the remarkable story </s>

<s> So, finding that it wanted something, I put that something in </s>

<s> [Sidenote: Mr Arthur Ryland.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Friday, Aug </s>
<s> 13th, 1869._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> RYLAND, Many thanks for your letter </s>
<s> I have very strong opinions on the subject of speechification, and hold that there is, everywhere, a vast amount too much of it </s>
<s> A sense of absurdity would be so strong upon me, if I got up at Birmingham to make a flourish on the advantages of education in the abstract for all sorts and conditions of men, that I should inevitably check myself and present a surprising incarnation of the soul of wit </s>
<s> But if I could interest myself in the practical usefulness of the particular institution; in the ways of life of the students; in their examples of perseverance and determination to get on; in their numbers, their favourite studies, the number of hours they must daily give to the work that must be done for a livelihood, before they can devote themselves to the acquisition of new knowledge, and so forth, then I could interest others </s>
<s> This is the kind of information I want </s>
<s> Mere holding forth "I utterly detest, abominate, and abjure" </s>
<s> I fear I shall not be in London next week </s>
<s> But if you will kindly send me here, at your leisure, the roughest notes of such points as I have indicated, I shall be heartily obliged to you, and will take care of their falling into shape and order in my mind </s>
<s> Meantime I "make a note of" Monday, 27th September, and of writing to you touching your kind offer of hospitality, three weeks before that date </s>
<s> I beg to send my kind regard to Mrs and Miss Ryland, and am always, Very faithfully yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Frederic Ouvry.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Sunday, Aug </s>
<s> 22nd, 1869._ MY DEAR OUVRY, I will expect a call from you at the office, on Thursday, at your own most convenient hour </s>
<s> I admit the soft impeachment concerning Mrs Gamp: I likes my payments to be made reg'lar, and I likewise likes my publisher to draw it mild </s>
<s> Ever yours </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr Arthur Ryland.] GAD'S HILL PLACE, HIGHAM BY ROCHESTER, KENT, _Monday, Sept </s>
<s> 6th, 1869._ MY DEAR MR </s>
<s> RYLAND, I am sorry to find--I had a foreshadowing of it some weeks ago--that I shall not be able to profit by your kind offer of hospitality when I come to Birmingham for _our_ Institution </s>
<s> I must come down in time for a quiet dinner at the hotel with my "Readings" secretary, Mr Dolby, and must away next morning </s>
<s> Besides having a great deal in hand just now (the title of a new book among other things), I shall have visitors from abroad here at the time, and am severely claimed by my daughter, who indeed is disloyal to Birmingham in the matter of my going away at all </s>
<s> Pray represent me to Mrs Ryland as the innocent victim of circumstances, and as sacrificing pleasure to the work I have to do, and to the training under which alone I can do it without feeling it </s>
<s> You will see from the enclosed that I am in full force, and going to finish my readings, please God, after Christmas </s>
<s> I am in the hope of receiving your promised notes in due course, and continue in the irreverent condition in which I last reported myself on the subject of speech-making </s>
<s> Now that men not only make the nights of the session hideous by what the Americans call "orating" in Parliament, but trouble the peace of the vacation by saying over again what they said there (with the addition of what they _didn't_ say there, and never will have the courage to say there), I feel indeed that silence, like gold across the Atlantic, is a rarity at a premium </s>
<s> Faithfully yours always </s>
<s> [Sidenote: Mr William Charles Kent.] OFFICE OF "ALL THE YEAR ROUND," _Thursday, Oct </s>
<s> 7th, 1869._ MY DEAR KENT, I felt that you would be deeply disappointed </s>
<s> I thought it better not to make the first sign while you were depressed, but my mind has been constantly with you </s>
<s> And not mine alone </s>
<s> You cannot think with what affection and sympathy you have been made the subject of our family dinner talk at Gad's Hill these last three days </s>
<s> Nothing could exceed the interest of my daughters and my sister-in-law, or the earnestness of their feeling about it </s>
<s> I have been really touched by its warm and genuine expression </s>
<s> Cheer up, my dear fellow; cheer up, for God's sake </s>
<s> That is, for the sake of all that is good in you and around you </s>
<s> Ever your affectionate Friend </s>

<s> C </s>
<s> Macready.] GAD'S HILL, _Monday, Oct </s>
<s> 18th, 1869._ MY DEAREST MACREADY, I duly received your letter nearly a fortnight ago, with the greatest interest and pleasure </s>
<s> Above all things I am delighted with the prospect of seeing you here next summer; a prospect which has been received with nine times nine and one more by the whole house </s>
<s> You will hardly know the place again, it is so changed </s>
<s> You are not expected to admire, but there _is_ a conservatory building at this moment--be still, my soul </s>
<s> This leaves me in the preliminary agonies of a new book, which I hope to begin publishing (in twelve numbers, not twenty) next March </s>
<s> The coming readings being all in London, and being, after the first fortnight, only once a week, will divert my attention very little, I hope </s>
<s> Harry has just gone up to Cambridge again, and I hope will get a fellowship in good time </s>
<s> Wills is much gratified by your remembrance, and sends you his warm regard </s>
<s> He wishes me to represent that he is very little to be pitied </s>
<s> That he suffers no pain, scarcely inconvenience, even, so long as he is idle </s>
<s> That he likes idleness exceedingly </s>
<s> He has bought a country place by Welwyn in Hertfordshire, near Lytton's, and takes possession presently </s>
<s> My boy Sydney is now a second lieutenant, the youngest in the Service, I believe </s>
<s> He has the highest testimonials as an officer </s>
<s> You may be quite sure there will be no international racing in American waters </s>
<s> Oxford knows better, or I am mistaken </s>
<s> The Harvard crew were a very good set of fellows, and very modest </s>
<s> Ryland of Birmingham doesn't look a day older, and was full of interest in you, and asked me to remind you of him </s>
<s> By-the-bye, at Elkington's I saw a pair of immense tea-urns from a railway station (Stafford), sent there to be repaired </s>
<s> They were honeycombed within in all directions, and had been supplying the passengers, under the active agency of hot water, with decomposed lead, copper, and a few other deadly poisons, for heaven knows how many years </s>
<s> I must leave off in a hurry to catch the post, after a hard day's work </s>
<s> Ever, my dearest Macready, Your most affectionate and attached </s>
